### [1] [Geometric Entropy and Retrieval Phase Transitions in Continuous Thermal Dense Associative Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07401)
*Tatiana Petrova,Evgeny Polyachenko,Radu State*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究分析了具有几何约束的现代Hopfield网络（密集联想记忆模型）的热力学记忆容量，推导了指数容量网络的相边界，比较了高斯核和Epanechnikov核的不同相结构特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在扩展经典成对联想记忆分析，探索具有连续状态的现代Hopfield网络在几何约束下的热力学记忆容量，特别是高容量密集联想记忆模型的理论极限。

Method: 采用热力学相边界分析方法，研究具有指数容量 $p = e^{αN}$ 的密集联想记忆网络，比较高斯核（LSE）和Epanechnikov核（LSR）两种核函数。针对$N$维球面上的连续神经元，分析几何熵仅依赖于球面几何而非核函数的特性。

Result: 在尖锐核（sharp-kernel）机制下，零温度时达到最大理论容量$α=0.5$；低于此阈值时，临界线将检索相与自旋玻璃相分离。两种核的相边界结构存在本质差异：LSE核的检索区域在$α\to 0$时可延伸至任意高温，但始终存在虚假模式的干扰；LSR核的有限支持引入阈值$α_{\text{th}}$，低于该阈值时虚假模式不贡献噪声基底，产生性质不同的检索机制。

Conclusion: 研究推进了高容量联想记忆理论，阐明了现代类注意力记忆架构中检索鲁棒性的基本极限，揭示了不同核函数对相结构和检索性能的定性影响。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamic memory capacity of modern Hopfield networks (Dense Associative Memory models) with continuous states under geometric constraints, extending classical analyses of pairwise associative memory. We derive thermodynamic phase boundaries for Dense Associative Memory networks with exponential capacity $p = e^{αN}$, comparing Gaussian (LSE) and Epanechnikov (LSR) kernels. For continuous neurons on an $N$-sphere, the geometric entropy depends solely on the spherical geometry, not the kernel. In the sharp-kernel regime, the maximum theoretical capacity $α= 0.5$ is achieved at zero temperature; below this threshold, a critical line separates retrieval from a spin-glass phase. The two kernels differ qualitatively in their phase boundary structure: for LSE, the retrieval region extends to arbitrarily high temperatures as $α\to 0$, but interference from spurious patterns is always present. For LSR, the finite support introduces a threshold $α_{\text{th}}$ below which no spurious patterns contribute to the noise floor, producing a qualitatively different retrieval regime in this sub-threshold region. These results advance the theory of high-capacity associative memory and clarify fundamental limits of retrieval robustness in modern attention-like memory architectures.

</details>


### [2] [Bilattice-Catastrophe Isomorphism for Four-Valued Logic in Digital Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07690)
*Jiu Hui Wu,Hua Tian,Mengqi Yuan,Kejiang Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文建立了Belnap四值逻辑（4VL）与突变理论（CT）之间的范畴对应关系，揭示了四值代数FOUR作为描述连续-离散接口的最小完备代数结构，并证明工程实践中X和Z的数学必要性源于拓扑不变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在建立离散四值逻辑（4VL）与连续突变理论（catastrophe theory）之间的代数桥梁，解释四值逻辑的鲁棒性，并为工程实践中经验性采用的X和Z提供数学基础。

Method: 基于双格-突变同构定理（bilattice-catastrophe isomorphism theorem）的严格验证，建立了突变范畴（catastrophe category）、交织双格范畴（interlaced bilattice category）和四值逻辑范畴（4VL category）之间的范畴对应关系。

Result: 证明了四值代数FOUR是描述具有对合对称性（involution symmetry）的连续-离散接口的最小完备代数结构；揭示了X和Z是离散化连续动力系统的拓扑不变量（topological invariants），编码了突变诱导不连续性的基本性质。

Conclusion: 该统一框架为解释四值逻辑的鲁棒性提供了基础，并支持跨学科扩展到不确定性传播（uncertainty propagation）、复杂系统建模和容错设计（fault-tolerant design）等领域。

Abstract: Belnap's four-valued logic, distinguished by its inherent bilattice structure, provides a natural algebraic bridge between discrete Four-valued logic (4VL) in circuit and continuous catastrophe theory (CT). Building on the rigorous verification of the bilattice-catastrophe isomorphism theorem, we establish a categorical correspondence spanning the catastrophe category, interlaced bilattice category, and 4VL category, with the cusp catastrophe emerging as the canonical CT counterpart to 4VL.This unification provides a foundational framework for explaining 4VL's robustness. Crucially, we demonstrate that the four-valued algebra FOUR is the minimal complete algebraic structure capable of describing continuous-discrete interfaces with involution symmetry. Unlike the empirical adoption of X and Z in engineering practice, our work reveals their mathematical necessity: X and Z are topological invariants of discretized continuous dynamical systems, encoding fundamental properties of catastrophe-induced discontinuities. The work enables cross-disciplinary extensions to uncertainty propagation, complex system modeling, and fault-tolerant design.

</details>


### [3] [Localization--non-ergodic transition in controllable-dimension fractal networks from diffusion-limited aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07700)
*Oleg I. Utesov,Alexei Andreanov,Tomasz Bednarek,Alexandra Siklitskaya,Sergei V. Koniakhin*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析具有可调维度的分形聚集体（fractal agglomerates）的光谱性质，建立了无序整数维系统与规则自相似物体物理特性之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在连接无序整数维系统与规则自相似物体的物理学，通过研究具有可调维度的分形聚集体的光谱特性来探索这一联系。

Method: 采用生成算法参数α控制分形聚集体的维度，研究嵌入2D和3D空间中的最近邻紧束缚模型（nearest-neighbor tight-binding model）在分形聚集体上的光谱性质。

Result: 在2D情况下所有本征态都是局域化的，而在3D情况下，随着α增加（从稀疏到稠密分形），出现了局域化-非遍历转变：在特定临界α值下，谱中出现亚扩展数量的临界态。分形聚集体的复杂几何结构还导致了紧凑局域态的奇特层次结构和态密度中的奇异性。

Conclusion: 分形聚集体的几何结构对光谱性质有显著影响，包括局域化转变和临界态的出现，这些现象在有序分形中具有典型性，建立了无序整数维系统与自相似物体之间的物理联系。

Abstract: Our study connects the physics of disordered integer-dimensional systems and regular self-similar objects by studying spectral properties of fractal agglomerates with tunable dimension. The latter is controlled by parameter $α$ of the algorithm that generates the agglomerates. We consider the nearest-neighbor tight-binding model on the agglomerates embedded in 2D and 3D, and observe that all eigenstates are localized in the 2D case, whereas in the 3D case, there is a localization--non-ergodic transition upon increasing $α$,i.e., going from sparse to dense fractals: a sub-extensive number of critical states emerge in the spectrum at a certain critical value of $α$. The complex geometry of the agglomerates is also responsible for a peculiar hierarchy of compact localized states and singularities in the density of states, which are typical for ordered fractals.

</details>


### [4] [FlowEqProp: Training Flow Matching Generative Models with Gradient Equilibrium Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08150)
*Alex Gower*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出梯度平衡传播（GradEP）方法，扩展平衡传播（EP）以训练能量梯度而非能量最小值，首次将EP应用于基于流的生成模型训练，在数字识别数据集上成功生成可识别样本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统平衡传播（Equilibrium Propagation, EP）方法仅能训练能量最小值，无法处理学习目标依赖于收敛动力系统速度场的任务。需要扩展EP框架以支持更广泛的应用场景，特别是基于流的生成建模。

Method: 提出梯度平衡传播（Gradient Equilibrium Propagation, GradEP）机制，引入弹簧势能（spring potential）使所有单元（包括可见单元）在动力学过程中演化，通过平衡位移编码学习的速度场。弹簧项和相应的微扰项均为纯二次型，保持了EP的硬件可实现性。

Result: 将GradEP应用于流匹配（flow matching）生成建模（称为FlowEqProp），在光学手写数字识别数据集上训练两层隐藏层MLP（24,896参数），仅使用局部平衡测量而无反向传播。模型在所有十个类别上生成可识别数字样本，训练动态稳定。时间无关能量景观支持超越训练时长的扩展生成，通过额外推理时间计算产生更清晰样本。

Conclusion: GradEP成功扩展了EP框架的应用范围，首次实现了基于平衡传播的流生成模型训练。该方法保持了硬件可实现性，在神经形态硬件上具有自然映射优势，更长的弛豫时间可产生更高质量输出。

Abstract: We introduce Gradient Equilibrium Propagation (GradEP), a mechanism that extends Equilibrium Propagation (EP) to train energy gradients rather than energy minima, enabling EP to be applied to tasks where the learning objective depends on the velocity field of a convergent dynamical system. Instead of fixing the input during dynamics as in standard EP, GradEP introduces a spring potential that allows all units, including the visible units, to evolve, encoding the learned velocity in the equilibrium displacement. The spring and resulting nudge terms are both purely quadratic, preserving EP's hardware plausibility for neuromorphic implementation. As a first demonstration, we apply GradEP to flow matching for generative modelling - an approach we call FlowEqProp - training a two-hidden-layer MLP (24,896 parameters) on the Optical Recognition of Handwritten Digits dataset using only local equilibrium measurements and no backpropagation. The model generates recognisable digit samples across all ten classes with stable training dynamics. We further show that the time-independent energy landscape enables extended generation beyond the training horizon, producing sharper samples through additional inference-time computation - a property that maps naturally onto neuromorphic hardware, where longer relaxation yields higher-quality outputs. To our knowledge, this is the first demonstration of EP training a flow-based generative model.

</details>

### [5] [Phenomenology of an Open Effective Field Theory of Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12321)
*Santiago Agüí Salcedo,Thomas Colas,Lennard Dufner,Enrico Pajer*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个开放引力动力学（open gravitational dynamics）理论框架，提出了一个描述宇宙晚期加速膨胀的最小化具体实现模型。该模型能够拟合重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation）观测数据，同时避免零能量条件（null energy condition）的违反，并产生多个可观测检验的相关预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质（dark matter）和暗能量（dark energy）的所有观测证据目前仅限于引力效应。因此，暗区（dark sector）可能等价地由受未知环境相互作用影响的时空度规理论描述。研究旨在构建一个开放引力动力学的一般理论，并研究其在宇宙晚期加速膨胀中的具体应用。

Method: 采用开放系统技术（open-system techniques）构建了开放引力动力学的一般理论框架。研究聚焦于该理论的一个最小化具体实现模型，该模型专门描述宇宙晚期加速膨胀。通过修改宇宙微扰理论（cosmological perturbation theory），并与ΛCDM模型进行比较分析。

Result: 模型能够良好拟合近期重子声学振荡测量数据，同时避免零能量条件的违反。研究发现：引力波光度距离相对于电磁光度距离存在耗散抑制；Bardeen势的演化发生改变，在引力滑移（gravitational slip）中产生清晰信号；低红移处的结构形成得到增强。这些效应的大小通过半解析估计表明在当前观测约束范围内，并为未来宇宙学巡天提供了明确目标。

Conclusion: 该开放引力动力学模型为暗区现象提供了新的理论框架，产生了一系列可观测检验的相关预测。这些效应不仅与当前观测约束兼容，而且为即将开展的宇宙学巡天提供了清晰的检验目标，有望推动对暗物质和暗能量本质的理解。

Abstract: All observational evidence for dark matter and dark energy is so far exclusively gravitational. Hence, the dark sector may be equivalently described by a theory of the spacetime metric whose dynamics is affected by interactions with an unknown environment. Adapting open-system techniques, we have recently constructed such a general theory of open gravitational dynamics. Here we study a minimal and concrete realization of this theory that describes the late-time acceleration of the Universe. Our model provides a good fit to recent baryon acoustic oscillation measurements by construction, while avoiding violations of the null energy condition. Moreover, it leads to a set of correlated and observationally testable predictions. Studying the modified cosmological perturbation theory and compared to the $Λ$CDM model we find: a dissipative suppression of the gravitational-wave luminosity distance relative to the electromagnetic one; a modification in the evolution of the Bardeen potentials with a clear signal in the gravitational slip; and an enhancement of structure formation at low redshift. We present semi-analytical estimates of the magnitude of these effects and show that they lie within the reach of current constraints while providing clear targets for upcoming cosmological surveys.

</details>


### [6] [A Dynamical Equilibrium Linking Nanohertz Stochastic Gravitational Wave Background to Cosmic Structure Formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08317)
*Manjia Liang,Peng Xu,Ruijun Shi,Zhoujian Cao,Ziren Luo,Minghui Du,Qiong Deng,Bo Liang,Jiaxiang Liang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种将随机引力波背景（SGWB）与物质作为动力学耦合非平衡系统处理的新框架，揭示了SGWB对宇宙物质的反作用效应，并通过NANOGrav数据验证了该框架的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background, SGWB）被视为天体物理和宇宙学源的被动遗迹，其对宇宙物质的反作用（back-reaction）被忽略。本研究旨在修正这一假设，将SGWB与物质视为动力学耦合的非平衡系统。

Method: 结合线性化广义相对论（linearized general relativity）与涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem），推导出驱动耦合系统趋向动态平衡的广义朗之万框架（generalized Langevin framework）。该框架预测了具有高频截止$\mathcal{W}$的独特应变谱和尺度依赖的耦合参数。

Result: 将平衡谱拟合到NANOGrav 15年数据集，获得了相对于超大质量黑洞双星基线的贝叶斯因子$48\pm 3.8$。PTA校准的屏蔽质量尺度$m_{c}\sim 10^{12}\text{--}10^{14}\,M_{\odot}$与ΛCDM导出的宇宙结构线性-非线性转变质量$M_{\rm NL}$在$\sim 8\,h^{-1}\,\mathrm{Mpc}$处重叠。$\mathcal{W}$可完全用$M_{\rm NL}$表示，其倒数具有SGWB-物质耦合相干阈值的物理解释。

Conclusion: 该框架表明SGWB与物质构成动力学耦合系统，$\mathcal{W}$成为连接纳赫兹引力波观测与晚期宇宙学领域的导出量。框架做出了可被未来大尺度结构巡天和空间引力波天文台验证的独特尺度依赖预测。

Abstract: The stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB) is conventionally treated as a passive relic of its astrophysical and cosmological sources, with negligible back-reaction on the matter content of the Universe. Here we show that this assumption needs to be modified once the SGWB and matter are treated as a dynamically coupled non-equilibrium system. Combining linearized general relativity with the fluctuation-dissipation theorem, we derive a generalized Langevin framework that drives the coupled system toward a dynamical equilibrium, which is characterized by a distinctive strain spectrum with a high-frequency cutoff $\mathcal{W}$, and a scale-dependent coupling parameter that screens gravity progressively for the most massive structures. Three findings support this framework. Fitting the equilibrium spectrum to the NANOGrav 15-year dataset yields a Bayes factor of $48\pm 3.8$ over the supermassive black hole binary baseline, achieved entirely within general relativity and the Standard Model. The PTA-calibrated screening mass scale $m_{c}\sim 10^{12}\text{--}10^{14}\,M_{\odot}$ overlaps, with no free cosmological parameter, the $Λ$CDM-derived linear-to-nonlinear transition mass $M_{\rm NL}$ of cosmic structure at $\sim 8\,h^{-1}\,\mathrm{Mpc}$. Most strikingly, promoting this concordance to a structural identification expresses $\mathcal{W}$ entirely in terms of $M_{\rm NL}$, and its inverse acquires a transparent physical reading as a coherence threshold for SGWB-matter coupling. $\mathcal{W}$ is thereby a derived quantity linking nanohertz gravitational-wave observables to the late-time cosmological sector. The framework makes distinctive scale-dependent predictions testable by forthcoming large-scale structure surveys and space-borne gravitational-wave observatories.

</details>


### [7] [Probing non-Gaussianity during reheating with SIGW in the LISA band](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08493)
*Gabriele Perna,Guillem Domènech*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究分析了宇宙再加热（reheating）时期的非标准演化对原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）影响下的标量诱导引力波（SIGWs）谱的影响，发现特定状态方程参数会在谱中留下可被LISA等第三代干涉仪探测的特征信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索宇宙再加热时期的非标准演化如何影响标量诱导引力波谱，特别是考虑原初非高斯性的存在，这对于理解早期宇宙演化和引力波探测具有重要意义。

Method: 研究方法包括分析非标准再加热动力学对SIGWs谱的影响，考虑状态方程参数w和声速平方c_s²的特征效应，并使用Fisher预报（Fisher forecast）评估不同参数组合下信号的可探测性。

Result: 研究结果表明，特定的w和c_s²值会在SIGWs谱中留下特征信号，这些特征可被LISA等第三代干涉仪探测；再加热动力学可以抑制或增强谱信号，对其可探测性产生关键影响。

Conclusion: 结论指出宇宙再加热时期的非标准演化在标量诱导引力波谱中产生可探测的特征，这些特征能够为早期宇宙动力学提供重要约束，并通过Fisher预报验证了不同参数下信号的可探测性潜力。

Abstract: We analyse the effects of a non-standard evolution of the Universe during the reheating epoch on the spectrum of scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) accounting for the presence of primordial non-Gaussianity. We show that given values of $w$ and $c_s^2$ leave characteristic features in the spectrum which can be detectable by third generation interferometers like LISA. In addition, we argue that the specific reheating dynamics can suppress or even enhance the spectrum, with crucial consequences for its detectability. We perform a Fisher forecast for different values of $w$ and different scans to assess the detectability of the signal when different values of the amplitude and central frequency are considered.

</details>


### [8] [The Heavy Tailed Non-Gaussianity of the Supermassive Black Hole Gravitational Wave Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08506)
*Juhan Raidal,Juan Urrutia,Ville Vaskonen,Hardi Veermäe*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究分析了超大质量黑洞双星（SMBH binaries）产生的引力波背景（GW background）的非高斯特征，发现其振幅分布具有普遍的重幂律尾端（heavy power-law tail）∝A⁻⁴，导致高阶统计矩发散，并证实了方差平均高斯近似（variance-averaged Gaussian approximation）的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索由超大质量黑洞双星（SMBH binaries）群体产生的引力波背景（GW background）的非高斯特征。当前研究需要理解这些引力波信号的统计特性，特别是其偏离高斯分布的程度，这对脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）数据分析至关重要。

Method: 研究方法包括分析超大质量黑洞双星引力波振幅分布（GW amplitude distribution, GWAD）的统计特性，特别是其幂律尾端行为。研究还考察了引力波诱导的计时残差（timing residuals）分布，并评估了方差平均高斯近似（variance-averaged Gaussian approximation）对描述这些统计特性的适用性。

Result: 研究结果显示，超大质量黑洞双星引力波振幅分布具有普遍的重幂律尾端∝A⁻⁴，而低振幅尾端则依赖于黑洞合并率和双星能量损失机制。计时残差分布继承了这一重尾特性，导致三阶及更高阶的系综平均统计矩发散。研究证实了方差平均高斯近似能准确描述计时残差统计。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，超大质量黑洞双星引力波背景表现出"单响亮源原理"（single loud source principle），即最强信号更可能由少量响亮源产生。方差平均高斯近似支持一种分解似然结构，可将标准高斯过程PTA后验与非高斯群体先验结合，从而在SMBH模型推断中一致地纳入非高斯效应。

Abstract: We study the non-Gaussian features of the gravitational wave (GW) background generated by a population of inspiraling supermassive black hole (SMBH) binaries. We show that the SMBH GW amplitude distribution (GWAD) features a universal heavy power-law tail $\propto A^{-4}$, while the low-amplitude tail depends on the SMBH merger rate and the energy-loss mechanisms of the binaries. The distribution of the induced timing residuals inherits this heavy tail. As a result, the ensemble averaged statistical moments of order three and higher diverge, limiting their usefulness as measures of non-Gaussianity, and the GW background from SMBH binaries exhibits the single loud source principle, according to which the strongest signals are more likely to be caused by a small number of loud sources. We confirm that the variance-averaged Gaussian approximation accurately describes the timing residual statistics. This approximation justifies a factored likelihood structure that combines standard Gaussian-process PTA posteriors with the non-Gaussian population prior, enabling consistent incorporation of non-Gaussian effects into SMBH model inference. We provide a fast and flexible Python implementation to compute the distribution of timing residuals from a given SMBH merger rate or GWAD.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [9] [Multiplicity dependence of prompt and non-prompt J/$ψ$ production at midrapidity in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07968)
*ALICE Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究测量了13 TeV质子-质子碰撞中J/ψ粒子的产额及其与非弹性碰撞中带电粒子多重数的依赖关系，发现J/ψ产额随多重数呈超线性增长，且在J/ψ发射方向区域增长更强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索高能质子-质子碰撞中粲夸克偶素（charmonium）J/ψ粒子的产生机制，特别是其产额与带电粒子多重数的依赖关系，以理解强子碰撞中的多重部分子相互作用（multi-parton interactions）和集体效应。

Method: 在$\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV的质子-质子碰撞中，通过双电子衰变道测量了中间快度区（$|y| < 0.9$）的瞬时（prompt）和非瞬时（non-prompt）J/ψ产额。将J/ψ产额和多重数相对于非弹性碰撞中的平均值进行归一化，并进一步将方位角区域划分为朝向J/ψ发射方向、横向和相反方向三个区域。

Result: 观测到瞬时和非瞬时J/ψ产额均随带电粒子多重数呈超线性增长，且趋势相似。在朝向J/ψ发射方向的区域也观察到类似行为，而在横向和相反方向区域的增长较弱。同时报告了瞬时J/ψ与D$^0$介子的多重数依赖产额比。

Conclusion: J/ψ产额与带电粒子多重数的超线性依赖关系表明，在高多重数质子-质子碰撞中可能存在集体效应或多重部分子相互作用增强粲夸克偶素产生。方位角依赖的差异进一步揭示了J/ψ产生与整体事件结构之间的关联。

Abstract: The yields of prompt and non-prompt J/$ψ$ and the fraction of non-prompt J/$ψ$ are measured at midrapidity ($|y| < 0.9$) via the dielectron decay channel as a function of the midrapidity charged-particle multiplicity ($|η| < 0.9$) in pp collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV. The J/$ψ$ yields and the multiplicity are normalized by their average value in inelastic collisions. The multiplicity-dependent yield ratio between prompt J/$ψ$ and D$^0$ is reported. The multiplicity is further divided into three azimuthal regions with respect to the J/$ψ$ momentum: toward the J/$ψ$ emission direction, transverse, or opposite to it. A stronger-than-linear increase of the self-normalized yields is observed for both prompt and non-prompt J/$ψ$ production, with similar trends. This behaviour is also observed in the toward region, while a weaker increase is observed in the transverse and away regions.

</details>


### [10] [Recent Neutrino Oscillation and Cross-Section Results from the T2K Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08259)
*Nick Latham*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: T2K实验通过近探测器系统降低系统不确定性，结合钆加载远探测器数据，提供了最新的中微子振荡结果和稀有相互作用通道的世界首次测量，展示了相互作用建模与振荡分析在寻找轻子CP破坏中的协同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: T2K实验旨在精确测量中微子混合和质量分裂参数，并主导寻找轻子电荷宇称破坏（leptonic charge-parity violation）的研究。通过近探测器复合体（near detector complex）降低系统不确定性是实现这一目标的关键。

Method: 采用T2K长基线中微子振荡实验装置，结合近探测器复合体进行高中子统计的中微子-核相互作用截面测量。首次使用钆加载远探测器（gadolinium-loaded far detector）数据，并对多种靶材进行测量。

Result: 获得了最新的T2K振荡结果，包括多个稀有相互作用通道（rare interaction channels）的世界首次测量。这些结果展示了相互作用建模与振荡分析在T2K-II时代寻找电荷宇称破坏中的协同作用。

Conclusion: T2K实验通过近探测器系统降低系统不确定性，结合钆加载远探测器数据，为精确测量中微子参数和寻找轻子CP破坏提供了重要进展，展示了相互作用建模与振荡分析的协同作用在T2K-II时代的重要性。

Abstract: The T2K long-baseline neutrino oscillation experiment in Japan continues to lead the search for leptonic charge-parity violation while providing precision measurements of mixing and mass splitting parameters. Central to this programme is the mitigation of systematic uncertainties through the near detector complex, which provides high-statistics neutrino-nucleus interaction cross-section measurements across various targets. This contribution presents the latest T2K oscillation results, incorporating the first data with a gadolinium-loaded far detector, and highlights several recent cross-section measurements, including several world-first measurements of rare interaction channels. Together, these results demonstrate the vital synergy between interaction modelling and oscillation analysis in the search for charge-parity violation in the T2K-II era.

</details>

Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,J. Zhao,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 首次在质子-质子碰撞中搜索轻子味破坏衰变 $B^+ \to π^+ μ^{\pm} e^{\mp}$，未观测到显著信号，设定分支比上限 $\mathcal{B} < 1.8 \times 10^{-9}$（90%置信度），比当前世界平均值严格两个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在首次在质子-质子碰撞中搜索轻子味破坏（lepton-flavour violating）衰变 $B^+ \to π^+ μ^{\pm} e^{\mp}$，这是对标准模型（Standard Model）以外新物理的重要探针。

Method: 利用LHCb实验在2011年至2018年间收集的质子-质子碰撞数据，对应积分亮度为9 fb$^{-1}$，进行轻子味破坏衰变的首次搜索。

Result: 未观测到显著信号，设定分支比上限 $\mathcal{B}(B^+ \to π^+ μ^{\pm} e^{\mp}) < 1.8 \times 10^{-9}$（90%置信度），比当前世界平均值严格两个数量级。

Conclusion: 这是LHC上对轻子味破坏 $b \to d$ 夸克跃迁的首个约束，也是迄今为止对 $b \to d μ^{\pm} e^{\mp}$ 跃迁最严格的上限，同时报告了超出标准模型的左手性和标量情景的限制。

Abstract: The first search for the lepton-flavour violating decays $B^+ \to π^+ μ^{\pm} e^{\mp}$ in proton-proton collisions is presented, using data collected by the LHCb experiment between 2011 and 2018, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 9 fb$^{-1}$. No significant signal is observed and an upper limit on the branching fraction is set at $\mathcal{B}(B^+ \to π^+ μ^{\pm} e^{\mp}) < 1.8 \times 10^{-9}$ at the $90\%$ confidence level, two orders of magnitude more restrictive than the current world average. This is the first constraint on lepton-flavour violating $b \to d$ quark transitions at the LHC and also sets the most stringent upper limits to date on $b \to d μ^{\pm} e^{\mp}$ transitions. Limits on left-handed and scalar scenarios beyond the Standard Model are also reported.

</details>

### [12] [Probabilistic Weyl Law for Twisted Toeplitz Matrices with Rough Symbols](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07370)
*Lucas Noël*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了带有小随机扰动的扭曲托普利茨矩阵（twisted Toeplitz matrices）的经验谱测度（empirical spectral measure）的收敛性，证明其在概率意义下弱收敛于符号函数（symbol）对勒贝格测度（Lebesgue measure）的前推（push-forward）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究扭曲托普利茨矩阵在随机扰动下的谱特性，特别是其经验谱测度的渐近行为。这类矩阵在频率维度上具有光滑符号，但在位置变量上仅具有分段赫尔德连续性（piecewise Hölder continuous）和跳跃型间断点。

Method: 分析带有小随机扰动的扭曲托普利茨矩阵，其符号函数在频率维度光滑，在位置变量上具有分段赫尔德连续性和跳跃型间断点。研究其经验谱测度的收敛行为。

Result: 证明经验谱测度在概率意义下弱收敛于符号函数对勒贝格测度的前推。这一收敛结果适用于具有特定正则性条件的扭曲托普利茨矩阵。

Conclusion: 扭曲托普利茨矩阵的经验谱测度在小随机扰动下收敛于符号函数的前推测度，即使符号在位置变量上仅具有分段赫尔德连续性和跳跃型间断点。

Abstract: In this article, we study the convergence of the empirical spectral measure of twisted Toeplitz matrices subject to small random perturbations. We show that the empirical spectral measure converges weakly in probability to the push-forward of the Lebesgue measure by the symbol. The symbol of the twisted Toeplitz matrices is assumed to be smooth in frequency, and only piecewise H{ö}lder continuous with respect to the position variable with discontinuities of jump type.

</details>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [13] [Comment on "On the emergence of preferred structures in quantum theory" by Soulas, Franzmann, and Di Biagio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.07674)
*Ovidiu Cristinel Stoica*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文分析表明，仅从哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）和态矢量（state vector）无法涌现出首选结构（preferred structures），并以Soulas等人提出的张量积结构（tensor product structure）构造为例，说明这种构造既不能保持对称性不变性，又与物理观测不相容，从而证实而非反驳了Stoica的先前结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在阐明仅从哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）$\mathsf{H}$和单位态矢量（unit state vector）$|ψ\rangle$出发，无法涌现出首选结构（preferred structures）的根本不可能性。这一分析通过具体考察Soulas等人提出的张量积结构（tensor product structure, TPS）构造来展示涌现障碍。

Method: 通过分析Soulas等人（2025）提出的具体张量积结构（tensor product structure, TPS）构造方法，该方法试图仅从$\mathsf{H}$和$|ψ\rangle$构建唯一TPS。研究重点考察了该构造的对称性不变性（invariance）以及与物理观测的相容性（compatibility），特别是通过分析编码纠缠（entanglement）的$|ψ(t)\rangle$与TPS关系随时间的变化来揭示其内在矛盾。

Result: 分析表明，Soulas等人构造的唯一张量积结构（tensor product structure）无法同时满足对称性不变性（invariance）和与物理观测的相容性（compatibility），因此不能作为Stoica（2022a）结论的有效反例。该构造的不相容性通过考察$|ψ(t)\rangle$与编码纠缠的TPS关系随时间变化而显现，实际上证实而非反驳了Stoica的先前结论。

Conclusion: Soulas等人的构造虽然具体，但恰当地展示了涌现结构的主要障碍，尽管尽力避免这些障碍却仍证实了它们的存在。这使得该构造成为阐释三重困境（trilemma）以及量子理论（quantum theory）中关系性和结构性方面的优秀教学工具，同时也揭示了通过手动固定不变量（invariants）来构造首选结构的方法在逻辑上等同于人为指定基本粒子质量，缺乏物理涌现的实质基础。

Abstract: This reply is also a friendly introduction to the impossibility of emergence of preferred structures from the Hamiltonian $\mathsf{H}$ and the unit vector $|ψ\rangle$ only. The obstructions to emergence are illustrated on the concrete construction of a tensor product structure (TPS) from Soulas et al., 2025 (arXiv:2512.07468v2). Soulas et al. offer their TPS as a counterexample to the proof from Stoica, 2022a (arXiv:2102.08620) that structures constructed only from $\mathsf{H}$ and $|ψ\rangle$ either contradict physical observations or can't describe them unambiguously.
  Soulas et al.'s construction of a unique TPS can't be both invariant and compatible with physical observations, so it can't be a counterexample. Its incompatibility becomes visible by examining how the relation between $|ψ(t)\rangle$ and the TPS, encoding the entanglement, changes in time. Therefore their TPS doesn't refute, but confirms (Stoica, 2022a).
  Besides this, since Soulas et al.'s method to construct preferred structures consists of choosing their invariants, by the same logic one could claim as well that the masses of elementary particles emerge uniquely just by fixing their values by hand.
  Soulas et al.'s construction is concrete and can illustrate the major obstructions for emergent structures, confirming them despite doing the best possible to avoid them. This makes it an excellent pedagogical tool to illustrate the trilemma, but also the relational and structural aspects of quantum theory and its symmetries.

</details>


### [14] [Trotterization with Many-body Coulomb Interactions: Convergence for General Initial Conditions and State-Dependent Improvements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07704)
*Di Fang,Xiaoxu Wu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为库仑相互作用多体量子系统的Trotter公式建立了严格的误差界，证明了二阶Trotter在哈密顿量定义域内的一般初始条件下具有1/4的收敛率，并识别了能提升收敛阶数的物理条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高效模拟库仑相互作用多体量子系统是量子物理、量子化学和量子计算中的基本问题，但面临独特挑战：哈密顿量是无界算子，希尔伯特空间维度随粒子数指数增长，库仑势具有奇异性、长程性、非光滑性和无界性，违反了许多现有最先进多体模拟分析的规律性假设。

Method: 本文为应用于库仑相互作用多体量子系统的Trotter公式建立了严格的误差界。研究分析了二阶Trotter公式在哈密顿量定义域内一般初始条件下的收敛行为，并识别了能改善收敛阶数的物理条件。

Result: 主要结果包括：对于哈密顿量定义域内的一般初始条件，二阶Trotter公式实现了1/4的收敛率，误差预因子对粒子数具有显式多项式依赖；识别了一组物理上有意义的初始状态条件，在这些条件下收敛率可提升至一阶和二阶。对于类氢系统，这些条件与具有足够高角动量的激发态相关。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，即使不引入任何库仑奇异性正则化，算法仍保持量子效率。理论发现与先前的数值观测一致，且1/4收敛率在氢基态中已被观察到，证明了其对物理和实践重要初始条件的相关性。

Abstract: Efficiently simulating many-body quantum systems with Coulomb interactions is a fundamental question in quantum physics, quantum chemistry, and quantum computing, yet it presents unique challenges: the Hamiltonian is an unbounded operator (both kinetic and potential parts are unbounded); its Hilbert space dimension grows exponentially with particle number; and the Coulomb potential is singular, long-ranged, non-smooth, and unbounded, violating the regularity assumptions of many prior state-of-the-art many-body simulation analyses. In this work, we establish rigorous error bounds for Trotter formulas applied to many-body quantum systems with Coulomb interactions. Our first main result shows that for general initial conditions in the domain of the Hamiltonian, second-order Trotter achieves a sharp $1/4$ convergence rate with explicit polynomial dependence of the error prefactor on the particle number. The polynomial dependence on system size suggests that the algorithm remains quantumly efficient, even without introducing any regularization of the Coulomb singularity. Notably, although the result under general conditions constitutes a worst-case bound, this rate has been observed in prior work for the hydrogen ground state, demonstrating its relevance to physically and practically important initial conditions. Our second main result identifies a set of physically meaningful conditions on the initial state under which the convergence rate improves to first and second order. For hydrogenic systems, these conditions are connected to excited states with sufficiently high angular momentum. Our theoretical findings are consistent with prior numerical observations.

</details>


### [15] [Inverse Laplace and Mellin integral transforms modified for use in quantum communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07787)
*Gustavo Alvarez,Igor Kondrashuk*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文简要回顾了基本积分变换，并针对扩展域提出了修改方案，探讨了其在量子计算机安全协议中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 积分变换是处理电子设备中信号和波包的有用数学工具，也可用于软件协议。论文旨在探讨如何修改逆积分变换以应用于量子色动力学中的轮廓积分解，并将其应用于量子计算机的安全协议。

Method: 论文简要回顾了基本积分变换，并提出了针对扩展域的修改方案。特别关注量子色动力学中的光学定理和重整化群方程，这些方程可通过梅林变量复平面中两种不同"对偶"方式的唯一轮廓积分求解。

Result: 论文提出修改逆积分变换以应用于轮廓积分解，这些修改后的逆变换可用于量子计算机的安全协议。通过复平面中的复映射将两种对偶表示联系起来。

Conclusion: 修改后的积分变换在量子计算机安全协议中具有应用潜力，为扩展域中的积分变换提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Integral transformations are useful mathematical tool to work out signals and wave-packets in electronic devices. They may be used in software protocols. Necessary knowledge may come from quantum field theory, in particular from quantum chromodynamics, in which the optic theorem and the renormalization group equation can be solved by a unique contour integral written in two different "dual" ways related between themselves by a complex map in the complex plane of Mellin variable. The inverse integral transformation should be modified to be applied for these contour integral solutions. These modified inverse transformations may be used in security protocols for quantum computers. Here we do a brief review of the basic integral transforms and propose their modification for the extended domains.

</details>


### [16] [Sufficiency and Petz recovery for positive maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08380)
*Lauritz van Luijk,Henrik Wilming*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了量子态族（统计实验）通过正迹保持（PTP）映射的相互转换，阐明了其数学结构，并建立了与Koashi-Imoto分解的推广联系。主要贡献包括：证明Neyman-Pearson检验生成最小充分Jordan代数，推导数据处理不等式等式的恢复映射存在性，以及建立PTP映射与可分解迹保持映射在二分态转换中的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子态族（统计实验）通过正迹保持（positive, trace-preserving, PTP）映射相互转换的数学结构，旨在将Koashi-Imoto分解推广到PTP设定中，并澄清相关代数结构。

Method: 采用最小充分Jordan代数（minimal sufficient Jordan algebras）作为核心数学工具，证明Neyman-Pearson检验生成该代数结构。同时系统回顾Jordan代数的数学背景，并针对近似有限维von Neumann代数证明了Frenkel公式。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）Neyman-Pearson检验生成最小充分Jordan代数，进而对应Koashi-Imoto分解的最小充分*-代数；2）相对熵或α-z量子Rényi散度的数据处理不等式等式在PTP情形下也意味着恢复映射的存在；3）两个二分态可通过PTP映射相互转换当且仅当可通过可分解迹保持映射转换。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将Koashi-Imoto分解推广到PTP设定，建立了量子态族转换的代数框架。通过最小充分Jordan代数统一了统计推断与量子信息处理，为PTP映射下的量子统计实验分析提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the interconversion of families of quantum states ("statistical experiments") via positive, trace-preserving (PTP) maps and clarify its mathematical structure in terms of minimal sufficient Jordan algebras, which can be seen to generalize the Koashi-Imoto decomposition to the PTP setting. In particular, we show that Neyman-Pearson tests generate the minimal sufficient Jordan algebra, and hence also the minimal sufficient *-algebra corresponding to the Koashi-Imoto decomposition. As applications, we show that a) equality in the data-processing inequality for the relative entropy or the $α$-$z$ quantum Rényi divergence implies the existence of a recovery map also in the PTP case and b) that two dichotomies can be interconverted by PTP maps if and only if they can be interconverted by decomposable, trace-preserving maps. We thoroughly review the necessary mathematical background on Jordan algebras. As a step beyond the finite-dimensional case, we also prove Frenkel's formula for approximately finite-dimensional von Neumann algebras.

</details>


### [17] [Rapid mixing for high-temperature Gibbs states with arbitrary external fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08408)
*Ainesh Bakshi,Xinyu Tan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 高温吉布斯态（Gibbs states）在外场作用下展现出复杂的纠缠特性和计算复杂性：外场可诱导纠缠，存在经典采样困难性，但同时存在高效的量子吉布斯采样器，使其成为量子优势的候选模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 吉布斯态是热平衡下量子物质的自然模型。研究旨在探究外场如何影响高温吉布斯态的纠缠结构和计算复杂性，特别是外场在诱导纠缠和产生计算困难性方面的作用。

Method: 引入满足细致平衡（detailed balance）的准局域Lindbladian，该动力学在任意局域外场存在下都能在$\mathcal{O}(\log(n/ε))$时间内快速混合至吉布斯态。同时分析外场强度$h$与逆温度$β$的交叉尺度关系$h\asymp β^{-1} \log(1/β)$。

Result: 外场可在原本可证明可分离的态中诱导纠缠。对于任何$β<1$，存在局域哈密顿量，使得在足够大的外场下，从相应吉布斯态的计算基分布中采样是经典困难的。但存在高效的量子吉布斯采样器。

Conclusion: 具有外场的高温吉布斯态是自然的物理模型，能够同时展现纠缠和经典困难性，同时允许高效的量子吉布斯采样器，这使其成为通过态制备实现量子优势的合适候选者。

Abstract: Gibbs states are a natural model of quantum matter at thermal equilibrium. We investigate the role of external fields in shaping the entanglement structure and computational complexity of high-temperature Gibbs states. External fields can induce entanglement in states that are otherwise provably separable, and the crossover scale is $h\asymp β^{-1} \log(1/β)$, where $h$ is an upper bound on any on-site potential and $β$ is the inverse temperature. We introduce a quasi-local Lindbladian that satisfies detailed balance and rapidly mixes to the Gibbs state in $\mathcal{O}(\log(n/ε))$ time, even in the presence of an arbitrary on-site external field. Additionally, we prove that for any $β<1$, there exist local Hamiltonians for which sampling from the computational-basis distribution of the corresponding Gibbs state with a sufficiently large external field is classically hard, under standard complexity-theoretic assumptions. Therefore, high-temperature Gibbs states with external fields are natural physical models that can exhibit entanglement and classical hardness while also admitting efficient quantum Gibbs samplers, making them suitable candidates for quantum advantage via state preparation.

</details>


### [18] [Thermal Time and Irreversibility from Non-Commuting Observables in Accelerated Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08349)
*Marcello Rotondo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了相对论量子场论中时间顺序何时具有可操作意义，表明当系统满足KMS条件且探测器通过非对易可观测量耦合时，不同操作序列变得物理可区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究时间顺序在相对论量子场论中何时具有可操作意义，因为仅时间参数本身并不能确保不同操作序列在物理上是可区分的。

Method: 采用局域化探测器模型，研究均匀加速的两能级探测器与闵可夫斯基真空中的量子场相互作用。通过非对易可观测量进行顺序耦合，并利用量子相对熵量化不对称性。

Result: 结果表明，当状态满足Kubo-Martin-Schwinger (KMS)条件且探测器通过非对易可观测量耦合时，不同操作序列变得可区分。在最小模型中，相关状态形成具有相同谱但不同生成元的一族非对易吉布斯态。

Conclusion: 时间顺序的可操作意义取决于系统是否满足KMS条件以及探测器是否通过非对易可观测量耦合。这种不对称性可通过量子相对熵量化，并在最小模型中得出仅依赖于温度与探测器能量标度无量纲组合的闭式表达式。

Abstract: We investigate when temporal ordering becomes operationally meaningful in relativistic quantum field theory using localized detector models. A time parameter alone does not ensure that different sequences of operations are physically distinguishable. We show that distinguishability arises when the state satisfies the Kubo--Martin--Schwinger (KMS) condition and the detector couples through non-commuting observables.
  We consider uniformly accelerated two-level detectors interacting with a quantum field in the Minkowski vacuum. The restriction of the vacuum to the detector trajectory induces a thermal response characterized by the Unruh temperature and the Tolman profile. For sequential couplings through distinct observables, the reduced detector state depends on the ordering of interactions already at second order, with a dependence controlled by the KMS parameter.
  This asymmetry is quantified using quantum relative entropy. In a minimal model, the relevant states form a family of non-commuting Gibbs states with identical spectra and different generators, yielding a closed-form expression depending only on the dimensionless combination of temperature and detector energy scale.

### [19] [Observation of genuine $2+1$D string dynamics in a U$(1)$ lattice gauge theory with a tunable plaquette term on a trapped-ion quantum computer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07436)
*Rohan Joshi,Yizhuo Tian,Kevin Hemery,N. S. Srivatsa,Jesse J. Osborne,Henrik Dreyer,Enrico Rinaldi,Jad C. Halimeh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在量子计算机上实现了2+1维U(1)量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics）的量子模拟，通过引入可调plaquette项，首次观测到真正的2+1维弦断裂（string-breaking）动力学现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理的量子模拟在2+1维中能够探索一维空间不存在的动力学现象，并触及经典模拟方法难以处理的物理区域。对于弦动力学（string dynamics）——与强子化（hadronization）相关——需要plaquette项来实现真正的2+1维行为，因为它赋予规范场动力学并允许光子样激发（photon-like excitations）的传播。

Method: 在Quantinuum System Model H2量子计算机上实现了具有可调plaquette项的U(1)量子链模型（quantum link model）。使用5×4物质点（matter-site）方晶格和51个量子比特，采用浅层电路设计，每个Trotter步（Trotter step）包含28层双量子比特门深度，最多1540个纠缠门。

Result: 从远离平衡的弦构型（string configurations）出发，测量了弦在晶格平面内传播的概率，发现仅当plaquette项存在时才出现真正的2+1维动力学特征。在共振区域（resonant regime），观察到弦段湮灭伴随产生屏蔽它们的电子-正电子对（electron-positron pairs）。仅当plaquette项非零时，物质产生扩展到整个晶格平面而非局限于初始弦路径。

Conclusion: 这些结果实验性地实现了弦断裂，并证明了二维空间中动力学规范场（dynamical gauge fields）的出现，为规范理论（gauge theories）的可编程量子模拟器中光子样传播（photon-like propagation）建立了途径。

Abstract: Quantum simulations of high-energy physics in $2+1$D can probe dynamical phenomena nonexistent in one spatial dimension and access regimes that are challenging for existing classical simulation methods. For string dynamics -- relevant to hadronization -- a plaquette term is required to realize genuine $2+1$D behavior, as it endows the gauge field with dynamics and enables the propagation of photon-like excitations. Here, we realize a U$(1)$ quantum link model of quantum electrodynamics in two spatial dimensions with a tunable plaquette term on a \texttt{Quantinuum System Model H2} quantum computer. We implement, to our knowledge, the largest quantum simulation of string-breaking dynamics reported to date, on a $5 \times 4$ matter-site square lattice using $51$ qubits. The simulation uses a shallow circuit design with a two-qubit gate depth of $28$ per Trotter step and up to $1540$ entangling gates. Starting from far-from-equilibrium string configurations, we measure the probability for the string to propagate within the lattice plane and find signatures of genuine $2+1$D dynamics only when the plaquette term is present. In a resonant regime, we observe the annihilation of string segments accompanied by the production of electron--positron pairs that screen them. We further find that, only with a nonzero plaquette term, matter creation extends across the lattice plane rather than remaining confined to the initial string path. These results experimentally realize string breaking and demonstrate the emergence of dynamical gauge fields in two spatial dimensions, establishing a route to photon-like propagation in programmable quantum simulators of gauge theories.

### [20] [Locked Subharmonic Oscillations in the Entanglement Spectrum of a Periodically Driven Topological Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07442)
*Rishabh Jha*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究展示了周期性驱动的自由费米子系统在纠缠谱中表现出尖锐的次谐波响应，揭示了零-π Floquet拓扑作为必要条件，以及相干非平衡制备作为充分条件的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期性驱动的量子系统通常表现出次谐波响应，但这种现象主要在相互作用系统中通过物理可观测量进行表征。本研究旨在探索在粒子数守恒的自由费米子系统中，纠缠谱是否也能展现出尖锐的次谐波特征。

Method: 研究采用两步驱动的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger链，其Floquet算符在准能量0和π处支持对称保护的边缘模式。通过分析初始态为这两个边缘扇区相干叠加时的子系统关联矩阵和纠缠谱演化，并与拓扑平凡相及Floquet本征态情况进行对比。

Result: 当初始态为边缘扇区相干叠加时，子系统关联矩阵在两个频闪结构间交替，单粒子纠缠能级展现出稳健的周期加倍响应，其傅里叶权重集中在驱动频率的一半处。相比之下，对角边缘密度因子晶格对称性保持平坦，而离对角边缘-键可观测量则提供相应的线性单体比较器。

Conclusion: 零-π Floquet拓扑是产生次谐波响应的必要条件，而相干非平衡制备则是额外的充分条件。研究结果表明纠缠谱学可作为Floquet拓扑相干性的尖锐子系统分辨探针。

Abstract: Periodically driven quantum systems can exhibit subharmonic response, usually characterized through physical observables and often discussed in interacting settings. Here we show that a sharp subharmonic signature already appears in the entanglement spectrum of a number-conserving free-fermion system. We study a two-step driven Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chain whose Floquet operator supports symmetry-protected edge modes at quasienergies $0$ and $π$. When the initial state is a coherent superposition of these two edge sectors, the subsystem correlation matrix alternates between two stroboscopic structures, and an overlap-tracked single-particle entanglement level distills a robust period-doubling response with Fourier weight concentrated at half the drive frequency. By contrast, diagonal edge densities remain flat by sublattice symmetry, while an off-diagonal edge-bond observable provides the corresponding linear one-body comparator. The effect disappears both when the initial state is replaced by a stroboscopically stationary Floquet eigenstate built from the same topological mode content, and when the system is placed in the topologically trivial phase where no edge modes exist. Altogether, these establish zero-$π$ Floquet topology as a necessary condition and coherent nonequilibrium preparation as the additional sufficient ingredient. Our results identify entanglement spectroscopy as a sharp subsystem-resolved probe of Floquet topological coherence.

### [21] [Charging Quantum Batteries via Dissipative Quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08151)
*Riccardo Grazi,Donato Farina,Niccolò Traverso Ziani,Dario Ferraro*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了开放量子电池（open quantum batteries）中的功提取问题，重点关注相互作用自旋链在弱耦合工程环境下的动力学行为。研究表明，耗散（dissipation）和退相干（dephasing）过程能够影响并塑造系统的遍历功（ergotropy），其中耗散可激活热态的功提取能力，而退相干则会抑制这一过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索开放量子系统中环境工程如何影响量子电池的功提取能力。具体关注耗散和退相干过程（无论是局域还是集体作用）在瞬态和稳态动力学中对遍历功的生成和塑造作用。

Method: 研究方法基于开放量子电池模型，采用相互作用的自旋链（XX模型）弱耦合到工程环境中。通过引入并行噪声通道和集体噪声通道之间的连续插值，系统性地表征环境结构对功可提取性的影响。分析聚焦于初始处于热吉布斯态（thermal Gibbs states）的二比特和四比特系统。

Result: 研究结果显示，纯耗散动力学能够从完全被动的热态激活有限的遍历功，产生温度依赖的瞬态机制，其中较热的初始态在类似姆潘巴（Mpemba-like）的遍历功效应中暂时优于较冷态。集体耗散导致稳态的被动性关键取决于初始温度和系统尺寸，这与非平凡暗子空间（dark subspaces）的出现相关。退相干通道则会抑制瞬态优势和稳态功提取。

Conclusion: 结论表明耗散环境和退相干环境对量子电池功提取能力存在本质差异。耗散过程能够激活热态的功提取潜力并产生温度依赖的瞬态效应，而退相干则会抑制这些优势，突显了环境工程在优化量子电池性能中的重要性。

Abstract: We investigate work extraction in open quantum batteries composed of interacting spin chains weakly coupled to engineered environments. Focusing on two- and four-qubit XX models initially prepared in thermal Gibbs states, we analyze how dissipation and dephasing, acting either locally or collectively, can generate and shape ergotropy during both transient and steady-state dynamics. By introducing a continuous interpolation between parallel and collective noise channels, we systematically characterize the impact of environmental structure on work extractability. We show that purely dissipative dynamics can activate finite ergotropy from completely passive thermal states, giving rise to temperature-dependent transient regimes where hotter initial states temporarily outperform colder ones in an ergotropic Mpemba-like fashion. In contrast, collective dissipation leads to steady states whose passivity crucially depends on the initial temperature and system size, a behavior we trace back to the emergence of non-trivial dark subspaces. Finally, we demonstrate that dephasing channels suppress both transient advantages and steady-state work extraction, highlighting the qualitative difference between dissipative and dephasing environments.

### [22] [Bayesian Optimization for Mixed-Variable Problems in the Natural Sciences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07416)
*Yuhao Zhang,Ti John,Matthias Stosiek,Patrick Rinke*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于混合变量（连续与离散）优化的广义概率重参数化方法，通过改进贝叶斯优化框架，实现了在非等距离散变量和高维离散空间中的高效梯度优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自然科学中，优化昂贵黑盒目标函数（expensive black-box objectives）在混合搜索空间（mixed search spaces）中是一个常见挑战。贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization, BO）虽然提供样本高效的策略，但在混合或高基数离散空间（high-cardinality discrete spaces）中效果下降，因为梯度不可用且获取函数优化计算量大。

Method: 本文推广了Daulton等人的概率重参数化（probabilistic reparameterization, PR）方法，使其能够处理非等距离散变量（non-equidistant discrete variables），从而在完全混合变量设置中实现基于梯度的优化，并采用高斯过程（Gaussian process, GP）代理模型。同时结合改进的贝叶斯优化工作流程，优化了核函数（kernel）的构建。

Result: 通过在合成和实验目标函数上进行系统基准测试，获得了优化的核函数构建方案，并证明了广义概率重参数化方法的鲁棒性。该方法能够高效优化高度不连续和离散化的目标函数景观（objective landscapes）。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一个实用的贝叶斯优化框架，用于解决自然科学中完全混合优化问题（fully mixed optimization problems），特别适用于噪声、离散化和数据有限的自洽实验室环境（autonomous laboratory settings）。

Abstract: Optimizing expensive black-box objectives over mixed search spaces is a common challenge across the natural sciences. Bayesian optimization (BO) offers sample-efficient strategies through probabilistic surrogate models and acquisition functions. However, its effectiveness diminishes in mixed or high-cardinality discrete spaces, where gradients are unavailable and optimizing the acquisition function becomes computationally demanding. In this work, we generalize the probabilistic reparameterization (PR) approach of Daulton et al. to handle non-equidistant discrete variables, enabling gradient-based optimization in fully mixed-variable settings with Gaussian process (GP) surrogates. With real-world scientific optimization tasks in mind, we conduct systematic benchmarks on synthetic and experimental objectives to obtain an optimized kernel formulations and demonstrate the robustness of our generalized PR method. We additionally show that, when combined with a modified BO workflow, our approach can efficiently optimize highly discontinuous and discretized objective landscapes. This work establishes a practical BO framework for addressing fully mixed optimization problems in the natural sciences, and is particularly well suited to autonomous laboratory settings where noise, discretization, and limited data are inherent.

Abstract: Superconductivity realized in bilayer nickelate thin films enables direct spectroscopic and transport studies at ambient pressure. Method: 该方法基于问题的积分薄壳电流密度公式（integral thin-shell current-density formulation），采用切比雪夫多项式展开（Chebyshev polynomial expansions）进行空间离散化，并使用线法（method of lines）进行时间积分，适用于开放和闭合轴对称壳层。

Abstract: Existing numerical methods for modeling magnetization in thin type-II superconducting films have mostly been developed for flat films. The method is based on the integral thin-shell current-density formulation of the problem, employs Chebyshev polynomial expansions for spatial discretization, and uses the method of lines for time integration. It applies to both open and closed axisymmetric shells and is so accurate that the solutions obtained can serve as benchmarks for numerical methods for general, not necessarily axisymmetric, thin-shell magnetization problems. As one of the examples, we consider magnetic shielding by a superconducting sphere.

### [25] [Exploring the conventional and anomalous Josephson effects at arbitrary disorder strength in systems with spin-dependent fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08231)
*Maryam Darvishi,F. Sebastián Bergeret,Stefan Ilić*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了在存在自旋轨道耦合、塞曼场和交变磁性等自旋相关场的情况下，超导体-正常金属-超导体（SNS）约瑟夫森结中约瑟夫森电流的理论。该理论适用于任意无序强度，超越了传统的扩散和弹道近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论通常局限于纯粹的弹道或扩散近似，而实验中的高迁移率样品总是包含一定程度的无序。因此需要发展一个能够处理任意无序强度的理论框架来描述这类实验系统。

Method: 使用线性化的准经典Eilenberger方程，推导出约瑟夫森电流的紧凑表达式。该方法能够处理任意无序强度，包括自旋轨道耦合、塞曼场和交变磁性等自旋相关场。

Result: 首先研究了在拉什巴和德雷塞尔豪斯自旋轨道耦合下，约瑟夫森临界电流在外加磁场中的演化，并讨论了如何利用这种依赖性探测结中的自旋轨道耦合。其次，证明了拉什巴自旋轨道耦合系统中的反常约瑟夫森（φ₀）效应在宽范围无序强度下保持稳健，在足够长的结中甚至能被适度无序增强。最后，研究了含交变磁体的无序结中的约瑟夫森电流，发现此类系统中的0-π转变会被无序抑制。

Conclusion: 该理论为描述包含一定无序的高迁移率样品实验系统提供了有用工具，弥补了纯粹弹道或扩散近似的不足。研究结果揭示了无序对自旋相关约瑟夫森效应的影响机制。

Abstract: We present a theory of the Josephson current in superconductor-normal metal-superconductor (SNS) junctions in the presence of generic spin-dependent fields, such as spin-orbit coupling (SOC), Zeeman fields, and altermagnetism. We consider systems with arbitrary disorder strength, going beyond the usual diffusive and ballistic approximations. Using the linearized quasiclassical Eilenberger equation, we derive a compact expression for the Josephson current, which is then applied to various situations of experimental interest. First, we investigate the evolution of the Josephson critical current in an applied magnetic field in the presence of Rashba and Dresselhaus SOC, and discuss how this dependence can be used to probe SOC in the junction. We then study the anomalous Josephson ($\varphi_0$) effect in systems with Rashba SOC and show that it remains robust over a wide range of disorder strength, and can even be enhanced by moderate disorder in sufficiently long junctions. Finally, we investigate the Josephson current in disordered junctions with altermagnets, and show how the $0$-$π$ transition in such systems is suppressed by disorder. Our results may be useful for describing experimental setups with high-mobility samples, which nevertheless always contain some amount of disorder, and where neither purely ballistic nor diffusive approximations are adequate.

### [26] [Topological multicomponent-pairing superconductivity in twisted bilayer cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08235)
*Yu-Hang Li,Congjun Wu,Wang Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了扭曲双层铜氧化物中多分量超导态的出现，特别是具有拓扑非平凡特性的三分量配对态 $s+d_1 e^{iφ_1}+d_2 e^{iφ_2}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索扭曲双层铜氧化物中多分量超导态（multicomponent superconducting state）的出现，特别是当相位差 $φ_1-φ_2\neq 0,π$ 时，这种三分量配对态（three-component pairing state）具有拓扑非平凡特性。

Method: 研究方法结合了金兹堡-朗道分析（Ginzburg--Landau analysis）与基于微观模型的自洽平均场计算（self-consistent mean-field calculations），以研究这种拓扑三分量配对态的稳定性。

Result: 研究结果表明，这种拓扑三分量配对态可以在相当大的参数范围内稳定存在，且扭曲双层铜氧化物即使在存在显著s波配对分量（s-wave pairing component）的情况下，仍能保持手性和拓扑特性。

Conclusion: 结论指出，扭曲双层铜氧化物能够支持具有拓扑非平凡特性的多分量超导态，即使在s波配对分量显著存在的情况下，系统仍能保持手性和拓扑性质。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of a multicomponent superconducting state in twisted bilayer cuprates, characterized by the order parameter $s+d_1 e^{iφ_1}+d_2 e^{iφ_2}$, where $s=s_1+s_2$ denotes the symmetric combination of the layer-resolved $s$-wave components, and $s_i$ and $d_i$ ($i=1,2$) represent the $s$-wave and $d$-wave pairings associated with the individual layers. In particular, when $φ_1-φ_2\neq 0,π$, this three-component pairing state is topologically nontrivial. By combining Ginzburg--Landau analysis with self-consistent mean-field calculations based on a microscopic model, we show that such a topological three-component pairing state can be stabilized over a substantial parameter regime. Our results indicate that twisted bilayer cuprates can remain chiral and topological even in the presence of a sizable $s$-wave pairing component.

</details>


### [27] [Three-Dimensional Electronic Structures in Superconducting Ruddlesden-Popper Bilayer Nickelate Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08430)
*Yueying Li,Lizhi Xu,Wei Lv,Zihao Nie,Zechao Wang,Yu Miao,Jianchang Shen,Guangdi Zhou,Wenhua Song,Heng Wang,Haoliang Huang,Junfeng He,Jin-Feng Jia,Peng Li,Qi-Kun Xue,Zhuoyu Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过变光子能量角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）系统研究了三维Ruddlesden-Popper双层镍酸盐超导薄膜的电子结构，揭示了轨道依赖的维度特性与超导能隙特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越铜酸盐的准二维范式，理解Ruddlesden-Popper双层镍酸盐中第三维度的作用对于解码其超导机制至关重要。本研究旨在系统探究三维电子能带结构，特别是不同轨道的维度特性。

Method: 采用变光子能量角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）技术，系统研究了超导(La,Pr,Sm)₃Ni₂O₇/SrLaAlO₄薄膜的三维电子能带结构。样品通过低温超高真空转移系统（cryogenic ultra-high vacuum suitcase）进行转移，超导起始温度T_c^onset约为48K。

Result: 研究揭示了轨道依赖的维度特性：d_{x²-y²}主导能带表现出准二维特征，而d_{z²}主导能带显示出有限的k_z色散。在所有观测能带中均识别出有限能隙，其中d_{z²}衍生能带的超导能隙Δ约为18meV，比值2Δ/k_BT_c约为8，超过弱耦合BCS极限。费米能级附近谱权重的抑制在超导转变温度以上持续存在，普遍存在的瀑布状谱特征证明了电子相互作用的存在。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了d_{z²}轨道和电子关联在镍酸盐超导中的关键作用，为镍酸盐超导的理论模型提供了重要约束。这些发现表明三维电子结构和轨道特性对理解镍酸盐超导机制至关重要。

Abstract: Beyond the quasi-two-dimensional (2D) paradigm of cuprates, the role of the third dimension of the Ruddlesden-Popper bilayer nickelates is essential to decoding their superconducting mechanism. Here, using angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) with varied photon energies, we systematically investigate the electronic band structures in three dimensions for superconducting (La,Pr,Sm)$_3$Ni$2$O$7$/SrLaAlO$4$ thin films (superconducting onset temperature $T_c^{\text{onset}} \sim 48$ K) transferred via a cryogenic ultra-high vacuum suitcase. We reveal an orbital-dependent dimensionality: while the $d{x^2-y^2}$-dominant bands exhibit a quasi-2D character, the $d{z^2}$-dominant band displays a finite $k_z$ dispersion. Finite energy gaps are identified on all observed bands across multiple high-symmetry directions. Systematic temperature-dependent analysis characterizes the superconducting nature of the gap on the $d{z^2}$-derived band, revealing a large gap $Δ\sim 18$ meV and a ratio $2Δ/k_BT_c\sim 8$ exceeding the weak-coupling BCS limit. The suppression of spectral weight near the Fermi level persists above the superconducting transition temperature. Ubiquitous waterfall-like spectral features evidence the presence of electron interactions. These results underscore the role of the $d_{z^2}$ orbital and correlations, placing constraints on theoretical models for nickelate superconductivity.

</details>

### [28] [Holographic Krylov Complexity for Charged, Composite and Extended Probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07432)
*Horatiu Nastase,Carlos Nunez,Dibakar Roychowdhury*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了具有非平凡内部结构和真正延展算子的全息扩展/Krylov复杂度。通过分析AdS$_5\times S^5$中携带守恒$R$荷的大质量粒子、重子顶点构型和巨引力子等结构化探针，以及延展的基本弦模型，揭示了内部结构和空间延展性对复杂度增长的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在扩展全息Krylov复杂度的分析范畴，探索具有内部结构和空间延展性的算子的复杂度特性。这有助于理解哪些特征是普适的，哪些依赖于算子的具体性质，并为理解带电、复合和延展激发的复杂度提供更清晰的场论框架。

Method: 采用全息对偶方法，首先研究AdS$_5\times S^5$中携带守恒$R$荷的大质量粒子，展示内部空间运动如何修正复杂度增长。接着分析从场论视角看似点状但具有体空间内在结构的探针：重子顶点构型（baryon-vertex configurations）和巨引力子（giant gravitons）。最后研究真正延展的探针：沿空间方向拉伸并落入AdS的基本弦（fundamental string）。

Result: 对于结构化但点状的探针，主导的大时间行为保留了共形场论中局域算子的特征形式，而内部结构和诱导荷产生信息丰富的次主导效应。对于延展探针，虽然主导行为仍显示预期的增长模式，但次主导项和中间区域与点状探针存在质的差异，表明延展算子携带对空间结构敏感的精细扩展复杂度概念。

Conclusion: 研究拓宽了可显式分析全息Krylov复杂度的探针类别，澄清了哪些特征是普适的、哪些依赖于算子性质。结果为理解带电、复合和延展激发的复杂度提供了具体证据，并开辟了通往更精确场论理解的途径，特别是对称分辨Krylov复杂度（symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity）的自然全息实现。

Abstract: We study the holographic spread/Krylov complexity of operators with non-trivial internal structure and of genuinely extended operators. We first consider a massive particle in AdS$_5\times S^5$ carrying conserved $R$-charge, and show how motion in the internal space modifies the complexity growth, yielding a natural holographic realisation of symmetry-resolved Krylov complexity. We then move to probes that are effectively pointlike from the field-theory viewpoint but possess an intrinsic structure in the bulk: baryon-vertex configurations and giant gravitons. Our results indicate that, for this broad class of structured but pointlike probes, the leading large-time behaviour retains the characteristic form expected for local operators in conformal theories, while the internal structure and induced charges produce informative subleading effects.
  We also study a genuinely extended probe, a fundamental string falling in AdS while stretched along a spatial direction, as a model for the spread complexity of a non-local operator. In this case, although the leading behaviour still exhibits the expected growth pattern, the subleading terms and intermediate regimes differ qualitatively from those of pointlike probes. This provides concrete evidence that extended operators carry a finer notion of spread complexity, sensitive to their spatial structure. Our results broaden the class of probes for which holographic Krylov complexity can be analysed explicitly, clarify which features are universal and which depend on the nature of the operator, and open a promising route toward a sharper field-theory understanding of complexity for charged, composite and extended excitations.

</details>


### [29] [A Duality Web for Non-Supersymmetric Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07433)
*Zihni Kaan Baykara,Matilda Delgado,Emilian Dudas,Hector Parra De Freitas,Cumrun Vafa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文基于M-理论和F-理论的几何描述，构建了非超对称弦理论的对偶网络，特别是通过$\mathbb{Z}_2$商构造将0A/0B定向面与E型/D型非超对称杂化弦联系起来，并验证了Bergman-Gaberdiel对偶和DMS猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于近期M-理论和F-理论中0A与0B弦的几何描述进展，旨在探索非超对称弦理论之间的对偶关系网络，特别是通过不同的$\mathbb{Z}_2$商构造来统一理解各类弦真空。

Method: 采用几何构造方法，对M-理论在$S^1\vee S^1$上进行不同的$\mathbb{Z}_2$商操作，以及对F-理论在$(S^1\vee S^1)\times S^1$上进行$\mathbb{Z}_2$商操作，从而生成0A/0B定向面（orientifolds）和非超对称杂化弦（heterotic strings）真空。

Result: 研究结果表明，M-理论的$\mathbb{Z}_2$商可产生0A定向面以及E型非超对称10维杂化真空，包括无快子（tachyon-free）的$SO(16)\times SO(16)$弦；F-理论的$\mathbb{Z}_2$商则产生0B定向面（包括无快子模型）以及与D型非超对称杂化弦对偶的构造。

Conclusion: 通过这一几何图像，研究解决了若干疑难问题，并为Bergman-Gaberdiel对偶（特定10维0B定向面与26维玻色弦在16维环面上Narain紧化的对偶）以及DMS猜想（10维0A定向面与玻色弦定向面在Narain紧化至10维的对偶）提供了进一步证据。

Abstract: Motivated by the recently proposed geometric descriptions of 0A and 0B in M-theory and F-theory, we propose a web of duality among non-supersymmetric strings. In particular we argue that the distinct $\mathbb{Z}_2$ quotients of M-theory on $S^1\vee S^1$ lead to both 0A orientifolds as well as non-supersymmetric 10d heterotic vacua of the E-type, including the tachyon-free $SO(16)\times SO(16)$ strings. Moreover we identify certain $\mathbb{Z}_2$ quotients of F-theory on $(S^1\vee S^1)\times S^1$ with 0B orientifolds (including a tachyon-free model) as well as others with dual to non-supersymmetric heterotic strings of the D-type. Moreover using this picture we resolve some puzzles and provide further evidence for the Bergman-Gaberdiel duality between a particular 0B orientifold in 10 dimensions and the Narain compactification of 26-dimensional bosonic strings on a 16-dimensional torus, as well as the DMS conjecture of a 0A orientifold duality in 10d with a bosonic string orientifold of a Narain compactification to 10d.

### [30] [Resurgence of high-energy string amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07444)
*Xavier Kervyn,Stephan Stieberger*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文从多角度分析n点树级弦振幅的高能固定角极限结构，揭示了高能展开系数由伯努利数而非低能区的多重zeta值组织，并通过复现理论将发散级数提升为跨级数，统一了低能和高能展开的解析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究弦振幅在固定角高能极限（α'→∞）下的结构，与低能极限（α'→0）形成对比，探索不同能区展开系数的数学结构差异及其统一描述。

Method: 采用多种互补方法：局部鞍点展开、代数差分方程及其渐近结构、Aomoto-Gauss-Manin连接和Mellin-Barnes表示的解析方法，以及扭曲相交理论和Lefschetz thimbles的几何方法。

Result: 高能展开的微扰系数由伯努利数（Bernoulli numbers）而非多重zeta值（multiple zeta values）组织；通过复现理论（resurgence theory）将发散级数提升为跨级数（transseries），其Stokes数据以非微扰单值贡献形式捕获非物理与物理运动学区域间的解析延拓；建立了统一低能和高能展开的微分与Mellin表述。

Conclusion: 弦振幅的高能和低能展开可通过统一的解析框架描述，其中高能展开系数具有伯努利数结构，且通过扭曲de Rham理论和Lefschetz thimbles可获得闭弦振幅高能极限的替代双拷贝表示。

Abstract: We analyze the fixed-angle high-energy ($α' \to \infty$) structure of $n$-point tree-level string amplitudes from complementary perspectives: locally via saddle-point expansions, algebraically via difference equations and their asymptotic structure, analytically via Aomoto-Gauss-Manin connection and Mellin-Barnes representation, and geometrically via twisted intersection theory and Lefschetz thimbles. Using, in turn, saddle-point analysis and finite-difference equations in the kinematic variables, we show that the perturbative coefficients in the resulting asymptotic series in $1/α'$ are organized by Bernoulli-number data, rather than by the multiple zeta values characteristic of the low-energy $α' \to 0$ regime. Resurgence theory allows upgrading these divergent series to transseries whose Stokes data capture the analytic continuation between unphysical and physical kinematic regions in the form of non-perturbative monodromy contributions. We derive the transseries for four-point open string amplitudes explicitly. We also construct a differential and Mellin formulation which place their low- and high-energy expansions in a common analytic framework and unifies them as asymptotic sectors of the same underlying object. We extend the difference-equation analysis to $n \geq 5$, where it yields perturbative high-energy asymptotic expansions and leads naturally to a higher-rank connection problem. Finally, translating our asymptotic analysis into the language of twisted de Rham theory, we derive an alternative double-copy representation of the high-energy limit of closed-string amplitudes in terms of Lefschetz thimbles for any $n$.

### [31] [The $\mathcal{N}=1$ Super-Grassmannian for CFT$_3$ and a Foray on AdS and Cosmological Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07446)
*Aswini Bala,Sachin Jain,Dhruva K. S.,Adithya A Rao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文构建了三维N=1超共形场论中n点函数的超Grassmann积分表示，通过该形式体系实现了共形不变性、超对称性和特殊超共形不变性的显式表达，并建立了分量关联函数间的简单代数关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为三维N=1超共形场论（N=1 SCFT₃）的n点函数构建一个形式化框架，该框架能够显式地实现共形不变性、超对称性和特殊超共形不变性，从而简化关联函数的计算和分析。

Method: 方法是通过构造超Grassmann积分表示（Super-Grassmannian integral representation），利用算子值delta函数约束显式地实现对称性要求，并建立分量关联函数间的代数关系。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）获得了分量关联函数间的简单代数关系，使得任何分量关联函数都可以通过其中一个分量确定；2）能够从纯粒子交换贡献的关联函数构造带接触图的(A)dS₄边界关联函数；3）通过胶微子对应项确定了(A)dS₄杨-米尔斯胶子四点函数；4）在超空间中建立了平直空间极限，与现有平直空间结果完全一致。

Conclusion: 该超Grassmann积分形式体系为三维超共形场论提供了强有力的计算框架，不仅简化了关联函数的计算，还能自然地推广到(A)dS₄边界关联函数的构造，并在平直空间极限下与已知结果一致。

Abstract: We construct a Super-Grassmannian integral representation for $n-$point functions in $\mathcal{N}=1$ SCFT$_3$. In this formalism, conformal invariance, supersymmetry, and special superconformal invariance are implemented manifestly through (operator-valued) delta function constraints. An important feature of this framework is the fact that we obtain simple algebraic relations among component correlators, which enable us to determine any component correlator in terms of just one of the component correlators. In particular, this formalism enables us to construct (A)dS$_4$ boundary correlators with contact diagrams from those that receive contributions purely from particle exchanges. We illustrate this by determining the (A)dS$_4$ Yang-Mills gluon four-point function from its gluino counterpart. Further, we establish the flat-space limit in super-space, finding a perfect agreement with existing flat-space results.

### [32] [Quantum Fluctuations and Newton-Cartan Geometry for Non-Relativistic de Sitter space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07449)
*Matthias Harksen,Diego Hidalgo,Watse Sybesma*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究二维德西特引力（de Sitter gravity）的非相对论实现，从边界和体描述两方面探讨，旨在理解德西特空间并为全息对偶（holographic duality）向非相对论方向扩展铺路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是深入理解德西特空间（de Sitter space），并为将全息对偶（holographic duality）扩展到非相对论方向奠定基础。通过分析二维德西特引力的非相对论实现，可以从边界和体两个角度获得新的物理洞见。

Method: 研究方法包括边界侧分析非相对论德西特引力的施瓦茨型边界作用量（Schwarzian-type boundary action），并计算其一圈配分函数（one-loop partition function）以评估量子涨落。不同于余伴随轨道构造（coadjoint-orbit construction），直接使用奥斯特罗格拉茨基形式（Ostrogradsky formalism）从作用量推导路径积分测度。体侧则构建相应的无挠牛顿-嘉当几何（torsionless Newton-Cartan geometry）。

Result: 研究结果显示温度依赖的前因子按$T^2$标度变化，其幂次与存在的四个全局对称生成元计数一致。在体侧，证明该几何满足非相对论JT类作用量（non-relativistic JT-like action）的运动方程，并将几何提升到三维洛伦兹几何（three-dimensional Lorentzian geometry）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功实现了二维德西特引力的非相对论描述，在边界侧获得了量子涨落的精确结果，在体侧建立了相应的几何结构，为全息对偶向非相对论方向的扩展提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study a non-relativistic realisation of two-dimensional de Sitter gravity both from its boundary and bulk description with the goal of learning about de Sitter space and paving the way for extending the holographic duality into a non-relativistic direction. On the boundary side, we analyse the Schwarzian-type boundary action associated with non-relativistic de Sitter gravity and evaluate its one-loop partition function in order to compute its quantum fluctuations. Rather than relying on the coadjoint-orbit construction, we derive the path integral measure directly from the action using the Ostrogradsky formalism. We find a temperature-dependent prefactor scaling as $T^2$, of which the power agrees with the counting of the four global symmetry generators present. On the bulk side, we construct the corresponding torsionless Newton-Cartan geometry and show that it satisfies the equations of motion of a non-relativistic JT-like action and uplift the geometry to a three-dimensional Lorentzian geometry.

</details>


### [33] [Decoding multiway gravitational junctions in AdS in terms of holographic quantum maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07463)
*Avik Chakraborty,Tanay Kibe,Martín Molina,Ayan Mukhopadhyay,Giuseppe Policastro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究多路连接（multiway junctions）的引力散射问题，这些连接将n个局部AdS₃时空粘合在一起，并探讨其在全息对偶中作为n个共形场论之间界面的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多路连接及其弦自由度如何被解释为n个相同全息共形理论之间的界面，每个理论定义在半无限线上。这扩展了早期关于2路连接的结果，旨在理解更一般情况下的对偶界面性质。

Method: 通过研究多路连接处的引力散射问题，在线性化阶分析对偶界面。使用由弦模式控制的相对自同构和仅由连接张力决定的散射矩阵来描述量子映射。

Result: 在线性化阶，对偶界面对应于量子映射，该映射可分解为仅由对偶连接张力决定的散射矩阵和由n-1个弦模式控制的Virasoro代数的相对自同构的乘积。这些结果具有普遍性，与背景态的线性修改无关。

Conclusion: 该研究推广了早期关于2路连接的结果，表明对偶界面是可调的能量传输器。论文还讨论了理解完整非线性引力问题对应的量子映射，并研究了Ward恒等式和幺正性界限。

Abstract: It has been shown that multiway junctions gluing $n$ copies of locally AdS$_3$ spacetimes ($n\geq 2$) can be described by $n-1$ strings obeying non-linear Nambu-Goto equations coupled by Monge-Ampère like terms. Here we study how such junctions along with their stringy degrees of freedom can be interpreted in terms of an interface between $n$ identical holographic conformal theories each defined on a semi-infinite line (wire). We study the gravitational scattering problem at the multiway junction, and show that at the linearized order the dual interfaces correspond to quantum maps which factorize into a product of a scattering matrix determined only by the tension of the dual junction and relative automorphisms of the Virasoro algebra governed by the $n-1$ stringy modes. Both of these are universal in the sense that they are independent of linear modifications of the background state. These generalize earlier results for the 2-way junctions implying that the dual interface is a tunable energy transmitter. We comment on understanding the quantum map corresponding to the full non-linear gravitational problem, and study Ward identities and unitarity bounds.

</details>


### [34] [Analytical solution to DGLAP integro-differential equation via complex maps in domains of contour integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/1912.02303)
*Gustavo Alvarez,Igor Kondrashuk*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究在简化DGLAP方程的单项劈裂函数模型中，通过复映射将DGLAP方程转化为BFKL方程，并利用复微分同胚将部分子分布函数的围道积分转化为标准积分形式，验证了贝塞尔函数的拉普拉斯逆变换可表示为巴恩斯围道积分。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用复平面上的梅林矩（Mellin moment）映射技术，将简化DGLAP方程转化为对偶积分微分方程（dual integro-differential equation）。进一步应用复微分同胚（complex diffeomorphism）将部分子分布函数（parton distribution functions）的围道积分（contour integral）转化为Gradshteyn和Ryzhik积分表中的标准积分形式。

Result: 研究发现该对偶积分微分方程可视为BFKL方程，且标准积分形式表现为复微分同胚雅可比行列式（Jacobian）的拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transformation）。验证了贝塞尔函数（Bessel function）的拉普拉斯逆变换（inverse Laplace transformation）可表示为巴恩斯围道积分（Barnes contour integral）形式。

Conclusion: 该研究系统阐述了简化DGLAP模型中的数学变换框架，为后续策略发展提供了重要理论基础。通过复映射技术建立了DGLAP与BFKL方程之间的联系，并揭示了相关积分变换的数学结构。

Abstract: A simple model for QCD dynamics in which the DGLAP integro-differential equation may be solved analytically has been considered in our previous papers arXiv:1611.08787 [hep-ph] and arXiv:1906.07924 [hep-ph]. When such a model contains only one term in the splitting function of the dominant parton distribution, then Bessel function appears to be the solution to this simplified DGLAP equation. To our knowledge, this model with only one term in the splitting function for the first time has been proposed by Blumlein in hep-ph/9506403. In arXiv:1906.07924 [hep-ph] we have shown that a dual integro-differential equation obtained from the DGLAP equation by a complex map in the plane of the Mellin moment in this model may be considered as the BFKL equation. Then, in arXiv:1906.07924 we have applied a complex diffeomorphism to obtain a standard integral from Gradshteyn and Ryzhik tables starting from the contour integral for parton distribution functions that is usually taken by calculus of residues. This standard integral from these tables appears to be the Laplace transformation of Jacobian for this complex diffeomorphism. Here we write up all the formulae behind this trick in detail and find out certain important points for further development of this strategy. We verify that the inverse Laplace transformation of the Laplace image of the Bessel function may be represented in a form of Barnes contour integral.

### [35] [From Matrix Models to Gaussian Molecules and the Einstein-Hilbert Action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07500)

Conclusion: 该矩阵模型为非微扰离散弦理论提供了统一框架，能够自然导出引力理论和规范理论的基本作用量。模型不要求度规满足壳上条件（on-shell condition），且相关常数在弦微扰展开中完全确定，体现了矩阵模型与弦理论之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: A matrix model on a D-dimensional Euclidean space is introduced as a generalization of random matrix models and as a non-perturbative definition of discretized closed string theory. The free energy of the matrix model is formally derived to all orders in string perturbation expansion and shown to be given in terms of invariant graph polynomials, whose coefficients enumerate ribbon graphs and are a refinement of the generalized Catalan numbers. The vacuum diagrams contributing to the free energy are found to be related to Gaussian molecules, known from the study of polymer structures.
  Coupling the matrix field to a curved background with Riemannian metric yields a non-perturbative definition of discretized string theory on this background. No on-shell condition for the metric is required to arrive at the free energy. Rather, it is shown that the free energy of the matrix model is the Einstein-Hilbert action with cosmological constant term. The gravitational and the cosmological constants are both formally determined to all orders in the string perturbation expansion. In fact, they are explicitly given by the expectation value of a particular graph invariant.
  Introducing a vector field, minimally coupled to a background gauge field, provides a discretized open-closed string theory, leading to the Yang-Mills action as well as intrinsic and extrinsic curvature terms.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在$\mathcal{N}=2$情况下成功重现了四胶子关联函数；在$\mathcal{N}=4$情况下构建了两种不同的超算子：一种包含自旋0到2的所有态，另一种以CPT自共轭方式构建，仅包含自旋0、1/2和1的算子，后者在平直空间极限下与$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM振幅直接匹配。

We test our formalism in $\mathcal{N}=2$ and $\mathcal{N}=4$ AdS$_4$ super Yang-Mills theories. In the $\mathcal{N}=2$ case, for instance, we reproduce the four-gluon correlator using the four-point scalar correlator as input. For $\mathcal{N}=4$, we construct the super-operator in two distinct ways. In one approach, the super-operator has a lowest component of spin zero and includes all states up to spin two. In the other approach, we build the super-operator in a CPT self-conjugate manner, which contains only operators with spin zero, spin half, and spin one mimicking flat space $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM super-field constructions. The latter construction is particularly interesting, as it matches directly with the $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM amplitudes in the flat space limit, thereby demonstrating the non-triviality and usefulness of our framework. Abstract: The Sen action for self-dual fields has been generalised by Hull to include two metrics which allows it to be defined on generic manifolds. In this paper we consider Kaluza-Klein compactifications of this action. The existence of two metrics presents novel challenges as there are two Kaluza-Klein towers of fields. We show that to find a consistent truncation one must include zero-modes associated to each of the two towers. Although this naively leads to a doubling of the massless degrees of freedom we show that on-shell this is not the case. We also discuss a deformation of the Sen action to include an additional form-field but which does not lead to new degrees of freedom on-shell but which arises naturally upon compactification.

Method: 从Hinterbichler和Rosen先前考虑的多标架相互作用一般类别出发，该类别包含标架（vielbeins）的反对称化乘积。我们为这些理论的无鬼性制定了必要条件。

Result: 对于两个标架，理论参数不受限制，重现了无鬼双度规理论（ghost-free bimetric theory）。但对于具有真正多场相互作用的两个以上标架，耦合被精确限制为产生已知的无鬼多标架理论，从而确立了其唯一性。

Abstract: So far, only a single theory of multiple spin-2 fields is known that features genuine multi-field interactions while remaining free of Boulware-Deser-type ghost instabilities. In this paper we show that this is the most general ghost-free multi spin-2 interaction type possible. We start with the general class of multivielbein interactions containing antisymmetrised products of vielbeins, considered earlier by Hinterbichler and Rosen. We formulate a necessary condition for these theories to be ghost-free. For two vielbeins the theory parameters remain unrestricted, reproducing the ghost-free bimetric theory. But for more than two vielbeins with genuine multi-field interactions, we show that the couplings are restricted precisely to yield the known ghost-free multivielbein theory, thus establishing its uniqueness. We also show that more general interactions, constructed using the ghost-free bimetric and multivielbein potentials as building blocks, satisfy the necessary ghost-free conditions provided the associated interaction graphs have a tree structure.

### [39] [Vacuum-induced current density from a magnetic flux threading a cosmic dispiration in $(D+1)$-dimensional spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07648)
*Herondy Mota*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过构建Klein-Gordon方程的归一化模函数，计算Wightman函数，进而获得电流密度的真空期望值。该方法适用于任意维度和质量场，包括有质量和无质量情况。

Abstract: We investigate the vacuum-induced current density for a charged scalar field in a $(D+1)$-dimensional cosmic dispiration spacetime threaded by a magnetic flux. This background combines a cosmic string and a screw dislocation, yielding a nontrivial helical geometry. By constructing the normalized mode functions of the Klein--Gordon equation, we evaluate the Wightman function and obtain the vacuum expectation value of the current density. We show that, in addition to the azimuthal component describing a persistent current around the defect, a nonvanishing axial component is induced as a direct consequence of the helical structure of the spacetime. Both components are periodic functions of the magnetic flux, depending only on its fractional part, reflecting the Aharonov--Bohm nature of the effect. Closed expressions are obtained for both massive and massless fields in arbitrary dimensions. We demonstrate that the screw dislocation parameter plays a crucial role in the behavior of the induced currents, leading to the regularization of the axial component at the origin and controlling its magnitude. The asymptotic behavior of both components is analyzed in detail. Our results reduce to known expressions in the absence of the screw dislocation, providing a consistency check. In particular, we examine the physically relevant $(3+1)$-dimensional case, where numerical analysis reveals nontrivial features arising from the interplay between topology and gauge effects.

### [41] [Linearized Q-Ball Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07713)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Linearized deformations of the thick-walled (low-amplitude) (1+1)-dimensional Q-ball may be decomposed into relativistic modes, which are roughly plane waves, and also long-wavelength corotating and counterrotating Floquet modes. Each mode oscillates at a pair of mirror frequencies which average to the Q-ball frequency. The corotating modes are those of a breather or oscillon plus a very loosely bound mode. The counterrotating modes are described by an irrational-level Pöschl-Teller potential, with two discrete modes which mix with their unbound mirrors, unbinding them and turning them into Feshbach-type quasinormal modes. Motivation: 研究动机在于探索费米子与电磁场之间的非最小导数耦合（nonminimal derivative couplings），这些耦合在一维量子环中产生类Rashba自旋-轨道相互作用（Rashba-like spin-orbit interactions）。与标准凝聚态物理场景不同，该研究旨在揭示磁场和电场背景均可能引发Rashba型相互作用的机制。

Method: 研究方法基于包含两个独立轴结构（axial structures）的广义狄拉克拉格朗日量（generalized Dirac Lagrangian），这些结构由场强$F_{μν}$及其对偶$\tilde{F}_{μν}$构建。研究首先进行系统性的非相对论展开（nonrelativistic expansion），然后详细分析模型的相对论内容，包括变形狄拉克算符（deformed Dirac operator）的规范结构、可容许的背景类别、有效双线性电流（effective bilinear current）以及相对论色散关系（relativistic dispersion relation）的分支分裂。

Result: 研究结果显示，两种耦合均诱导出形式为$\boldsymbol{\mathcal{F}}\cdot(\boldsymbol{p}\times\boldsymbolσ)$的有效哈密顿量，表明磁场和电场背景均可产生Rashba型相互作用。研究推导了精确解析能级和归一化本征旋量，计算了Aharonov-Anandan几何相位，并分析了持续自旋电流（persistent spin currents）及其相关的微分自旋响应$\mathcal{G}_s = \partial\mathcal{J}_\varphi^z/\partialξ$。此外，研究首次从光谱学和介观场景推导了对两个洛伦兹不变耦合$\mathfrak{g}_1$和$\mathfrak{g}_2$的系统性数量级约束。

Conclusion: 该研究系统揭示了非最小导数耦合在量子环中产生类Rashba相互作用的机制，并建立了对耦合参数的理论约束。研究还讨论了物理含义、特征信号和可能的实验类比，并展望了涉及无序、噪声和非平衡自旋动力学的多个有前景的研究方向。

Abstract: We investigate a class of nonminimal derivative couplings between fermions and electromagnetic fields that generate Rashba-like spin--orbit interactions in one-dimensional quantum rings. Starting from a generalized Dirac Lagrangian containing two independent axial structures built from the field strength $F_{μν}$ and its dual $\tilde{F}_{μν}$, we perform a systematic nonrelativistic expansion and show that both couplings induce effective Hamiltonians of the form $\boldsymbol{\mathcal{F}}\cdot(\boldsymbol{p}\times\boldsymbolσ)$. This reveals that magnetic as well as electric background fields may give rise to Rashba-type interactions, in contrast with standard condensed-matter scenarios. Before passing to the nonrelativistic limit, we analyze the relativistic content of the model in detail: the canonical structure of the deformed Dirac operator, the admissible background classes, the effective bilinear current, and the branch splitting of the relativistic dispersion relation, which constitutes the primary relativistic signature of the theory. We derive exact analytical energy levels and normalized eigenspinors for the resulting ring Hamiltonian, compute Aharonov--Anandan geometric phases, and analyze persistent spin currents together with the associated differential spin response $\mathcal{G}_s = \partial\mathcal{J}_\varphi^z/\partialξ$. Exploiting the analytical control offered by the model, we derive the first systematic order-of-magnitude bounds on the two Lorentz-invariant couplings $\mathfrak{g}_1$ and $\mathfrak{g}_2$ from both spectroscopic and mesoscopic scenarios, identifying the experimental channels most sensitive to the new physics encoded in these operators. We discuss physical implications, signatures, and possible experimental analogs, and outline several promising directions involving disorder, noise, and nonequilibrium spin dynamics.

</details>

*Daichi Ide,Katsushi Ito,Wataru Kono*
