<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索ODE/IM对应关系（ordinary differential equation/integrable model correspondence）在E₆⁽¹⁾仿射李代数（affine Lie algebra）相关常微分方程中的适用性，验证这一数学物理对应关系的普适性。

Method: 采用对角化方法（diagonalization method）对ODE的解进行WKB展开（WKB expansion），并计算WKB系数沿Pochhammer围道（Pochhammer contour）的周期积分。同时计算二维共形场论（two-dimensional conformal field theory）中与E₆⁽¹⁾相关的W-对称性（W-symmetry）在柱面上的运动积分（integrals of motion）。

Result: 计算结果显示，二维共形场论中运动积分在最高权态（highest-weight state）上的特征值与ODE的周期积分在六阶精度内完全一致，验证了ODE/IM对应关系在E₆⁽¹⁾情况下的正确性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功验证了ODE/IM对应关系对于E₆⁽¹⁾仿射李代数相关常微分方程的适用性，为这一数学物理对应关系在更广泛代数结构中的推广提供了重要证据。

Abstract: We study the ODE/IM correspondence for the ordinary differential equation associated with the affine Lie algebra $E_6^{(1)}$. The WKB expansion of the solution of the ODE is performed by the diagonalization method, and the period integrals of the WKB coefficients along the Pochhammer contour are calculated. We also compute the integrals of motion on a cylinder in two-dimensional conformal field theory with W-symmetry associated with $E_6^{(1)}$. Their eigenvalues on the highest-weight state are shown to agree with the period integrals up to the sixth order.

### [44] [Rindler Physics with a UV Cutoff on the Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07915)
*Seiken Chikazawa,Seiji Terashima*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过晶格化Rindler空间中的自由标量场，探讨了具有紫外截断（UV cutoff）的量子场论。研究发现，相对于局域晶格Rindler哈密顿量，闵可夫斯基真空并非精确热态，但远离视界的可观测量在连续极限下仍呈现预期的热行为。紫外截断导致全局闵可夫斯基描述与基于局域Rindler哈密顿量的楔形描述在算符层面不再等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨紫外截断（UV cutoff）如何影响Rindler空间中的量子场论，特别是Unruh效应在晶格化处理下的表现。该工作旨在理解截断引入后，全局闵可夫斯基描述与局域Rindler描述之间的等价性是否仍然成立。

Method: 采用晶格化方法，在Rindler坐标中研究自由标量场，引入紫外截断。通过分析Wightman函数、Unruh-DeWitt探测器响应、Rindler真空能量密度以及推迟格林函数（retarded Green function）等物理量，考察截断效应。

Result: 研究发现，闵可夫斯基真空相对于局域晶格Rindler哈密顿量并非精确热态。然而，对于远离视界的可观测量，Wightman函数和Unruh-DeWitt探测器响应在连续极限下重现预期的热行为。视界处的紫外奇异性被拉伸视界（stretched-horizon）贡献所取代，推迟格林函数显示在拉伸视界处存在反射分量。

Conclusion: 结论表明，Unruh效应在操作意义上仍然存在，尽管在态层面失去了精确热性。紫外截断引入后，全局闵可夫斯基描述与基于局域Rindler哈密顿量的楔形描述在算符层面不再等价，这为紫外正则化理论提供了有效的"砖墙"图像（brick-wall picture）。

Abstract: We investigate quantum field theory in Rindler space with a UV cutoff by considering a free scalar field on a lattice in Rindler coordinates. We find that the Minkowski vacuum is not exactly thermal with respect to the local lattice Rindler Hamiltonian. Nevertheless, for observables sufficiently far from the horizon, the Wightman function and the Unruh--DeWitt detector response reproduce the expected thermal behavior in the continuum limit. Thus, the Unruh effect survives operationally, even though exact thermality is lost at the state level. We also show that the Rindler vacuum energy density reproduces the standard continuum behavior away from the horizon, while the UV singularity at the horizon is replaced by a stretched-horizon contribution. Furthermore, the retarded Green function exhibits a component reflected at the stretched horizon, implying that an ingoing wave packet is reflected at a proper distance of order the cutoff. This provides an effective brick-wall picture in the UV-regulated theory. Our analysis suggests that, once a cutoff is introduced, the global Minkowski description and the wedge description based on a local Rindler Hamiltonian are no longer equivalent at the operator level.

### [45] [Classification of Pati--Salam Asymmetric $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ Heterotic String Orbifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07950)
*Luke A. Detraux,Alon E. Faraggi,Benjamin Percival*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We develop a systematic classification of asymmetric $\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold actions in Pati--Salam heterotic string vacua constructed in the free fermionic formulation. Starting from symmetric $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold vacua with an $SO(10)$ GUT, we allow the Pati--Salam breaking vector to act asymmetrically on the internal degrees of freedom. The asymmetric orbifold action freezes geometrical moduli whilst inducing doublet--triplet splitting in the untwisted sector. Notably, this doublet--triplet splitting operates for any asymmetric action, including pure asymmetric shifts that preserve all geometric moduli, and is therefore independent of moduli stabilisation. Classifying the breaking vector according to its twist action, we find six inequivalent classes of geometric moduli spaces characterised by 12, 8, 4 or 0 real untwisted moduli. Through combining these asymmetric twists with all compatible asymmetric shifts, 24 inequivalent cases are identified and characterised by their residual moduli content and internal Narain lattice. For each case we construct representative basis sets admitting three chiral generations, providing the starting point for further classification within each class. We perform explicit GGSO phase enumerations in representative model classes with 12, 8, 4 and 0 moduli, classify the resulting $\mathcal{N} = 1$ and $\mathcal{N} = 0$ vacua according to phenomenological criteria and identify exophobic, phenomenologically viable models. We compute the partition function and corresponding one-loop vacuum energy at the free fermionic point in moduli space for each phenomenologically viable model across the four classes. As the number of geometrical moduli decreases, the number of distinct partition functions for these vacua collapses to a small number, reflecting a pronounced degeneracy under GGSO phase variations.

### [46] [Leading low-temperature correction to the Heisenberg-Euler Lagrangian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07996)
*Felix Karbstein*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明海森堡-欧拉拉格朗日量（Heisenberg-Euler Lagrangian）在恒定电磁场中的两圈图低温领头修正，可以从其单圈零温对应项中高效提取。通过实时形式（real-time formalism）分离零温贡献与有限温度修正，该计算变得极为简单，仅需对单圈零温拉格朗日量求场强导数。此外，通过单粒子可约蝌蚪图（one-particle reducible tadpole structures）有效修饰两圈低温贡献，生成了低温极限下高阶圈图贡献的子集，并对其领头强场行为进行了提取和全阶求和。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用平衡量子场论的实时形式（real-time formalism），明确分离零温贡献与有限温度修正。核心方法是对单圈零温海森堡-欧拉拉格朗日量求场强导数，从而提取两圈低温领头修正。进一步通过单粒子可约蝌蚪图结构修饰低温贡献，生成高阶圈图贡献的子集。

Result: 成功从单圈零温拉格朗日量中高效提取了两圈低温领头修正，计算过程变得极为简单。通过蝌蚪图修饰生成了低温极限下高阶圈图贡献的子集，并提取了给定圈阶下的领头强场行为。最终实现了这些贡献的全阶求和（resummation）。

Conclusion: 本文建立了海森堡-欧拉拉格朗日量不同圈阶低温修正之间的直接联系，提供了一种高效计算两圈低温领头修正的简化方法。通过蝌蚪图结构进一步扩展了该方法，能够生成并求和低温极限下的高阶圈图贡献子集，为有限温度量子电动力学（QED）计算提供了新视角。

Abstract: In this note, we show that the well-known leading low-temperature correction to the Heisenberg-Euler Lagrangian in a constant electromagnetic field arising at two loops can be efficiently extracted from its one-loop zero-temperature analogue. Resorting to the real-time formalism of equilibrium quantum field theory that explicitly separates out the zero-temperature contribution from the finite-temperature corrections the determination becomes essentially trivial. In essence, it only requires taking derivatives of the Heisenberg-Euler Lagrangian at one loop and zero temperature for the field strength. As a bonus, we then effectively dress the low-temperature contribution at two loops by one-particle reducible tadpole structures. This generates a subset of higher-loop contributions to the Heisenberg-Euler Lagrangian in the limit of low temperatures. We extract their leading strong-field behavior at a given loop order, and finally resum these to all loop orders.

### [48] [Hard to shock DBI: wave propagation on planar domain walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08142)
*E. Babichev,B. Gafarov,S. Ramazanov,M. Valencia-Villegas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了薄平面畴壁上由标量DBI模型描述的波传播，重点关注焦散（激波）形成过程及其对畴壁粒子发射的影响。研究发现，在2D平直时空的双曲情况下，从光滑初始条件出发不会产生奇异性，但在更高维、膨胀宇宙或修正DBI模型中，特征曲线不再平行，不过DBI在这些物理相关情境中仍保持无激波状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究薄平面畴壁上由标量DBI（Dirac-Born-Infeld）模型描述的波传播特性，特别关注焦散（caustic）或激波（shock）形成的可能性。这一过程可能导致畴壁产生强烈的粒子发射，对宇宙学中的畴壁问题具有重要意义。

Method: 通过分析标量DBI模型在薄平面畴壁上的波传播特性，采用特征曲线（characteristic curves）方法研究相关偏微分方程（PDE）。研究涵盖了2D平直时空、更高维度的球面波、膨胀宇宙（expanding Universe）以及为避免宇宙学畴壁问题所需的最小修正DBI模型等多种物理情境。

Result: 在2D平直时空的双曲（hyperbolic）情况下，从光滑初始条件出发不会产生奇异性，因为相关PDE的特征曲线族始终保持平行（尽管通常不是直线）。然而，在更高维度、膨胀宇宙或修正DBI模型中，特征曲线不再保持平行。尽管如此，研究证明DBI在所有物理相关情境的双曲情况下仍保持无激波状态。

Conclusion: 平面畴壁上的焦散形成只能源于双曲性的丧失，且具有尖点（cusp）轮廓。本文揭示的超越2D平直时空设置的DBI特征曲线非平凡结构能显著影响尖点形成过程，这为理解畴壁动力学提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We investigate propagation of generic waves on thin planar domain walls effectively described by the scalar DBI model. We pay a particular attention to the possibility of caustic (shock) formation - the process, which may lead to intensive particle emission by domain walls. It is demonstrated that no singularities arise in DBI in 2D flat spacetime in the hyperbolic case, if one starts from smooth initial conditions. Technically, this happens because the same family characteristics of the relevant PDE remain parallel at all the times, albeit not being straight lines generically. Crucially, characteristic curves cease to be parallel beyond the simplified setup of DBI in 2D flat spacetime. In particular, this is shown to be the case in $D>2$ for spherical waves, in an expanding Universe, and in the case of a minimal deformation of DBI necessary for avoiding the domain wall problem in cosmology. However, we prove that DBI remains shock free in the hyperbolic case in all these physically relevant situations. This strongly suggests that caustics can form on planar domain walls only due to the loss of hyperbolicity, and they have a cusp profile. We demonstrate, how the non-trivial structure of DBI characteristics beyond the 2D flat spacetime setup uncovered in this work can significantly affect cusp formation.

### [49] [Discrete symmetries of Feynman integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08332)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在全面研究费曼积分族的一类离散对称性，这些对称性定义为将族的不同扇区相互映射的变量仿射变换。研究动机在于理解这些对称性的数学结构及其对费曼积分计算的影响。

Method: 方法包括：证明这些变换总是编码为费曼参数的置换，与定义费曼积分的积分表示无关；在圈动量空间中构造编码此类置换的仿射映射；将对称性自然嵌入扭上同调理论框架。

Result: 主要结果包括：证明了周期和交配对在对称变换下不变；获得了固定扇区内对称性作用下扭上同调群表示的分解；发现该表示的字符与相应不动点集的欧拉特征成正比；推导了存在非平凡对称群时给定扇区主积分数量的公式。

Conclusion: 研究结合了图论、群论和代数拓扑等数学工具，成功将费曼积分的离散对称性系统化。作为应用，获得了任意非零质量配置下四圈以内香蕉积分的主积分数量，展示了理论框架的实际计算价值。

Abstract: We perform a comprehensive study of a certain class of discrete symmetries of families of Feynman integrals, defined as affine changes of variables that map different sectors of the family into each other. We show that these transformations are always encoded into permutations of the Feynman parameters that relate the Lee-Pomeransky polynomials of the two sectors, irrespective of the integral representation used to define the Feynman integrals. We then construct an affine map in loop-momentum space that encodes such a permutation. We also show that these symmetries can be naturally embedded into the framework of twisted cohomology theories, and the period and intersection parings are invariant under the symmetry transformations. If we focus on symmetries within a fixed sector, we obtain a group acting on the twisted cohomology group, and we study the decomposition of this action into irreducible representations. One of our main mathematical results is that the character of this representation is proportional to the Euler characteristic of the corresponding fixed-point set. We then study the implications for Feynman integrals, in particular for the intersection matrix in a canonical basis. We also present a formula for the number of master integrals in a given sector in the presence of a non-trivial symmetry group in terms of the Euler characteristics of fixed-point sets. As an application, we obtain the numbers of master integrals for banana integrals with up to four loops for arbitrary configurations of non-zero masses. In order to achieve our results, we had to combine tools from various different areas of mathematics, including graph theory, group theory and algebraic topology.

</details>


### [50] [Lifshitz-like Magnetic Black Branes: Third Law of Thermodynamics and the Null Energy Condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08431)
*Irina Ya. Aref'eva,Kristina Rannu,Viktor Zlobin*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在通过势重构方法解析求解爱因斯坦-伸缩子-麦克斯韦模型，并系统研究黑洞解中零能条件与热力学第三定律之间的关系。通过获得显式的黑洞化函数（blackening function），而非仅依赖数值数据，能够深入探讨热力学第三定律的有效性。

Method: 开发了基于势重构方法的程序，以积分形式求解爱因斯坦-伸缩子-麦克斯韦模型。将此方法应用于三个具体模型：模型I（5维含两个麦克斯韦场，各向异性由高斯函数和Lifshitz函数描述）；模型II（5维模型，各向异性由两个Lifshitz参数参数化）；模型III（6维含一个2-形式场和一个3-形式场，度规由两个Lifshitz参数参数化）。

Result: 对于模型I和II，同时满足零能条件和热力学第三定律的参数区域显示两者之间没有相关性。相反，对于模型III，零能条件的有效性意味着热力学第三定律的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了不同维度与场构型下，零能条件与热力学第三定律之间关系的差异性：在5维模型中两者无关联，而在6维模型中前者蕴含后者。这为理解引力理论中能量条件与热力学定律的深层联系提供了新见解。

Abstract: We develop a procedure to solve Einstein-dilaton-Maxwell models in quadratures using the potential reconstruction approach. We then apply this procedure to three distinct models, examining both the null energy condition (NEC) and the validity of the third law of thermodynamics in each case. The explicit knowledge of the blackening function -- as opposed to relying solely on numerical data -- allows us to discuss the validity of the third law in detail. The three models considered are: (I) a 5D model with two Maxwell fields, featuring anisotropy specified by a Gaussian function and a Lifshitz function; (II) the same 5D model as in (I), but with anisotropy parametrized by two Lifshitz parameters; and (III) a 6D model with one 2-form and one 3-form field, with the metric parametrized by two Lifshitz parameters. We show that for models I and II the parameter regions, where both the NEC and the third law are satisfied, exhibit no correlation between the two conditions. In contrast, for model III the validity of the NEC implies the validity of the third law.

### [51] [Lifshitz-like black branes in arbitrary dimensions and the third law of thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08441)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功构建了任意维度D的精确各向异性黑洞膜解，包含各向异性标度指数和一般扭曲因子（包括高斯形式）。发现在特定参数范围内，两个模型都满足熵随温度趋零而消失的热力学第三定律，但对于特定扭曲因子或耦合常数，熵温关系呈现非单调或多值行为。

Abstract: In this paper we present a systematic construction of an(isotropic) black brane solutions in arbitrary spacetime dimensions $D$ in particular, with Lifshitz-like asymptotics. Two distinct holographic models are considered. The first model involves a scalar field with a potential coupled to two Maxwell fields, allowing for both electric and magnetic charges. The second model includes a scalar field, a Maxwell field, and a three-form field strength of a Kalb-Ramond field. For each model, exact solutions for the metric, scalar field, gauge fields, and coupling functions are derived, incorporating anisotropic scaling exponents and general warp factors, including Gaussian forms. The results generalize previously known five-dimensional anisotropic black brane solutions to arbitrary dimensions. We show that the third law of thermodynamics, which requires entropy to vanish as temperature approaches zero, is satisfied for a certain range of parameters in both models. However, for specific warp factors or coupling constants, the entropy-temperature relation exhibits non-monotonic or multi-valued behavior, suggesting the possibility of phase transitions and a violation of the third law.

### [52] [$\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric Field Theories at Finite Temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08459)
*Oleksandr Diatlyk,Andrei Katsevich,Fedor K. Popov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究PT对称（PT-symmetric）标量场理论在纯虚耦合下的热性质，旨在理解自由能、热质量和单点函数如何对应二维共形场论（Conformal Field Theories）的算符维度和三点函数。

Method: 引入"热正规序（thermal normal-ordering）"方案重整化红外发散贡献，建立系统的ε展开（ε-expansion）框架，计算立方和五次O(N)模型的自由能、热质量和单点函数，并与二维非幺正最小模型（non-unitary minimal models）的精确结果比较。

Result: 成功计算了立方和五次O(N)模型的自由能密度、热质量和单点函数，在二维情况下与M(2,5)和M(3,8)_D模型的精确结果进行了比较，并采用双侧帕德外推（two-sided Padé extrapolations）获得了三维、四维和五维的热自由能估计值。

Conclusion: 通过热正规序方案有效解决了PT对称标量场理论中的红外发散问题，建立了系统的ε展开框架，为研究非幺正共形场论的热性质提供了有效计算方法，并在不同维度下获得了可靠的热自由能估计。

Abstract: We investigate the thermal properties of $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric scalar field theories with purely imaginary couplings. The free energy governs the asymptotic density of states, providing an effective measure of the number of degrees of freedom, while thermal masses and one-point functions provide predictions for operator dimensions and three-point functions in the corresponding $d=2$ Conformal Field Theories. Naive finite-temperature perturbation theory near upper critical dimensions is spoiled by infrared divergences. To remove these divergences, we introduce a ''thermal normal-ordering'' scheme that resums these contributions and yields a systematic $ε$-expansion. This framework allows us to compute the free energy, thermal masses, and one-point functions in the cubic and quintic $O(N)$ models. We compare the thermal free energy density, thermal masses, and one-point function in two dimensions with exact results derived from the proposed Ginzburg-Landau descriptions of the non-unitary minimal models $M(2,5)$ and $M(3,8)_D$. Eventually, we employ two-sided Padé extrapolations to obtain estimates for the thermal free energy in $d=3,4,5$.

### [53] [On Carrollian Loop Amplitudes for Gauge Theory and Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08498)
*Vijay Nenmeli,Bin Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究规范理论和引力理论中无质量粒子散射的卡罗尔振幅（Carrollian amplitudes）在圈图层次的性质，包括有限单圈振幅的解析结构、超对称理论中的微分算子表示、eikonal区域的对数行为，以及红外发散因式分解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索无质量粒子在零无限远（null infinity）位置空间的散射振幅——卡罗尔振幅在圈图层次的性质，特别是其在规范理论和引力理论中的解析结构、红外行为以及因子化特性。

Method: 主要采用文献[1]的修正梅林变换（modified Mellin prescription）方法，计算了规范理论和引力理论中的单圈四点卡罗尔振幅，包括平面N=4超杨-米尔斯理论（super Yang-Mills theory）和N=8超引力理论（supergravity）的MHV振幅。

Result: 结果显示规范理论中的有限单圈四点卡罗尔振幅保持类似树图的解析结构；超杨-米尔斯理论的卡罗尔MHV振幅可表示为微分算子作用于树图振幅；eikonal区域引力散射的卡罗尔振幅在卡罗尔时间u上呈现对数行为；红外发散可通过自然因子化获得红外安全定义。

Conclusion: 卡罗尔振幅在圈图层次展现出丰富的解析结构，包括微分算子表示、对数行为等新特征；不同理论中的红外发散可通过自然因子化处理，为这类振幅提供了红外安全的定义框架。

Abstract: Carrollian amplitudes are scattering amplitudes of massless particles written in position space at null infinity. We study various aspects of Carrollian amplitudes for gauge theory and gravity at loop level using primarily the modified Mellin prescription of [1]. Finite one-loop four-point Carrollian amplitudes in gauge theory are shown to maintain an analytic structure similar to tree level results. We compute the one-loop four-point Carrollian MHV amplitudes in planar $N=4$ super Yang-Mills theory, which are expressed as differential operators acting on tree level Carrollian amplitudes. This result is generalized to all loop orders using the Bern-Dixon-Smirnov (BDS) formula. Similar structures are observed at one-loop for Carrollian MHV amplitudes in $N=8$ supergravity. We next consider $2\to 2$ scattering of massless scalars via gravitational interactions in the eikonal regime and show that the corresponding Carrollian amplitudes exhibit logarithmic behavior in the `Carroll time' $u$. We compute the discontinuities of these Carrollian amplitudes up to $O(G^3)$ and show that they are descendants of Carrollian Born amplitudes. We observe similar logarithmic behavior in Carrollian amplitudes associated with the one-loop scalar box diagram. The dependence of this amplitude on dual scaling dimensions also differs from standard tree level results. Finally, we further study the infrared (IR) divergences of Carrollian amplitudes in massless scalar QED, gravity, and Yang-Mills theory. We show that Carrollian amplitudes in these theories naturally factorize, allowing us to provide an IR-safe definition for these objects.

</details>


### [54] [Beyond Discontinuities: Cosmological WFCs from the Supersymmetric Orthogonal Grassmannian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08512)
*Yu-tin Huang,Chia-Kai Kuo,Yohan Liu,Jiajie Mei*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文展示了如何通过$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称性扩展正交格拉斯曼流形（orthogonal Grassmannian）构造，以完整描述守恒流波函数系数（WFCs），而非仅其不连续部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 波函数系数（WFCs）可用正交格拉斯曼流形描述，但守恒流的WFCs满足非齐次Ward恒等式，导致格拉斯曼构造仅能重现其不连续部分（discontinuities），需要解决这一局限性。

Method: 利用$\mathcal{N}=2$超对称性关联自旋与非自旋WFCs，通过在格拉斯曼公式中添加运动学预因子（kinematic prefactor）来捕获完整WFCs，并基于超对称不变量解释格拉斯曼公式的正负分支。

Result: $\mathcal{N}=2$超对称性使格拉斯曼公式能够完整描述守恒流WFCs，其正负分支对应不同的超对称不变量，并在平直空间极限下产生不同的螺旋度振幅（helicity amplitudes）。

Conclusion: 超对称性为格拉斯曼构造提供了必要的补充结构，使其能够处理非齐次Ward恒等式，从而完整描述守恒流波函数系数，并揭示了格拉斯曼分支与超对称不变量之间的深层联系。

Abstract: Recently, it has been shown that wave function coefficients (WFCs) admit a natural description in terms of the orthogonal Grassmannian, furnishing homogeneous solutions to the three-dimensional conformal Ward identities in spinor-helicity variables. This, however, presents a challenge for WFCs of conserved currents, which satisfy inhomogeneous Ward identities; correspondingly, the Grassmannian construction reproduces only their \textit{discontinuities}. In this paper, we show that $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetry, by relating spinning and non-spinning WFCs, leads to a Grassmannian formula augmented by a kinematic prefactor that captures the full WFC. Moreover, we show that the positive and negative branches of the Grassmannian formula admit a natural interpretation in terms of supersymmetric invariants, and give rise to distinct helicity amplitudes in the flat-space limit.

</details>

### [55] [Biogenic bubbles enable microbial escape from physical confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07768)
*Babak Vajdi Hokmabad,Thomas Appleford,Hao Nghi Luu,Meera Ramaswamy,Maziyar Jalaal,Sujit S. Datta*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非运动微生物广泛存在于土壤、沉积物等物理限制环境中，但其在这些环境中的扩散机制尚不清楚。研究旨在探索非运动微生物在受限环境中如何实现长距离扩散。

Method: 使用酵母作为模型生物，研究其在透明屈服应力基质（yield-stress matrix）中的行为。通过观察发酵过程产生的溶解CO₂过饱和现象，分析生物气泡（biogenic bubbles）的成核、生长和上升机制。

Result: 发酵驱动溶解CO₂过饱和，成核产生生物气泡，这些气泡生长、屈服基质并上升，通过流体力学夹带细胞垂直移动。连续气泡成核形成持久柱状菌落，多个菌落通过发酵副产物相互作用，形成自维持的导管网络。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了微生物扩散的第三种模式——代谢驱动活性物质（Metabolically Driven Active Matter），其中代谢副产物重塑限制环境的物理景观，驱动群体尺度运动。这一发现对生态学、环境科学和生物技术具有重要意义。

Abstract: Immotile microbes inhabit nearly every environment on Earth, from soils and sediments to food matrices -- yet how they disperse through these physically confining environments is poorly understood. Here, we show that immotile microbial colonies confined in a model transparent yield-stress matrix can achieve long-range dispersal by harnessing their own metabolism. Using yeast as a model organism, we find that fermentation drives dissolved CO$_2$ to supersaturation, nucleating biogenic bubbles that grow, yield the matrix, and rise, hydrodynamically entraining cells vertically in their wake. Sequential bubble nucleation sculpts persistent columnar colonies extending far beyond what growth alone permits. Multiple colonies interact via their fermentation byproducts, merging and mixing genetically as they collectively sculpt self-sustaining conduit networks. Our findings reveal a third mode of microbial dispersal, distinct from the canonical mechanisms of motility and growth, with implications for ecology, environmental science, and biotechnology. More broadly, they exemplify a previously unrecognized class of active behavior -- Metabolically Driven Active Matter -- in which metabolic byproducts reshape the physical landscape of confinement to drive population-scale motion.

### [56] [Active Transport as a Mechanism of Microphase Selection in Biomolecular Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08316)
*Le Qiao,Peter Gispert,Lukas S. Stelzl,Friederike Schmid*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立了一个最小扩散-运输模型，通过线性稳定性理论（linear stability theory）和三维模拟进行分析。该模型考虑了相分离蛋白与细胞骨架马达蛋白的随机结合及沿丝状网络的主动再分布。

Result: 模型揭示了在极低的结合/释放分数下，系统从宏观相分离向微相分离（microphase separation）转变。调节马达结合速率b或运输速度可实现凝聚体尺寸的亚线性控制（L ∼ b^{-1/4}），范围从纳米到微米尺度。在非对称细胞骨架环境中，运输不对称性驱动凝聚体形态从球形向圆柱形转变。

Conclusion: 这种独立于热力学参数的机制为凝聚体组织提供了多功能、时空可编程的途径，并为设计具有可调结构的合成活性乳液提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Cells control the size and organization of biomolecular condensates formed by liquid-liquid phase separation (LLPS), but multiple mechanisms likely contribute to this control and remain to be fully elucidated. Here we propose a transport-driven mechanism in which stochastic binding of phase-separating proteins to cytoskeletal motor proteins, followed by active redistribution along filament networks, generates an effective long-range repulsion that arrests coarsening and selects a finite condensate size. A minimal diffusion-transport model, analyzed by linear stability theory and three-dimensional simulations, reveals a transition from macroscopic to microphase separation at remarkably low binding/release fractions, corresponding to minute motor-bound populations. Tuning motor binding rates $b$ or transport velocities enables sublinear control of condensate sizes ($L \sim b^{-1/4}$) from nanometers to micrometers. In anisotropic cytoskeletal environments, transport asymmetry drives morphological transitions from spherical to cylindrical condensates. Operating independently of thermodynamic parameters, this mechanism provides a versatile, spatiotemporally programmable route to condensate organization and informs the design of synthetic active emulsions with tunable architectures.

### [57] [Superradiance enhances and suppresses fermionic pairing based on universal critical scaling rate in two order parameters systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07407)
*Yilun Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于朗道连续相变理论的新范式，用于研究具有两个或多个序参数（order parameters）的复杂系统。通过引入一个通用物理量来量化两个序参数之间的变化率，并以双模拉比模型和1D费米-迪克模型为例，展示了超辐射相变如何调控双自旋配对强度和超导带隙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 与单一序参数系统不同，由两个或多个序参数描述的系统会呈现更复杂、更丰富的相图和临界现象。在双序参数系统中，一个序参数的相变可能影响另一个序参数的强度，这种相互作用机制需要系统研究。

Method: 基于朗道连续相变理论（Landau's theory of continuous phase transitions），从自由能（free energy）的通用公式出发，推导出一个决定两个序参数变化率的通用物理量。以双模拉比模型（two-mode Rabi model）和一维费米-迪克模型（1D Fermi Dicke model）作为验证实例。

Result: 理论分析结果在所选模型中得到了验证，展示了超辐射相变（superradiant phase transition）如何调控双自旋配对强度（two-spin pairing strength）和超导带隙（superconductor band gap）。该方法为量化序参数间的相互作用提供了具体工具。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了研究具有两个或多个序参数的复杂系统的新范式，为通过序参数间的相互作用增强或抑制特定物理效应提供了新途径。该方法具有普适性，可应用于更广泛的复杂系统研究。

Abstract: Distinguished from the system with one order parameter, systems described by two or more order parameters will manifest more complex and much richer phase diagram and critical phenomena. In systems of two order parameters, the phase transition of one order parameter may influence the strength of another. Focus on the Landau's theory of continuous phase transitions, we give a general physcial quantity to decide the changing rate of the two order parameters based on a general formula of free energy. Taking two-mode Rabi model and the 1D Fermi Dicke model as the examples, we verify our analytical results and show how the superradiant phase transition manipulates the two-spin pairing strength and the superconductor band gap. Our work proposes the new paradigm to study the complex systems with two or more order parameters and provides novel avenue to enhancing or suppressing the desired physical effect by such interplay.

</details>


### [58] [Programmable Dynamic Phase Control of a Quasiperiodic Optical Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07631)
*Andrew O. Neely,Cedric C. Wilson,Ryan Everly,Yu Yao,Raffaella Zanetti,Charles D. Brown*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种可编程、动态的二维准周期光学晶格实验方案，实现了相位噪声的显著抑制和高速相位调制，为直接观测和控制准晶体中的量子动力学提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准周期系统（quasiperiodic systems）的量子动力学具有丰富的物理行为，结合了周期性系统中数学上禁止的旋转对称性和缺乏平移对称性下的长程有序。利用量子模拟器（quantum simulator）的新实验探针将为准周期系统的物理提供新见解。

Method: 提出了一种创建可编程、动态的二维准周期光学晶格（quasiperiodic optical lattice）的实验方案，该方案具有高度抑制的相位噪声。通过超冷原子（ultracold atoms）在光学晶格势中的实现，利用构成晶格的单个激光束的灵活性、可调性和纯度，实现对丰富系统的精确控制。

Result: 观察到高达5 kHz频率分量的相位噪声抑制，在DC-60 Hz频段报告了超过70 dB的相位噪声抑制。进一步展示了350 kHz的相位调制带宽，实现了晶格的完全平移和相位控制，包括势的旋转对称性变化，速度超过晶格反冲速度（lattice recoil velocity）。

Conclusion: 该方案通过Floquet engineering开辟了更丰富的可实现系统空间，为直接观测和控制准晶体（quasicrystals）中的量子动力学铺平了道路。

Abstract: The quantum dynamics of quasiperiodic systems display a rich variety of physical behaviors due to the combination of rotational symmetry that is mathematically forbidden in periodic systems, and long-range order despite the lack of translation symmetry. New experimental probes into these dynamics with a quantum simulator, consisting of ultracold atoms in an optical lattice potential, will yield new insights into the physics of quasiperiodic systems. This potential is imbued with the flexibility, tunability, and purity of the individual laser beams that constitute it, allowing for exquisite control over a rich system. Programmable dynamic control over the lattice beam phases opens up an even richer space of achievable systems via Floquet engineering. We thus describe an experimental scheme for creating a programmable, dynamic, two-dimensional (2D) quasiperiodic optical lattice with heavily suppressed phase noise. We observe suppression of phase noise for frequency components up to 5 kHz, and report phase noise suppression of over 70 dB over the DC-60 Hz frequency band. We further demonstrate a phase modulation bandwidth of 350 kHz. This scheme allows for full translational and phasonic control of the lattice, including changes to the rotational symmetry of the potential, at speeds exceeding the lattice recoil velocity, which paves a path towards direct observation and control of quantum dynamics in quasicrystals.

### [59] [Axion-like Particles and Lepton Flavor Violation in Muonic Atoms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07481)
*Girish Kumar,Alexey A. Petrov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了Mu2e实验在简化轴子类粒子（ALP）框架下探测μ⁻e⁻→e⁻e⁻过程的潜力，该过程涉及味破坏耦合和可能的不可见衰变。分析显示，尽管轻ALP能增强该过程，但现有实验约束（特别是Δa_e和μ→3e）严重限制了可观测率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索Mu2e实验探测μ⁻e⁻→e⁻e⁻过程的潜力，这是一个在μ子原子中发生的轻子味破坏过程。该过程在简化轴子类粒子（ALP）框架下进行研究，该框架包含e-μ味破坏耦合和电子味对角赝标量耦合。

Method: 计算了ALP介导的跃迁率贡献，并分析了分支比随媒介粒子质量和原子核电荷数的标度关系。将模型与μ→eγ、μ→3e、μ→eγγ、μ→e+inv、μ子-反μ子转换以及电子和μ子反常磁矩等实验约束进行比较。

Result: 在固定耦合下，分支比随媒介粒子质量减小而增加，并标度为(Z-1)³，有利于重核。Δa_e提供了参数空间最严格的限制之一。应用实验室约束后，铝中μ⁻e⁻→e⁻e⁻的可观测分支比最多为O(10⁻²⁰)，共振区域2m_e<m_a<m_μ-m_e受到更强抑制。

Conclusion: 尽管轻ALP能在固定耦合下参数化增强μ⁻e⁻→e⁻e⁻过程，但现有实验界限（特别是Δa_e、μ→3e、μ→eγ和μ子振荡）严重限制了可观测率。最高可达到的值与接近当前极限的B(μ→3e)密切相关，表明即将进行的Mu3e实验将探索与该μ子原子信号相关的最有前景区域。

Abstract: We explore the potential of the Mu2e experiment to probe the lepton-flavor-violating process $μ^- e^- \to e^- e^-$ in a muonic atom within a simplified axion-like particle (ALP) framework featuring flavor-violating $e$-$μ$ couplings and a flavor-diagonal pseudoscalar coupling to electrons, which also allows for possible invisible ALP decays into a dark sector. We compute the ALP-mediated contribution to the transition rate and show that, at fixed couplings, the branching ratio increases for lighter mediators and scales as $(Z-1)^3$, favoring heavier nuclei. We compare the model against constraints from $μ\to eγ$, $μ\to 3e$, $μ\to eγγ$, $μ\to e+\mathrm{inv}$, and muonium-antimuonium conversion, as well as from the anomalous magnetic moments of the electron and muon. Additional astrophysical and beam-dump limits on the electron coupling are also discussed. A key result is that $Δa_e$ provides one of the most stringent probes of the parameter space and, in the global scan, excludes the largest fraction of sampled points. After applying the laboratory constraints used in the scan, the viable branching ratio for $μ^- e^- \to e^- e^-$ in aluminum drops to at most $\mathcal{O}(10^{-20})$, while the resonant region $2m_e<m_a<m_μ-m_e$ is much more heavily suppressed. The highest achievable values are closely tied to $\mathcal{B}(μ\to 3e)$ near its current limit, indicating that the upcoming Mu3e experiment will explore the most promising region relevant for this muonic-atom signal. Our analysis shows that, although a light ALP can parametrically enhance $μ^- e^- \to e^- e^-$ at fixed couplings, existing bounds -- especially $Δa_e$, $μ\to 3e$, $μ\to eγ$, and muonium oscillations -- severely limit the observable rate.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功构建了求解DGLAP类型积分微分方程的算法，该算法能够在耦合常数α的所有阶次上运行。算法显著简化了复平面围道积分的计算过程，相比现有方法更为简洁高效。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于复分析的新算法，能够有效求解DGLAP类型积分微分方程，特别是在处理耦合常数α的所有阶次时。算法通过简化复平面围道积分的计算，提供了比现有方法更优的解决方案。

Abstract: We propose an algorithm to find a solution to an integro-differential equation of the DGLAP type for all the orders in the running coupling $α$ with splitting functions given at a fixed order in $α.$ Complex analysis is significantly used in the construction of the algorithm, we found a simpler way to calculate the involved integrals over contours in the complex planes than by any of the methods known at present.

### [61] [$\bar B\to D^{(*)}\ell\bar ν$ Branching Ratios and Evidence for Isospin Breaking in $Υ(4S)$ Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08391)
*Martin Jung,Stefan Schacht*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于$\bar B\to D^{(*)}\ell\bar ν$衰变测量$R^{\pm0}$比值的新方法，获得了迄今为止单通道最精确的$R^{\pm0}$值，并发现$Υ(4S)$衰变中存在同位旋破坏（isospin violation）的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于精确测定$R^{\pm0}=\mathcal B(Υ(4S)\to B^+B^-)/\mathcal B(Υ(4S)\to B^0\bar B^0)$比值，这对于理解$Υ(4S)$衰变中的同位旋破坏效应至关重要。同时需要解决现有文献中$\bar B\to D^{(*)}\ell\bar ν$分支分数（branching fractions）分析的不一致性，以缓解$V_{cb}$谜题（$V_{cb}$ puzzle）。

Method: 方法基于$\bar B\to D^{(*)}\ell\bar ν$衰变模式，对可用数据进行综合分析，并行提取分支分数和$R^{\pm0}$信息，并提供它们的相关性以避免在唯象分析（phenomenological analyses）中重复使用信息。通过纠正旧分析中的处理不一致性，并在可能情况下修正d'Agostini偏差（d'Agostini bias）。

Result: 获得了迄今为止单通道最精确的$R^{\pm0}$值，与1的差异约为2σ。与其他通道先前可用测定的组合得到$R^{\pm0}=1.062(19)$，构成了$Υ(4S)$衰变中同位旋破坏的证据。$\bar B\to D^{(*)}\ell\bar ν$分支分数结果比文献平均值高出最多1.6σ，从而减少了$V_{cb}$谜题。

Conclusion: 结论表明$Υ(4S)$衰变中存在同位旋破坏效应，在实验和唯象分析中必须考虑这一效应。通过纠正分析不一致性和偏差，提高了分支分数测量的准确性，有助于缓解$V_{cb}$谜题。

Abstract: We introduce a new method for the determination of the ratio of production fractions $R^{\pm0}=\mathcal B(Υ(4S)\to B^+B^-)/\mathcal B(Υ(4S)\to B^0\bar B^0)$ based on $\bar B\to D^{(*)}\ell\bar ν$ decays. Given the importance of these modes, we perform a comprehensive analysis of the available data, extracting the information on their branching fractions and \Rpmz in parallel and providing their correlations in order to avoid double-use of this information in phenomenological analyses. We obtain the most precise value for $R^{\pm0}$ from a single channel so far, about 2$σ$ from unity. The combination with previously available determinations from other channels yields $R^{\pm0}=1.062(19)$, constituting evidence for isospin violation in $Υ(4S)$ decays. This demonstrates the necessity to take this effect into account in experimental and phenomenological analyses. The results for the $\bar B\to D^{(*)}\ell\bar ν$ branching fractions are up to $1.6σ$ larger compared to averages available in the literature, owing to the removal of overlooked inconsistencies in the treatment of older analyses and correcting for d'Agostini bias where possible, thereby reducing the $V_{cb}$ puzzle.

</details>


### [62] [Constraining Ultralight Scalar Dark Matter in the Galactic Center with the S2 Orbit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08053)
*Jiang-Chuan Yu,Yan Cao,Lijing Shao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 考虑实标量场φ与标准模型粒子之间的线性和二次耦合，分析两种代表性ULDM结构：标量引力原子（scalar gravitational atom）和球状孤子（spherical soliton）。利用S2星观测到的近日点进动率（periastron precession rate）来约束ULDM参数。

Result: 二次耦合诱导非振荡扰动，导致长期轨道演化。对于引力原子|211⟩态，在m∼10⁻¹⁸ eV处约束ULDM与Sgr A*的质量比β≲10⁻³；对于延伸至∼0.2 pc的球状孤子，在m∼3×10⁻²⁰ eV处约束β≲1。二次耦合常数限制在质量范围10⁻²⁰ eV≲m≲10⁻¹⁸ eV内超越现有界限。

Conclusion: 银河系中心S星轨道动力学为探测超轻暗物质提供了有力手段，获得的二次耦合常数约束在特定质量范围内优于现有界限，展示了该方法的探测潜力。

Abstract: The dense environment of our Galactic Center (GC) offers a unique laboratory for probing ultralight dark matter (ULDM). We explore the prospect of detecting a scalar ULDM field through its effects on the orbital dynamics of S-stars around the supermassive black hole in the GC, Sgr A$^*$. We consider both linear and quadratic couplings between the real scalar field $φ$ and Standard Model particles, and analyze two representative ULDM structures: the scalar gravitational atom and the spherical soliton. We find that quadratic coupling induces a non-oscillatory perturbation, leading to a long-term secular orbital evolution. We use the observed periastron precession rate of S2 star to put stringent constraints on the total ULDM mass in the GC and the quadratic coupling constant. For the gravitational atom $|211\rangle$ state, we constrain the mass ratio of ULDM to Sgr A$^*$ to $β\lesssim 10^{-3}$ at $m \sim 10^{-18}$ eV, and for the spherical soliton which extends to $\sim 0.2\,$pc, the mass ratio is limited to $β\lesssim 1$ at $m \sim 3\times10^{-20}$ eV. Notably, the resulting limits on the quadratic coupling constant surpass current bounds in the mass range $10^{-20} \,\text{eV} \lesssim m \lesssim 10^{-18}$ eV.

### [63] [Scalars at the Cosmological Collider: Full Shapes of Tree Diagrams and Bispectrum Searches using Planck Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07434)
*Soubhik Kumar,Qianshu Lu,Zhong-Zhi Xianyu,Yisong Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 宇宙学对撞机（Cosmological Collider）通过原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）探测暴胀时期的高能物理，本文对三类交换过程进行了统一计算，并用Planck数据进行了搜索，发现微弱证据支持特定参数空间存在非高斯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学对撞机（Cosmological Collider）为探测极高能量下的粒子谱和基本相互作用提供了独特机会，通过大质量粒子衰变产生的非解析振荡性原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）可以揭示暴胀时期的高能物理。

Method: 对三类交换过程（'single exchange'、'double exchange'、'triple exchange'）进行统一计算，推导出在整个运动学空间有效的双谱（bispectrum）显式形状函数，并使用Planck数据进行搜索分析。

Result: 在Planck数据中未发现非高斯性（NG）的明确证据，但在考虑标量化学势（scalar chemical potential）机制扩展后，在参数空间$ω- M \simeq 3H$处发现了全局1.5$σ$水平的非零非高斯性证据。

Conclusion: 宇宙学对撞机信号在标准场景中受到指数抑制，但通过标量化学势等机制可以增强信号，使得探测暴胀时期$M\gg H$的大质量粒子成为可能，为高能物理探测提供了新途径。

Abstract: The Cosmological Collider (CC) provides a unique opportunity to probe the particle spectrum and fundamental interactions at extremely high energies. Massive particles, via their decay into inflaton quanta, can induce a non-analytic, oscillatory, primordial non-Gaussianity (NG), including the bispectrum. At tree level, three classes of such processes contribute to the bispectrum: 'single exchange', 'double exchange', and 'triple exchange', depending on the number of massive particle propagators. We provide a unified evaluation of all three diagrams and derive the explicit shape functions for the bispectrum, valid across the entire kinematic space. We perform a search for these three processes with the Planck data, finding no evidence for NG. We also consider simple extensions of the minimal scenario that can counter the exponential suppression of the non-analytic signature, and produce on-shell particles with masses $M\gg H$, the Hubble scale during inflation. In particular, we focus on the 'scalar chemical potential' mechanism and extend our previous search to a wider range of chemical potential ($ω$) and $M$, finding global 1.5$σ$ evidence for non-zero NG for the parameter space $ω- M \simeq 3H$.

### [64] [Gauged Q-balls in flat potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07454)
*Julian Heeck,Yu Zhi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了平坦势能（flat potentials）中的规范Q-球（gauged Q-balls），这类势能常见于超对称模型（supersymmetric models）。研究发现，尽管全局Q-球（global Q-balls）在平坦势能中与Coleman的Q-球有本质差异，但其规范版本却表现出惊人的相似性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索平坦势能中的规范Q-球，这类势能常见于超对称模型。先前研究主要关注满足Coleman薄壁判据（Coleman's thin-wall criterion）的标量势能，而对平坦势能中的规范Q-球研究不足。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）分析平坦势能中的规范Q-球；2）提供这些孤子（solitons）的解析近似；3）与数值解进行比较；4）研究Proca Q-球（即赋予规范玻色子质量），这连接了全局和规范两种情况。

Result: 研究发现，尽管全局Q-球在平坦势能中与Coleman的Q-球有本质差异，但规范Q-球在平坦势能中却表现出惊人的相似性。研究提供了这些孤子的解析近似，并与数值解进行了比较验证。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，平坦势能中的规范Q-球与Coleman的Q-球具有显著相似性，尽管相应的全局Q-球存在本质差异。同时，Proca Q-球的研究揭示了全局和规范情况之间的连续过渡。

Abstract: Q-balls are large bound-state systems of scalar particles, described classically through localized solutions of the equations of motion. Promoting the required stabilizing $U(1)$ symmetry to a gauge symmetry leads to gauged Q-balls, which cannot grow beyond some maximal size and charge on account of the repulsive gauge interactions. These gauged Q-balls have been studied extensively for scalar potentials that satisfy Coleman's thin-wall criterion; here, we explore gauged Q-balls in flat potentials, which often occur in supersymmetric models. Even though global Q-balls in flat potentials are qualitatively different from Coleman's Q-balls, we find that the gauged versions are remarkably similar. We provide analytic approximations for these solitons and compare to numerical solutions. In addition, we study Proca Q-balls, i.e. make the gauge bosons massive, which interpolates between the global and gauged cases.

</details>


### [65] [Forward trijet production in proton-nucleus collisions: gluon initiated channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07509)
*Paul Caucal,Marcos Guerrero Morales,Farid Salazar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在领头阶（leading order）计算了质子-原子核碰撞中胶子引发通道的前向三喷注（forward trijet）产生微分截面，采用色玻璃凝聚（CGC）有效理论，首次观察到四胶子顶点拓扑结构与瞬时贡献相似的结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究质子-原子核碰撞中胶子引发通道的前向三喷注产生微分截面，验证稀密混合形式（dilute-dense hybrid formalism）在一圈阶（one-loop order）的有效性，为质子-原子核碰撞中双喷注/双强子产生的完整次领头阶（next-to-leading order）计算提供关键要素。

Method: 采用色玻璃凝聚（Color Glass Condensate, CGC）有效理论，在稀密近似（dilute-dense approximation）下进行计算，使用夸克和胶子传播子与小x背景胶子场相互作用的有效顶点，并运用协变微扰理论（covariant perturbation theory）方法。

Result: 结果表示为类光威尔逊线（light-like Wilson lines）的多部分子颜色关联子（multiparton color correlators）与微扰冲击因子（perturbative impact factors）的卷积，以紧凑表达式组织；首次发现四胶子顶点拓扑结构遵循与瞬时贡献相似的结构；积分终态实胶子时，快度发散（rapidity divergence）贡献于领头阶颜色关联子的JIMWLK实部，而共线发散（collinear divergence）贡献于初态胶子部分子分布函数和终态碎裂函数（fragmentation functions）的演化。

Conclusion: 这些结果验证了一圈阶的稀密混合形式，是质子-原子核碰撞中双喷注/双强子产生完整次领头阶计算的关键要素，为理解高能碰撞中的多部分子动力学提供了重要理论框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we present the results for the forward trijet production differential cross section in the gluon initiated channel at leading order in proton-nucleus collisions. The calculations are carried out within the Color Glass Condensate (CGC) effective theory, and in the dilute-dense approximation, using effective vertices for the quark and gluon propagators interacting with the small-$x$ background gluon field. We employ the covariant perturbation theory approach and disentangle the amplitudes into regular and instantaneous contributions. Our results are expressed as convolutions of multiparton color correlators of light-like Wilson lines and perturbative impact factors, organized in compact expressions in terms of the ``bare" topologies of the contributing diagrams. The gluon initiated channel receives contributions from a $q\bar{q}g$ and a $ggg$ final state. Interestingly, when considering the $ggg$ final state, we observe, for the first time, that the four-gluon vertex topology follows a structure similar to the instantaneous contributions. Furthermore, when integrating (one of) the real gluon(s) in the final state, we identify that: i) the rapidity divergence contributes to the real part of JIMWLK of the leading-order color correlator; and ii) the collinear divergence contribute to the evolution of initial-state gluon parton distribution function, and final state fragmentation functions. These results validate the dilute-dense hybrid formalism at one-loop order, and are key ingredients towards the complete next-to-leading order calculation of dijet/dihadron production in proton--nucleus collisions.

</details>


### [66] [Memory effect on the heavy quark dynamics in hot QCD matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07982)
*Jai Prakash,Ling Hai Li,Ying Shan Zhao,Yifeng Sun*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在广义朗之万方程框架下研究了记忆效应对重夸克动力学的影响，通过分数阶微分方程生成具有幂律衰减的时间相关热噪声，分析了记忆对动量关联、平均平方动量演化、平均平方位移和平均动能的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究记忆效应对夸克胶子等离子体中重夸克动力学的影响，特别是时间相关热噪声如何改变重夸克在介质中的输运行为。

Method: 采用广义朗之万方程框架，通过分数阶微分方程生成具有幂律衰减的时间相关热噪声，使用Caputo分数阶导数（order parameter $ν$）进行公式化。

Result: 计算表明时间相关热噪声显著影响重夸克动力学，具体体现在动量关联、平均平方动量时间演化、平均平方位移和平均动能等物理量上，并对重夸克横向动量分布的高阶归一化中心矩产生重要影响。

Conclusion: 时间相关热噪声对夸克胶子等离子体中的重夸克动力学具有实质性影响，记忆效应通过分数阶导数描述的幂律衰减噪声显著改变了重夸克的输运特性。

Abstract: We study the heavy quark dynamics in the presence of memory within the framework of a generalized Langevin equation. Time correlated thermal noise with power-law decay is generated by a fractional differential equation, formulated using the Caputo fractional derivative with order parameter $ν$. The effect of memory is calculated through the momentum correlation, the time evolution of the average squared momentum, the average squared displacement, and the average kinetic energy. The effect of memory is further studied for the higher normalised central moments of the heavy quark transverse-momentum distribution. The results indicate that time correlated thermal noise substantially influences heavy quark dynamics in the quark gluon plasma.

Abstract: Dynamic control of visible light is crucial for technologies such as holographic displays and adaptive optics. Passive metasurfaces can shape wavefronts at the subwavelength scale and active metasurfaces promise to extend this functionality into the temporal domain. However, existing metasurfaces for dynamic phase manipulation typically cannot deliver phase modulation across a broad range without causing variations in the scattering amplitude. Here, we use an inverse-design pipeline to numerically demonstrate a hybrid-2D excitonic metasurface platform offering independent amplitude and phase control in the visible regime. Harnessing the gate-tunable excitonic response of monolayer WS2 retrieved from experiments, we design a pi-phase modulator with a uniform amplitude profile. Adding a second tunable monolayer, we achieve independent control of the amplitude and phase over the full 0-2pi phase range, which we leverage for a reconfigurable beam-steering metadevice. Our results demonstrate how hybrid-2D excitonic metasurfaces enable electrically tunable wavefront shaping in the visible regime.

Method: 研究建立了新的BSW读出系统，并与现有MRR平台并行运行，确保在几乎相同的实验条件下进行检测。两种传感器均用多种SARS-CoV-2刺突蛋白（Spike）和核衣壳蛋白（Nucleocapsid）变体进行功能化，以捕获特异性宿主抗体。

Conclusion: 本研究证实BSW和MRR技术均为强大、低成本的候选技术，适用于下一代临床诊断和血清学监测。两种无标记光学生物传感平台在SARS-CoV-2抗体检测方面表现出优异的性能，为精准医疗和流行病监测提供了可靠的技术选择。

Abstract: This study presents a rigorous comparative analysis of two label-free optical biosensing platforms, Bloch surface wave (BSW) and microring resonator (MRR), for the detection of SARS-CoV-2 antibodies in human serum. The results demonstrate that both platforms provide rapid, quantitative, and sensitive detection of anti-Spike and anti-Nucleocapsid antibodies without the need for secondary labels. ### [69] [Experimental Evidence of Thermal Capillary Waves Excitation on a Microsphere Surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08255)
*Abhishek Sureshkumar,Georges Perin,Julien Lapeyre,Rozenn Bernard,Kelig Terrien,Bertrand Dudoux,Adil Haboucha,Hélène Ollivier,Yannick Dumeige,Stéphane Trebaol*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了微球谐振器中表面散射损耗的根本来源是热激发的毛细波（thermally excited capillary waves），而非传统认为的制造缺陷。通过高分辨率原子力显微镜和统计分析，研究证实了亚纳米级冻结毛细波的存在，为设计超高Q值微球谐振器提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回音壁模式（Whispering-gallery-mode, WGM）微球谐振器在短波长应用中面临散射诱导光学损耗的根本限制，这制约了可实现的品质因子（Q-factor）。虽然表面粗糙度被认为是主要损耗来源，但其物理起源一直不明确，传统理解将其归因于不可避免的制造缺陷。

Method: 研究采用高分辨率原子力显微镜（atomic force microscopy, AFM）结合严格的统计分析，在亚纳米水平上定量识别了冻结毛细波（frozen capillary fluctuations）的特征信号。实验提取的粗糙度参数与基于毛细波理论（capillary wave theory）的理论预测进行了对比。

Result: 实验结果表明，热激发的毛细波是微球腔中散射损耗的根本来源。提取的粗糙度参数与毛细波理论的理论预测高度一致，证实了冻结毛细波的存在。这些发现从根本上修正了当前对表面散射损耗的解释，确立了热力学波动（thermodynamic fluctuations）而非制造缺陷作为限制粗糙度的机制。

Conclusion: 通过识别冻结毛细波作为限制因素，该工作为通过制造管理策略设计超高Q值微球谐振器开辟了新途径，特别是在散射损耗最为严重的可见光和紫外光子学（visible- and ultraviolet-photonic）应用中。研究从根本上修正了对表面散射损耗的现有理解。

Abstract: Whispering-gallery-mode (WGM) microsphere resonators have emerged as a versatile platform across various photonic applications. Despite significant progress, their performance at short wavelengths is fundamentally limited by scattering-induced optical losses that restrict achievable quality factors (Q-factor). Although surface roughness has long been recognised as the leading cause of these losses, its physical origin has remained unclear, with current understanding attributing it to unavoidable fabrication imperfections. Here, we show that thermally excited capillary waves are the fundamental source of scattering losses in microsphere cavities. Using high-resolution atomic force microscopy (AFM) combined with rigorous statistical analysis, we quantitatively identify the characteristic signatures of frozen capillary fluctuations at the sub-nanometre level. The experimentally extracted roughness parameters show close agreement with theoretical predictions based on capillary wave theory. These findings fundamentally revise the prevailing interpretation of surface scattering losses and establish thermodynamic fluctuations, rather than fabrication defects, as the limiting roughness mechanism. By identifying frozen capillary waves as the limiting factor, this work opens new pathways for engineering ultra-high-Q microsphere resonators through fabrication management strategies, particularly for visible- and ultraviolet-photonic applications where scattering losses are most severe.

</details>


### [70] [Dynamical Control of Non-Hermitian Coupling Between Sub-Threshold Nanolasers Enables Q-Switched Pulse Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08487)
*Kristian Seegert,Roberto Gajardo,Guillaume Huyet,Fabrice Raineri,Guilhem Madiot*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米光子学（non-Hermitian photonics）为开放系统中光学模式的增益和损耗调控提供了框架，能够控制其光谱和动力学特性。动态调节模式损耗的能力为实现传统上依赖腔Q值调制（Q-factor modulation）的功能（如Q开关）提供了途径。

Method: 采用两个波导耦合的纳米腔（waveguide-coupled nanocavities），在各自激光阈值以下运行，并施加不对称光泵浦（asymmetric optical pumping）。通过瞬态载流子诱导失谐（carrier-induced detuning）改变腔间干涉条件，动态控制集体模式的增益和损耗。使用速率方程模型（rate-equation model）描述载流子动力学与模式耦合的相互作用。

Result: 在磷化铟平台（indium phosphide platform）上的实验显示，在连续波操作中无法高效激光的腔体能够产生光脉冲，其时间特性由载流子动力学决定。当跨越共振条件时，存储的载流子能量以光脉冲形式快速释放。

Conclusion: 非厄米耦合可用于随时间控制有效腔损耗，为集成光子系统中的脉冲生成提供了一条新途径。该方法展示了在纳米光子平台实现传统Q开关功能的可能性。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian photonics provides a framework to engineer the gain and loss of optical modes in open systems, enabling control of their spectral and dynamical properties. In particular, the ability to dynamically tune modal losses offers a route to implement functionalities traditionally relying on cavity Q-factor modulation, such as Q-switching, within nanophotonic platforms. Here, we demonstrate the generation of short optical pulses in a pair of phase-coupled photonic crystal nanolasers exploiting non-Hermitian coupling. Two waveguide-coupled nanocavities are operated below their individual lasing thresholds and subjected to asymmetric optical pumping, such that a transient carrier-induced detuning modifies the interference conditions between them. This dynamically controls the gain and loss of the collective modes, and, upon crossing a resonance condition, leads to the rapid release of stored carrier energy as an optical pulse. A rate-equation model captures the interplay between carrier dynamics and modal coupling and reproduces the observed behavior. Experiments performed on an indium phosphide platform show pulse generation from cavities that do not lase efficiently on their own in continuous-wave operation, with temporal characteristics governed by carrier dynamics. These results indicate that non-Hermitian coupling can be used to control the effective cavity losses in time, providing a route to pulse generation in integrated photonic systems.

### [71] [Fresnel zone plates for reconfigurable atomic waveguides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08518)
*A. M. Pike,A. Dorne,L. Pickering,M. Jamieson,I. T. MacCuish,E. Riis,M. Y. H. Johnson,V. A. Henderson,P. F. Griffin,A. S. Arnold*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型菲涅尔波带片（FZP），结合了传统FZP的高分辨率优势和空间光调制器（SLM）的动态控制能力，实现了可扩展的大面积环形结构生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统菲涅尔波带片（Fresnel zone plates, FZPs）虽然能形成清洁的衍射极限焦点，但具有静态相位剖面；而空间光调制器（spatial light modulators, SLMs）虽能动态控制光束强度和相位，但体积庞大且像素尺寸受限（约10μm）。需要一种结合两者优势的新方法。

Method: 提出了一种新型"最佳结合"型FZP，相当于一个平凸环形透镜（plano-convex donut lens）。该设计将FZP处的光强局部分布和全局相位直接映射到像平面，且可扩展至目前与直接SLM生成不兼容的大面积环形结构。

Result: 同一FZP在不同SLM照明下可生成多种结构：环形和弧形、双环、相位缠绕和环形晶格（或它们的动态组合）。这种平滑且可适应的近场波导结构特别适用于超冷原子的萨尼亚克干涉测量（Sagnac interferometry）。

Conclusion: 新型FZP设计成功结合了传统FZP的高分辨率优势和SLM的动态控制能力，为超冷原子实验中的波导应用提供了理想平台，实现了大面积环形结构的动态生成和相位控制。

Abstract: Fresnel zone plates (FZPs), with patterns of $1\,μ$m resolution, allow the formation of clean, diffraction-limited foci -- but have a static phase profile. Spatial light modulators (SLMs) allow dynamic control of spatial beam intensity and phase -- but are bulky and currently limited to roughly $10\,μ$m pixel sizes and $1\,$Mega-pixel formats. Here, we present a new `best-of-both' kind of FZP, scalable to large area rings currently incompatible with direct SLM generation. It is equivalent to a plano-convex donut lens, whereby light's local intensity and global phase at the FZP map directly onto the image plane. The same FZP under different SLM illumination can generate: rings and arcs, double-rings, phase windings and ring lattices (or dynamic combinations thereof). The smooth and adaptable near-field waveguide this enables will be ideal for Sagnac interferometry with ultracold atoms.

### [72] [Direction-aware topological descriptors for Young's modulus prediction in porous materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08105)
*Rafał Topolnicki,Michał Bogdan,Jakub Malinowski,Bartosz Naskręcki,Maciej Harańczyk,Paweł Dłotko*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种方向感知拓扑数据分析（direction-aware TDA）框架，通过将压缩轴显式嵌入过滤函数来克服传统拓扑描述符无法表示加载方向的问题，显著提高了多孔材料各向异性力学响应的预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拓扑数据分析（TDA）中使用的经典拓扑描述符在空间轴置换下具有不变性，因此无法表示加载方向，而加载方向对于建模各向异性力学响应至关重要。这一局限性阻碍了TDA在方向相关材料特性预测中的应用。

Method: 通过引入方向感知TDA框架，将压缩轴显式嵌入用于计算持久同调（persistent homology）和欧拉特征曲线（Euler characteristic profile）描述符的过滤函数中。该方法在多个涵盖广泛结构各向异性范围的多孔材料数据集上进行验证。

Result: 方向感知描述符比方向无关描述符产生更高的预测精度，且性能增益随各向异性程度系统性增加。即使在名义上各向同性的材料集合中，方向感知描述符仍保持竞争力并经常改善R²值，表明其对超越体各向异性测量的力学相关方向组织具有敏感性。

Conclusion: 方向感知TDA为连接多孔结构与方向相关弹性特性提供了一条通用途径，并激励其在自然存在优先方向的各向异性材料建模问题中的应用。该框架在保持紧凑、可转移表示的同时，接近直接在体素化结构上训练的卷积神经网络的准确性。

Abstract: Classical topological descriptors used in topological data analysis (TDA) are invariant under permutations of spatial axes and therefore cannot represent the loading direction, which is essential for modeling anisotropic mechanical response. Here, this limitation is addressed by introducing a \emph{direction-aware TDA framework} in which the compression axis is explicitly embedded into filtration functions used to compute both persistent homology and Euler characteristic profile descriptors. Across multiple porous-material datasets spanning a broad range of structural anisotropy, direction-aware descriptors yield higher predictive accuracy than their direction-agnostic counterparts, with performance gains that increase systematically with anisotropy. Notably, direction-aware descriptors remain competitive and often improve $R^2$ even for nominally isotropic ensembles, indicating sensitivity to mechanically relevant directional organization beyond bulk anisotropy measures. When used as inputs to gradient-boosted tree models, the proposed descriptors approach the accuracy of convolutional neural networks trained directly on voxelized structures while retaining a compact, transferable representation. The study considers multiple datasets spanning weak to strong anisotropy, enabling systematic validation of direction-aware topology across regimes. Overall, the results establish direction-aware TDA as a general route for linking porous structure to direction-dependent elastic properties and motivate its use in anisotropic materials modeling problems where a preferred direction naturally arises.

</details>

### [73] [Quasicrystal Architected Nanomechanical Resonators via Data-Driven Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07379)
*Kawen Li,Hangjin Cho,Richard Norte,Dongil Shin*

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种从周期性结构转向非周期性结构（特别是准晶体）的纳米机械谐振器设计范式转变，通过数据驱动框架实现了软夹持（soft clamping）和高品质因数（Q_m ~ 10^7），展示了准晶体作为下一代纳米机械谐振器平台的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然界中非周期性有序（aperiodic order）结构（如蝴蝶翅膀和核爆残留物）常表现出对边界和对称约束的敏感性降低。虽然通过声子带隙（phononic stopbands）实现的软夹持已成为实现高品质因数纳米机械谐振器的核心策略，但其实践应用主要局限于周期性声子晶体（phononic crystals），而非周期性结构的潜力尚未充分探索。

Method: 研究引入了一种从周期性结构转向非周期性结构的设计范式转变，特别关注准晶体（quasicrystals, QCs）这一特殊类别。采用数据驱动设计框架（data-driven design framework）来系统识别和利用带隙行为，实现了准晶体架构中的软夹持。

Result: 基于12重对称准晶体的谐振器在MHz频率下实现了品质因数Q_m ~ 10^7和亚纳克级有效质量，对应的力灵敏度达到26.4 aN/√Hz，优于先前报道的二维声子晶体。这证明了准晶体架构中软夹持的可行性。

Conclusion: 准晶体为下一代纳米机械谐振器提供了稳健平台，并开启了超越周期性有序的新设计领域。这些结果确立了准晶体作为实现高性能纳米机械系统的新范式。

Abstract: From butterfly wings to remnants of nuclear detonation, aperiodic order repeatedly emerges in nature, often exhibiting reduced sensitivity to boundaries and symmetry constraints. Inspired by this principle, a paradigm shift is introduced in nanomechanical resonator design from periodic to aperiodic structures, focusing on a special class: quasicrystals (QCs). Although soft clamping enabled by phononic stopbands has become a central strategy for achieving high-$Q_m$ nanomechanical resonators, its practical realization has been largely confined to periodic phononic crystals, where band structure engineering is well established. The potential of aperiodic architectures, however, has remained largely unexplored, owing to their intrinsic complexity and the lack of systematic approaches to identifying and exploiting stopband behavior. Here we demonstrate that soft clamping can be realized in quasicrystal architectures and that high-$Q_m$ nanomechanical resonators can be systematically achieved through a data-driven design framework. As a representative demonstration, the 12-fold QC-based resonator exhibits a quality factor $Q_m \sim 10^7$ and an effective mass of sub-nanograms at MHz frequencies, corresponding to an exceptional force sensitivity of $26.4$~aN/$\sqrt{\text{Hz}}$ compared to previous 2D phononic crystals. These results establish QCs as a robust platform for next-generation nanomechanical resonators and open a new design regime beyond periodic order.

</details>


### [74] [Classification of magnon thermal Hall systems based on U(1) to non-Abelian gauge fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07391)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过引入多重磁子晶格的非阿贝尔SU(N)规范场理论框架，分析其非对易性如何防止贝里曲率抵消；以具有Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用的120°共面反铁磁体作为SU(3)平台的典型实现。

Result: 非阿贝尔规范场的非对易性有效避免了贝里曲率抵消，确保了非零热霍尔响应；建立了包含二维晶格几何和磁结构变体的材料分类表，为识别包括反铁磁体和交变磁体在内的热霍尔材料提供统一指南。

Abstract: Magnon thermal Hall effect in insulating magnets is the manifestation of Berry curvature in magnon bands, which is formulated using the emergent gauge fields that act on magnons as a fictitious magnetic field. In ferromagnets, it is commonly accepted as the outcome of U(1) gauge fields generated by Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions and spin textures, but this mechanism is often suppressed by symmetry-enforced cancellations in many lattice geometries, known as a no-go rule. As a result, antiferromagnetic insulators have long been considered as unfavorable platforms for the effect. We show that antiferromagnets with multiple magnetic sublattices naturally host non-Abelian SU(N) gauge fields in magnon band structures, providing a robust rule-to-go mechanism. The noncommutativity of these gauge fields prevents Berry-curvature cancellation and guarantees a nonvanishing thermal Hall response. As a minimal realization, we demonstrate that a coplanar 120$^{\circ}$ antiferromagnet with Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions constitutes a canonical SU(3) platform for the magnon thermal Hall effect. We provide a table of so-far-known two-dimensional lattice geometries and variants of magnetic structures, along with the corresponding gauge fields, providing a unified guideline for identifying magnetic materials, including antiferromagnets and altermagnets, that host thermal Hall transport.

Abstract: The Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model describes a tight-binding one-dimensional (1D) lattice with alternating nearest-neighbor amplitudes. For this reason, many studies in the area of topological phases of matter often consider the SSH model as a subject for various extensions that give rise to more sophisticated topological phenomena. The purpose of this article is to review, in sufficient detail, existing approaches to extending the SSH model. This includes extensions by increasing the dimensionality of the lattice, enlarging the size of its unit cell, or adding extra terms that represent various physical effects. For each approach, some extended SSH models studied in relevant existing literature are discussed as case studies. Noteworthy properties of such models, which are of topological origin, are further comprehensively elaborated.

### [76] [Mode-Resolved Multiband Ballistic Transport and Conductance Thresholds in Bilayer Graphene Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07504)
*Dan-Na Liu,Jun Zheng,Pierre A. Pantaleon*

Method: 采用完整的四带描述（full four-band description）研究双层石墨烯结中的弹道输运。分析静电门控、层间偏压（interlayer bias）和均匀面内应变（homogeneous in-plane strain）对电子传输的影响，特别关注角分辨输运（angle-resolved transport）特性。

Result: 无应变时，对称性约束在特定入射角抑制传输；层间偏压通过模式混合（mode mixing）解除抑制并打开可调输运带隙（transport gap）。四带描述识别出独特的电导阈值，标志着势垒内上带传播的开始，产生电导斜率变化。均匀应变作为几何控制机制，通过重塑动量空间能带结构重新分布角向传输窗口（angular transmission window）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为解释双层石墨烯中的角分辨输运提供了统一框架，并确立多带弹道输运作为能带结构几何的实际探针。应变在保持基于对称性的解耦同时，将传输抑制条件从正入射移开，为输运控制提供了新机制。

Abstract: We study ballistic transport in bilayer graphene junctions and show how electrostatic gating, interlayer bias, and homogeneous strain provide complementary control over electron transmission. In the absence of strain, transport is governed by symmetry constraints that suppress transmission at specific incidence angles despite the availability of states. An interlayer bias lifts this suppression through mode mixing and opens a tunable transport gap. Within a full four-band description, we identify a distinct conductance threshold that marks the onset of propagation of the upper band inside the barrier. This produces a clear change in the slope of the conductance and serves as an experimentally accessible transport fingerprint of the multiband structure and interlayer coupling. Homogeneous in-plane strain acts as a geometric control mechanism. By reshaping the band structure in momentum space, it redistributes the angular transmission window and suppresses conductance without introducing disorder. Importantly, strain preserves the underlying symmetry-based decoupling responsible for transmission suppression while shifting its condition away from normal incidence. These results provide a unified framework for interpreting angle-resolved transport in bilayer graphene and establish multiband ballistic transport as a practical probe of band-structure geometry.

Method: 采用反射几何测量（reflection-geometry measurements）研究超纯硅（ultrapure silicon）在宽温度范围内的高次谐波产生温度依赖性。同时引入一维原子链模型（one-dimensional atomic-chain model），用随机晶格位移模拟非相干声子涨落。

Abstract: High-harmonic generation in solids has emerged as a powerful probe of ultrafast electron dynamics and lattice motion, and recent theoretical work has suggested that thermally driven lattice fluctuations can act as an effective source of decoherence in the harmonic-generation process. However, a direct experimental link between high-harmonic emission and temperature-driven incoherent phonons has remained unclear. Here, we investigate the temperature dependence of high-harmonic generation in ultrapure silicon using reflection-geometry measurements over a wide temperature range. We observe that the harmonic yield increases significantly with decreasing temperature. To interpret these results, we introduce a one-dimensional atomic-chain model in which finite temperature is represented by random lattice displacements that mimic incoherent phonon fluctuations. The simulations reproduce the magnitude of temperature-dependent change of the harmonic signal and support a picture in which thermally induced lattice disorder enhances electron-hole decoherence, thereby reducing high-harmonic emission. Our results establish incoherent phonons as an important source of decoherence in solid-state high-harmonic generation.

The focus is on the dependence of the skyrmion dynamics on the RE concentration. Parameters of the CoGd ferrimagnet are utilized in the numerical work. ### [79] [Multiscale morphology and contact mechanics of physisorbed Al and Cu nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07646)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Using large-scale molecular dynamics simulations, we investigate the scaling of morphological and contact mechanics properties of Al and Cu nanoparticles (NPs) physisorbed on suspended graphene. The characteristic linear size of a NP ranges from 1 nm to 49 nm, covering a length scale of 1.5 decades. The NPs were obtained using a procedure mimicking thermal dewetting of thin films. Calculations show that NPs with a surface area-to-volume ratio above about 1.8 nm$^{-1}$, or with a linear size under 3-6 nm, behave differently from larger particles. For these smaller NPs, scaling of their total surface area and volume with the linear size can deviate from quadratic and cubic dependencies, respectively. Their mean interfacial separation and relative contact area change rapidly with size, exhibiting substantial variation. In contrast, for larger NPs, these quantities approach the thermodynamic limit. The height distributions of all particles exhibit a narrow spike and a decaying tail, both of which can be fit to Gaussians for larger NPs. In contrast, the interfacial gap distributions are close to a single Gaussian. The height power spectrum density (PSD) heatmaps of the smaller NPs are smeared and do not manifest a clear structure in contrast to the sixfold symmetry of the PSD of the larger ones. The maximum spatial frequency of the hexagonal 2D PSD roughly corresponds to the nearest-neighbor atomic distance of Al and Cu. For larger NPs with diameters of 20-25 nm, the isotropic height PSD exhibits power-law regions, which can be interpreted as self-affine roughness with Hurst exponents of 0.1-0.56. We also calculate the relative difference between the apparent contact area and the approximated area of the bottom atomic layer. Our simulations illustrate how surface topography evolves with NP size and suggest that larger NPs can have random surface roughness.

Using angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy and first-principles calculations for a Laves-phase superconductor CsBi2, which features a Bi-pyrochlore 3D network with strong SOC, we identify two characteristic electronic structures with a large DOS. ### [81] [Interaction-driven transport in a non-degenerate mixture of Dirac and massive fermions at charge neutrality point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07846)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在伽利略不变性破缺系统中不同载流子物种间的相互作用如何产生丰富的输运现象，特别关注HgTe量子阱在电荷中性点实现的二维混合系统。

Method: 发展了非简并二维混合系统中质量狄拉克费米子与有质量费米子电导率的全面理论框架，采用自洽的温度依赖方法分析两种载流子物种间的相互作用。

Result: 电导率随温度升高呈现明显交叉行为：低温下由质量狄拉克载流子主导，产生类似石墨烯电荷中性点的温度无关电导率；高温下有质量空穴被热激发，与狄拉克载流子的库仑散射导致负的非德鲁德修正。

Conclusion: 电荷中性点条件下的HgTe量子阱为研究无伽利略不变性系统中相互作用驱动的输运提供了清洁、高度可调的平台，使系统输运响应成为物种间量子摩擦的内在探针。

Abstract: The interplay between distinct carrier species in systems with broken Galilean invariance gives rise to a rich landscape of interaction-driven transport phenomena. Here, we develop a comprehensive theory for the electrical conductivity of a non-degenerate two-dimensional mixture of massless Dirac and massive fermions, a system realized in HgTe quantum wells tuned to the charge neutrality point. In this regime, all carriers are thermally activated, enabling a self-consistent, temperature-dependent interplay between the two species. We demonstrate that the conductivity undergoes a distinct crossover as temperature increases: at low temperatures, transport is dominated by massless Dirac carriers, yielding a temperature-independent conductivity reminiscent of graphene's charge neutrality point. As the temperature rises, massive holes become thermally excited, and their mutual Coulomb scattering with Dirac carriers induces a negative, non-Drude correction to the conductivity. We show that this correction is governed by the dominant scattering mechanism: short-range interparticle interactions yield a stronger suppression than long-range Coulomb interactions, and it scales monotonically with temperature. Crucially, the charge neutrality condition ensures that the chemical potential is not externally pinned but is determined self-consistently, making the system's transport response an intrinsic probe of inter-species quantum friction. Our findings establish HgTe quantum wells at charge neutrality as a clean, highly tunable platform for isolating and quantitatively studying interaction-driven transport in the absence of Galilean invariance, offering a direct pathway to explore regimes where interparticle collisions dominate over disorder.

### [82] [Layer-by-layer water filling in molecular-scale capillaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07946)
*Mingwei Chen,Jingshan Wang,Artem Mishchenko,Ivan Timokhin,Fengchao Wang,Andre K. Geim,Qian Yang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在纳米尺度下，水分子不能被视为连续流体，但分子离散性对毛细凝聚和填充过程的影响尚不清楚。理解这一机制对于解释自然现象和技术应用中的纳米毛细现象至关重要。

Method: 研究采用范德华组装（van der Waals assembly）技术制备纳米毛细管，并使用原子力显微镜（atomic force microscopy）监测湿度驱动下水吸收过程中的管壁变形。

Result: 观察到两种不同的填充机制：柔性毛细管呈现逐层填充（layer-by-layer filling），管壁以约3 Å的步长变形，对应单个水分子层的顺序进入；刚性毛细管则表现为突然填充（abrupt filling）。

Conclusion: 分子离散性显著影响毛细现象，管壁柔顺性（wall compliance）决定了离散填充与突然填充之间的选择，这一发现源于变形能与周期性壁-水相互作用（oscillatory wall-water interactions）的竞争。

Abstract: Under ambient humidity, water spontaneously condenses in pores only a few nanometers in size, making nanoscale capillarity central to numerous natural phenomena and technological applications. At these dimensions, water may no longer be treated as a continuous fluid, yet the consequences of molecular discreteness for capillary condensation and filling remain poorly understood. Here we study nanocapillaries fabricated by van der Waals assembly and, using atomic force microscopy, monitor their wall deformations during humidity-driven water uptake. We observe two distinct regimes: layer-by-layer filling of flexible capillaries and abrupt filling of rigid ones. Flexible walls deform in steps of ~3 Å, corresponding to the sequential entry of individual water molecular layers. The different filling regimes are explained by the competition between deformation energy and oscillatory wall-water interactions. Our findings show that the molecular discreteness of water can profoundly affect ubiquitous capillary phenomena, with wall compliance selecting between discrete and abrupt filling.

### [83] [Optical Hall absorption sum rule and spectral compensation in time-reversal-breaking moiré and Hofstadter systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08043)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学光谱学为拓扑量子态提供了强大的无接触探测手段，但反称霍尔吸收的精确约束条件远不如其纵向对应物发展完善。研究受到早期霍尔电导率求和规则的启发，旨在建立相应的光学约束框架。

Method: 研究首先为反称光学电导率（其虚部控制手性相关吸收）构建了首个频率矩约束条件。随后在两类时间反演破缺的拓扑系统中验证该求和规则：零场莫尔连续模型和均匀磁场下的霍夫施塔特模型。

Result: 在零场莫尔连续模型中，频率矩精确为零，意味着任何低频反常霍尔吸收必须被相反符号的高频谱权重补偿。在霍夫施塔特模型中，该矩取由磁通密度决定的普适值，与微观模型细节无关。

Conclusion: 光学霍尔吸收求和规则通过连接低频和高频谱贡献，为量化圆二色性约束和诊断朗道能级混合提供了严格框架。研究展示了已知霍尔谱约束在现代相互作用拓扑材料中获得新的实验相关性内容。

Abstract: Optical spectroscopy provides a powerful, contact-free probe of topological quantum states, yet exact constraints on antisymmetric Hall absorption remain much less well developed than their longitudinal counterparts. Motivated by earlier Hall-conductivity sum rules, we formulate the corresponding first-frequency-moment constraint for the antisymmetric optical conductivity, whose imaginary part governs chirality-dependent absorption. We then demonstrate this sum rule in two classes of time-reversal-breaking topological systems. For a zero-field moiré continuum model hosting topological bands, the moment vanishes exactly, implying that any low-frequency anomalous Hall absorption must be compensated by higher-frequency spectral weight of the opposite sign. For a Hofstadter model under a uniform magnetic field, the same moment takes a universal value fixed by the magnetic flux density, independent of microscopic model details. By linking low- and high-frequency spectral contributions, this optical Hall absorption sum rule provides a rigorous framework for quantifying circular dichroism constraints and diagnosing Landau-level mixing. Our results show how a known Hall spectral constraint acquires new and experimentally relevant content in modern interacting topological materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现Zitterbewegung面积速率的符号定义了旋转方向，并重现了狄拉克点对陈数（Chern number）的贡献。该关系与初始态无关，适用于一般的两带狄拉克模型（two-band Dirac models）。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了带间量子动力学（interband quantum dynamics）与拓扑能带几何（topological band geometry）之间的直接联系，超越了半经典区域（semiclassical regime）的限制。

Abstract: We establish an exact analytical relation between Zitterbewegung dynamics and the band geometry in two-dimensional Dirac systems. By identifying a time-independent antisymmetric observable-the \textit{areal rate of Zitterbewegung}-we show that this quantity is directly determined by the Berry curvature. Its sign defines the sense of rotation and reproduces the contributions of Dirac points to the Chern number. This relation is independent of the initial state and holds for generic two-band Dirac models. Our findings reveal a direct connection between interband quantum dynamics and topological band geometry beyond the semiclassical regime.

Abstract: Achieving long-range ferrimagnetic order in purely organic systems remains a major challenge in molecular magnetism. Starting from a spin-1/2--spin-1 dimer as the elemental ferrimagnetic unit, we employ inelastic electron tunneling spectroscopy to resolve low-energy magnetic excitations and extract the parameters of the Heisenberg Hamiltonian. These findings establish a molecular platform for designing tunable heterospin systems with robust exchange interactions, opening routes toward multi-level spin encoding in qudit-based quantum technologies.

Method: 本文提出了一种基于万尼尔函数（Wannier functions）的新方法来量化OAM算符，该方法建立在现代轨道磁化理论（modern theory of orbital magnetization）基础上，能够同时捕捉OHC的局域（local）和巡游（itinerant）贡献。

Conclusion: 该方法改进了对固体中轨道角动量的理解，并为复杂材料中各种轨道效应的精确估计提供了有效途径。

Abstract: In the field of orbital dynamics and orbital transport, a particularly important quantity is the so-called orbital Hall conductivity (OHC), which is expressed in terms of operators of velocity and orbital angular momentum (OAM). To overcome the difficulties in treating the unbounded position operator, very often atom-centered approximations are used, which capture only a part of the local contributions to the OAM operator. Here, we promote a new approach to quantify the OAM operator in the basis of Wannier functions, which is based on the modern theory of orbital magnetization and which captures both local and itinerant contributions to the OHC. By performing first-principles calculations for various materials, we show that significant corrections to the OHC by non-local effects arise when compared to common approximations. Our approach improves the understanding of the OAM in solids and allows for a precise estimation of various orbital effects in complex materials.

### [87] [Valley-controlled many-body exciton interactions in monolayer WSe$_2$ phototransistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08382)
*Daniel Vaquero,Cédric A. Cordero-Silis,Daniel Erkensten,Roberto Rosati,Martijn H. Takens,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Ermin Malic,Marcos H. D. Guimarães*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用偏振分辨脉冲激光光电流谱技术（polarization-resolved pulsed-laser photocurrent spectroscopy），通过谷选择性激发（valley-selective excitation）在单层WSe₂中实现全光控制。圆偏振激发选择性地在单一谷中填充激子，而线偏振激发则同时填充两个谷。

Abstract: Many-body exciton interactions shape the optoelectronic response of atomically-thin transition metal dichalcogenides, yet optical control of these interactions remains largely unexplored. To date, modulation of exciton-exciton interactions has primarily relied on electrical gating or van der Waals engineering. Here, we demonstrate all-optical control of many-body exciton interactions in monolayer WSe$_2$ via valley-selective excitation using polarization-resolved pulsed-laser photocurrent spectroscopy. Circular excitation selectively populates excitons in a single valley, whereas linear excitation populates both valleys, inducing a valley-dependent nonlinear photoresponse. We observe helicity-dependent exciton renormalization, alongside a two-fold enhancement of sublinear photocurrent scaling under circular excitation, reflecting single-valley population of interacting excitons. A microscopic model incorporating intervalley-exchange and exciton-exciton annihilation mediated by dark and bright exciton populations reproduces the nonlinear valley-selective response. These results establish the valley degree of freedom as an all-optical control parameter for tuning many-body excitonic effects and, exploring correlated exciton states and valleytronic applications in two-dimensional semiconductors.

Abstract: The phenomenon of electron tunneling has long been central to quantum transport and continues to provide a powerful framework for understanding and controlling electronic processes in solids. The emergence of van der Waals (vdW) materials has greatly expanded this opportunity by enabling atomically thin heterostructures with clean interfaces, engineered barriers, and highly tunable band alignment. In this review, we discuss the fundamental mechanisms of photo-assisted transport and the realization of vdW tunnel junctions, and show how they provide electrical access to nonequilibrium dynamics and collective excitations in quantum materials. We further examine emerging functionalities including photodetection, tunneling-driven light emission, sensing, and memory. Finally, we present a forward-looking perspective on new opportunities such as quantum-geometric probes, twist-resolved spectroscopy, moire ferroelectricity, and scalable architectures for computing and sensing.
