### [89] [Electromagnetic wave propagation in static black hole spacetimes: an effective refractive index description in Schwarzschild geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07371)
*Abdullah Guvendi,Omar Mustafa Semra Gurtas Dogan,Hassan Hassanabadi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了在静态球对称黑洞时空中电磁波传播的完全协变且规范不变（gauge-invariant）的表述，将径向动力学转化为亥姆霍兹型（Helmholtz-type）方程，并引入有效折射率（refractive index）来统一描述引力红移、曲率效应和角动量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立静态球对称黑洞时空中电磁波传播的完全协变且规范不变的理论框架，避免引入辅助坐标变换或视界正则变量（horizon-regular variables），为波光学、半经典和数值研究提供坚实基础。

Method: 从弯曲背景上的无源麦克斯韦方程（source-free Maxwell equations）出发，根据宇称（parity）分解电磁扰动，系统约化为规范不变动力学变量；通过适当的场重定义消除一阶导数项，将径向动力学转化为亥姆霍兹型方程。

Result: 轴向和极向（axial and polar）扇区服从相同的宇称无关主方程（parity-independent master equation），其精确等谱性（exact isospectrality）作为四维麦克斯韦理论的直接结果自然出现；在史瓦西几何（Schwarzschild geometry）中获得了闭合解析形式的折射率。

Conclusion: 该描述为电磁波在黑洞时空中的传播和衰减提供了透明且物理直观的解释，在统一光学框架下编码了引力红移、曲率效应和角动量，为更一般静态引力背景下的研究建立了坚实基础。

Abstract: We present a fully covariant and gauge-invariant formulation of electromagnetic wave propagation in static, spherically symmetric black hole spacetimes, developed entirely within Schwarzschild-like coordinates. Start ing from the source-free Maxwell equations on a curved background, electromagnetic perturbations are de composed according to parity and systematically reduced to gauge-invariant dynamical variables without introducing auxiliary coordinate transformations or horizon-regular variables. Both axial and polar sectors are shown to obey the same parity-independent master equation, and their exact isospectrality emerges nat urally as a direct consequence of Maxwell theory in four dimensions. By eliminating first-derivative terms through an appropriate field redefinition, the radial dynamics is cast into a Helmholtz-type equation, which motivates the introduction of an effective, position- and frequency-dependent refractive index encoding grav itational redshift, curvature effects, and angular momentum within a unified optical framework. Specializing to the Schwarzschild geometry, we obtain the refractive index in closed analytical form and analyze its behavior in the near-horizon, intermediate, and asymptotic regimes. The resulting description provides a transparent and physically intuitive interpretation of electromagnetic evanescence, and propagation in black hole spacetimes, and establishes a robust foundation for wave-optical, semiclassical, and numerical studies in more general static gravitational backgrounds.

</details>


### [90] [Exact quasinormal residues and double poles from hypergeometric connection formulas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07400)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于库默解（Kummer solutions）的连接公式，构建了显式的量子化函数（quantization function）来编码任意线性渐近边界条件。通过该函数的闭合形式Digamma导数（Digamma derivative）代数控制频率相关谱因子，避免了积分计算。

Conclusion: 该形式体系为可约化为高斯超几何方程的径向边值问题提供了统一的数学框架，能够代数处理频域格林函数的极点结构和准正规模谱，特别适用于分析双极点准正规模和异常谱特征。

Abstract: We develop a unified mathematical method for the pole structure of frequency-domain Green's functions and the associated quasinormal spectra in radial boundary value problems reducible to the Gauss hypergeometric equation. By systematically employing connection formulas for Kummer solutions, we construct an explicit quantization function that encodes arbitrary linear asymptotic boundary conditions. We demonstrate that the frequency-dependent spectral factor entering the residue formula is controlled algebraically by the closed-form Digamma derivative of this quantization function, bypassing integral evaluation. Furthermore, we establish the simultaneous vanishing of the quantization function and its first derivative as a direct algebraic criterion for double-pole QNMs. The formalism is successfully benchmarked against the exact BTZ black hole spectrum and provides an analytic diagnostic for the exceptional lines and nearly double-pole excitations in the Nariai/Pöschl-Teller limit.

Conclusion: 该研究旨在通过分析规范固定量子化方法的一致性，为解决球对称引力与标量场耦合系统在圈量子引力中的Dirac量子化问题提供新的途径。

Abstract: The Dirac quantization of spherically symmetric gravity coupled to a scalar field in Loop Quantum Gravity remains unresolved, mainly because of the difficulty in maintaining a consistent constraint algebra at the quantum level. One possible way to overcome this obstruction is to fix the gauge by coupling the system to a physical clock. However, this approach requires careful control of the consistency of the gauge-fixed theory and factor-ordering ambiguities. Here, we address these issues by analyzing whether the gauge-fixed quantization reproduces the well-known results for the quantization of a black hole in vacuum using the Dirac method. This requires a treatment valid throughout the outer region of the black hole, where the asymptotic approximations considered in previous studies do not hold true.

Result: 外尔规范理论是唯一具有物理规范玻色子的时空对称性规范理论，且外尔反常（Weyl anomaly）自由。该理论具有精确的几何解释，所有尺度均源于几何起源，并在其自发对称性破缺相中生成爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用（Einstein-Hilbert action）和正宇宙学常数。

Abstract: In 1918 Weyl introduced Weyl conformal geometry and its associated quadratic action which was the first gauge theory, of a spacetime symmetry, the Weyl gauge theory (of dilatations and Poincaré symmetry). The initial physical interpretation of his theory was however short-lived and led to the downfall of Weyl geometry as a physical theory. We review how this action was re-born into a physical Weyl gauge theory of gravity. This is the only gauge theory of a spacetime symmetry with a physical gauge boson, is Weyl anomaly-free, has {\it exact} geometric interpretation, with all scales of geometric origin, and generates Einstein-Hilbert action and a positive cosmological constant in its spontaneously broken phase. A more fundamental Weyl-Dirac-Born-Infeld gauge theory action exists in Weyl geometry, that does not need a UV regularisation, of which the (geometrically regularised) Weyl gauge theory is the leading order.

Abstract: We apply a general relativistic framework to static and rotating black hole solutions in Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity or modified gravity (MOG). Our results yield exact analytic, closed-form relations expressing the mass $M$, the MOG coupling parameter $α$, and the distance $D$ of a Schwarzschild-MOG black hole in terms of a minimal set of directly measurable elements of the accretion disk: the total frequency shift, the telescope aperture angle, and the redshift rapidity. The resulting expressions are derived for particles close to the midline and line of sight, where the redshift rapidity is treated as a relativistic invariant encoding the evolution of the frequency shift with respect to the emitter's proper time in MOG spacetime. We further extend the formalism to the rotating Kerr-MOG geometry and obtain corresponding relations that determine the rotation parameter $a$ jointly with $M$, $α$, and $D$ on the midline. In the rotating background, we introduced the redshift acceleration (general-relativistic version of jerk) to disentangle the spacetime parameters. Crucially, the explicit appearance of $α$ in these formulas enables direct empirical estimation of this parameter, thereby providing a means to test for departures from standard general relativity. The previous results obtained in the standard Schwarzschild/Kerr backgrounds are recovered in the limit $α\to 0$. The derived expressions are concise and suitable for incorporation into black hole parameter-estimation pipelines.

Method: 研究量化了短时致密双星并合引力波信号与常见LIGO瞬态噪声相互作用时，推断后验分布的偏移情况，作为信号并合时间与噪声时间间隔的函数。

Result: 研究发现"blip"、"thunder"和"fast-scattering"等瞬态噪声对质量、自旋和天空位置参数估计产生统计显著的偏差。大多数情况下所有参数都容易受到显著偏差影响，且信号时间先验内的噪声比外部噪声造成更极端的偏差。

Conclusion: 研究提供了受重叠噪声源影响最大的参数估计，以及无需噪声消除即可获得无偏源属性估计的引力波信号与噪声之间的"安全"时间间隔标准。

Abstract: Data from gravitational-wave (GW) detectors often contains a high rate of non-Gaussian transient noise, known as glitches. The parameters estimated from GW signals coinciding with detector glitches are occasionally biased away from their true values. During the first part of the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) observing run, 29% of GW candidates had overlapping or nearby glitches in one or more detectors. In the latter part of the fourth observation run, sensitivity improvements have increased the rates of GW detection. Consequently, scenarios in which GW signals and detector glitches overlap in time are more likely. In this study, we quantify shifts in inferred posterior distributions for short-duration compact binary coalescence GW signals interacting with common LIGO glitches as a function of time between the signal merger time and the glitch. We find statistically significant biases in parameter estimation for mass, spin, and sky position for "blip", "thunder", and "fast-scattering" glitches. Using these results, we provide estimates of what parameters are most affected by overlapping noise sources, as well as what constitutes a "safe" time separation between a gravitational wave signal and a glitch, without requiring glitch subtraction for unbiased source property estimation. We find that in a majority of cases, all parameters are susceptible to significant bias due to glitch interference. Additionally, we find that glitches that occur within the time prior of the GW signal cause more extreme biases than glitches outside of the time prior.

Abstract: Based on the backward ray-tracing method, this paper numerically investigates the shadow and polarization images of rotating Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet (EGB) black hole within the framework of a thin disk model. We systematically analyze the effects of the main model parameters and the observation inclination angle $θ_o$ on both types of images. The results show that, as an intrinsic property of the black hole, the inner shadow undergoes significant deformation with increasing $θ_o$. The increase of the GB coupling constant $ξ$ only reduces the size of the inner shadow, while the spin parameter a does not alter its size but also its shape. And, the photon ring is more sensitive to variations in $θ_o$, while it is less affected by $ξ$ and $a$. For polarization images, the influence of $ξ$ on the polarization intensity is generally consistent with that observed in the accretion disk images. However, the polarization direction near the region of the inner shadow and photon ring changes significantly with $ξ$. This feature can provide an additional and effective observational tool for extracting information about the spacetime structure in Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet (EGB) gravity. Finally, we conclude that, compared to previous reliance on either accretion disk or polarization images alone, the simultaneous combination and synergistic analysis of both can more profoundly reveal the optical properties of rotating EGB black holes, providing a stronger theoretical basis for identifying such black holes through future high-resolution observations.

### [96] [Quasinormal modes of the thick braneworld in $f(T)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07858)

Abstract: We investigate the quasinormal modes (QNMs) of a thick brane model in $f(T)$ gravity with $f(T) = T + αT^2$. Requiring the energy density to remain positive and the scalar field to be real constrains the parameter $α$ to the range $[-\frac{7}{48},\frac{1}{48}]$. Within this allowed region, we find that the parameter $α$ can induce a brane-splitting structure. The quasinormal frequencies of the system are computed using both the asymptotic iteration method and the Bernstein spectral method. The two approaches show good agreement in the low-overtone regime. For $α<0$, the decay rate of the first QNM decreases as $|α|$ increases, whereas higher overtones exhibit the opposite behavior. To further examine the influence of model parameters on the QNM spectrum, we also perform numerical time-domain evolution of perturbations, whose results are consistent with the frequency-domain analysis. Our results provide a concrete example of quasinormal spectra in thick brane models within $f(T)$ gravity and may offer useful insights for future observational tests of extra dimensions.

### [97] [Observational Quantities in Quasi-Newtonian Descriptions of Cosmological Space-Times](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08119)
*Asta Heinesen,Davide Fontana,Timothy Clifton*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种"准牛顿（quasi-Newtonian）"框架，用于分析具有无剪切叶理（shear-free foliation）的宇宙时空中的距离和红移测量。该框架将广义相对论宇宙学与牛顿自由度联系起来，为理解非微扰结构提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用准牛顿框架，假设时空允许无剪切叶理，且能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）以静止质量密度为主，物质的三维速度在准牛顿系中较小。在此基础上推导运动学和光传播的基本结果，并利用简并Kasner解作为示例进行说明。

Result: 研究结果为运动学和光传播提供了基本公式，能够用量化方式描述观测量与Friedmann宇宙学预测的偏离。该方法为理解当前宇宙学张力提供了新视角，将相对论时空结构表达为可从宇宙学微扰理论和后牛顿展开中理解的物理量。

Conclusion: 准牛顿框架为分析广义相对论宇宙学中的非微扰结构提供了有效工具，通过牛顿自由度理解相对论时空结构，并为解决当前宇宙学张力问题提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: We investigate measures of distance and redshift in cosmological space-times that admit a shear-free foliation, which we henceforth refer to as `quasi-Newtonian'. Space expands isotropically in this description, and small-scale gravitational physics has a natural Newtonian limit, which makes it ideal for considering the physics of wide classes of cosmological models. By assuming that the energy-momentum tensor is dominated by rest-mass density, and that the 3-velocity of matter is small in the quasi-Newtonian frame, we derive fundamental results for kinematics and light propagation. Our results provide a new way of formulating general-relativistic cosmologies with non-perturbative structures in terms of quantities that can be understood from cosmological perturbation theory and post-Newtonian expansions, and allow us to quantify departures of observables from the predictions of Friedmann cosmology. It thereby provides a route to understanding inherently relativistic space-time structures, such as those that occur in Lemaître-Tolman-Bondi, Szekeres solutions, and Bianchi cosmologies in terms of Newtonian degrees of freedom. We illustrate our results using the degenerate Kasner solution as an example, and explain how our approach can be used to provide new insights into the current cosmological tensions.

</details>


### [98] [Detecting Chiral Gravitational Wave Background with a Dipole Pulsar Timing Array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08141)

Conclusion: 偶极脉冲星计时阵列系统（dPTA）提供了一种探测纳赫兹引力波背景中宇称破缺效应的新方法，并显著扩展了可探测频率范围，为引力波天文学开辟了新的观测窗口。

Abstract: The pulsar timing array (PTA) is a powerful technique for detecting nanohertz gravitational wave backgrounds (GWBs). However, conventional PTAs lack sensitivity to parity violation in the GWB. In this work, we propose a dipole pulsar timing array system (dPTA). By deriving the overlap reduction functions (ORFs) from the cross-correlation of timing signals, we find that this system exhibits sensitivity to chiral GWBs in the nanohertz regime. Furthermore, through numerical calculations of its sensitivity curves, we demonstrate that the dPTA extends the detectable frequency range of PTAs for GWBs from the nanohertz to the microhertz regime.

We then analyze the horizon structure, Hawking temperature, extended phase-space thermodynamics, and the associated equation of state. In addition, we investigate null and timelike geodesics, with emphasis on the effective potentials, photon sphere, shadow radius for a static observer at finite distance, and innermost stable circular orbit. The resulting framework furnishes the exact AdS extension of the asymptotically flat PINLED black hole and provides a coherent basis for numerical and phenomenological studies of its thermodynamic, optical, and orbital properties.

### [100] [GW231123: False Massive Graviton Signatures from Unmodeled Point-Mass Lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08179)
*Baoxiang Wang,Tao Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: GW231123作为当前最强的引力波透镜候选事件，其未建模的点质量透镜效应会模拟出虚假的非零引力子质量信号，一旦纳入透镜模型分析，该异常信号即消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在解释GW231123引力波事件中出现的异常现象：使用未包含透镜效应的IMRPhenomXPHM模板分析时，观测到明显的非零引力子质量后验分布。该异常为检验点质量透镜如何影响基于传播的引力测试提供了独特案例。

Result: 未建模的点质量透镜效应确实能产生虚假的引力子质量信号：使用未包含透镜的IMRPhenomXPHM模板恢复时，产生与真实数据相似的显著虚假引力子质量后验；而包含透镜的分析结果相互一致，均无证据支持非零引力子质量。

Abstract: GW231123 is the strongest current candidate for a lensed gravitational wave event and a unique case for testing how point-mass lensing affects propagation-based tests of gravity. In the real GW231123 data, an unlensed IMRPhenomXPHM analysis yields an apparent nonzero graviton mass posterior. We show that this anomaly is naturally explained by unmodeled point-mass lensing: once lensing is included, the apparent graviton mass signal disappears. In GW231123-like injection-recovery tests, a lensed NRSur7dq4 signal with zero graviton mass, recovered with the same unlensed IMRPhenomXPHM template, produces a similarly pronounced spurious graviton mass posterior, whereas lensing-included analyses with IMRPhenomXPHM, IMRPhenomXO4a, and NRSur7dq4 remain mutually consistent with no evidence for nonzero graviton mass. The similarity between the injected and real data posteriors shows that unmodeled point-mass lensing can mimic modified gravitational wave propagation. These results identify a concrete failure mode in tests of gravity and strengthen the interpretation of GW231123 as a lensed candidate.

### [102] [Dynamics for Spin-$1/2$ Particles in Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08202)
*E. Maciel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在哈密顿框架下，探讨了自旋-1/2粒子在静态球对称爱因斯坦-高斯-博内特（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet）黑洞时空中的量子动力学，推导出包含高斯-博内特耦合参数修正的力算符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于超越经典测地线运动，在量子层面描述粒子动力学，同时纳入相对论和量子效应，特别是在包含高阶曲率修正的爱因斯坦-高斯-博内特引力理论背景下。

Method: 方法基于弯曲时空中的狄拉克方程（Dirac equation），采用标架形式（tetrad formalism）和关联的自旋联络（spin connection）进行表述，在EGB背景下构建相应的狄拉克哈密顿量（Dirac Hamiltonian），并由此推导位置和动量算符的海森堡运动方程（Heisenberg equations of motion）。

Result: 获得了速度算符和力算符的显式表达式，结果显示力算符包含明确依赖于高斯-博内特耦合参数ξ的修正项，这些修正编码了量子层面上引力相互作用的高阶曲率修正，特别是在强场区域，有效径向力显著偏离广义相对论的对应结果。

Conclusion: 该算符方法提供了超越经典测地线运动的粒子动力学直接描述，证明了在爱因斯坦-高斯-博内特黑洞时空中，量子粒子的动力学行为受到高阶曲率修正的显著影响，这些修正通过力算符中的ξ依赖项体现，在强场区域变得尤为重要。

Abstract: I investigate the quantum dynamics of a spin-$1/2$ particle in a static, spherically symmetric Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet (EGB) black-hole spacetime within the Hamiltonian framework. Starting from the Dirac equation in curved spacetime, formulated via the tetrad formalism and the associated spin connection, we construct the corresponding Dirac Hamiltonian in the EGB background. Using this Hamiltonian, we derive the Heisenberg equations of motion for the position and momentum operators, obtaining explicit expressions for the velocity and force operators. This operator-based approach provides a direct description of particle dynamics beyond classical geodesic motion, incorporating both relativistic and quantum effects. We show that the resulting force operator contains corrections explicitly dependent on the Gauss-Bonnet coupling parameter $ξ$, which encode higher-curvature modifications of the gravitational interaction at the quantum level. In particular, the effective radial force deviates from its general relativistic counterpart by terms that become significant in the strong-field regime.

### [103] [Unifying topological, geometric, and complex classifications of black hole thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08315)
*Shi-Hao Zhang,Shao-Wen Wei,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明了黑洞热力学的三种分类方案在实数域内是等价的，通过温度曲线的极值点数量统一了基于局部几何性质、全局拓扑不变量和黎曼曲面叶状结构的分类框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞热力学近期出现了三种不同的分类方案：基于温度函数的局部几何性质、全局拓扑不变量以及复平面中的黎曼曲面叶状结构。研究旨在揭示这些看似不同的方案之间的内在联系。

Method: 通过建立两个对应关系（dictionary）：一个将热稳定性与温度曲线的单调性联系起来，另一个将黑洞状态数量与黎曼曲面的叶状结构数（foliation number）相关联。研究证明了温度曲线极值点的数量决定了所有三种框架中的分类。

Result: 三种分类方案在实数域内是等价的，这种统一性可追溯至黑洞解空间的临界点结构（critical point structure）。多个黑洞示例表明，通过计算极值点可以获得拓扑不变量和相变信息。

Conclusion: 该统一框架简化了黑洞热力学分析，并为探索更复杂的黑洞系统提供了理论基础。温度曲线极值点的计数成为连接不同分类方案的核心桥梁。

Abstract: Black hole thermodynamics has recently witnessed three distinct classification schemes: based on local geometric properties of the temperature function, global topological invariants, and Riemann surface foliations in the complex plane. We show that these schemes are equivalent in the real domain via two dictionaries: one linking thermal stability to the monotonicity of the temperature curve, and the other connecting the number of black hole states to the foliation number of a Riemann surface. The number of extremal points of the temperature curve determines the classification in all three frameworks, tracing this unification to the critical point structure of the black hole solution space. As an illustration, several black holes demonstrate how counting extrema yields topological invariants and phase transition information. This unified framework simplifies black hole thermodynamic analysis and provides a foundation for exploring more complex black holes.

### [104] [Pyramid Interferometers: Direct Access to Cosmological Gravitational Wave Chirality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08471)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙引力波背景为研究远超出地面实验能标的宇称破坏物理提供了重要窗口，但传统共面探测器网络对各项同性圆偏振不敏感，无论其相对取向如何。这一局限性阻碍了对早期宇宙宇称破坏和基本对称性破缺的探测。

Method: 提出了一种新型共定位三维干涉仪设计（Pyramid），其非共面配置能够几何隔离手征性。该设计是第三代引力波探测器的自然延伸，通过区分共面相关通道和非共面通道来分离偏振信号。

Result: 共面相关通道对圆偏振不敏感，而共定位非共面通道对未偏振背景不敏感，仅在存在非零净螺旋度时获得响应。Pyramid干涉仪因此能够独特地探测宇宙引力波手征性。

Conclusion: Pyramid干涉仪为探测宇宙引力波手征性提供了独特工具，开辟了测试早期宇宙宇称破坏和基本对称性破缺的现实地面途径，是第三代引力波探测器的自然扩展。

Abstract: The cosmological gravitational wave background provides a powerful window on parity-violating physics at energies far beyond the reach of terrestrial experiments. However, any co-located planar detector network is insensitive to isotropic circular polarization, independent of its relative orien- tation. In this letter, we show that this no-go result can be evaded by a new class of co-located 3D interferometer designs, which we call Pyramid, whose non-coplanar configuration geometrically isolates chirality. This new design is a natural extension of the third generation of gravitational wave detectors. The coplanar correlation channel is blind to circular polarization, whereas the co-located non-coplanar channel is insensitive to the unpolarized background and acquires a response only in the presence of nonzero net helicity. Pyramid interferometers therefore furnish a unique probe of cosmological gravitational-wave chirality, opening a realistic terrestrial pathway to test parity violation and fundamental symmetry breaking in the early Universe.

### [105] [Metric affine gravity with dynamical chronology protection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08511)
*Moustafa Ismail,David Mattingly*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出将时序保护（chronology protection）从派生性质提升为构建修正引力理论的指导原则，并引入一个玩具度规-仿射引力模型，通过破坏投影不变性动态生成全局时间函数来实现稳定因果性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文的动机源于观察到某些修正引力理论（如拟态引力（mimetic gravity）和Horava-Lifshitz引力）虽非为时序保护而设计，但都通过稳定因果性（stable causality）在经典层面实现了这一性质。这暗示时序保护本身可从派生性质提升为构建修正引力理论的指导原则，特别是如果其在量子引力层面的实现会在有效作用量中留下红外印记。

Method: 作者引入了一个玩具度规-仿射引力（metric-affine gravity）模型，该模型仅修改几何部分。该模型通过破坏投影不变性（projective invariance）动态生成全局时间函数（global time function），从而实现了稳定因果性。

Result: 该模型成功实现了稳定因果性。研究进一步表明，拟态引力可作为该模型的一个特例被恢复，同时一个更广泛的暗物质（dark sector）自然地涌现出来。

Conclusion: 时序保护可以作为构建修正引力理论的一个指导原则。通过破坏投影不变性动态生成全局时间函数，可以在仅修改几何部分的度规-仿射引力模型中实现稳定因果性，并自然地包含拟态引力等特例和更广泛的暗物质现象。

Abstract: Modified theories of gravity often introduce geometric structure beyond general relativity in order to address unresolved problems in the gravitational sector without invoking ad hoc matter fields. Mimetic gravity, for example, generates an effective cosmological dark sector by isolating the conformal mode of the metric, while Horava--Lifshitz gravity attains power-counting renormalizability by endowing spacetime with a preferred dynamical foliation. Although chronology protection was not the original motivation for either theory, both enforce it classically through stable causality. This suggests that chronology protection itself may be elevated from a derived property to a guiding principle for constructing modified gravitational theories, especially if its implementation at the quantum-gravitational level leaves infrared imprints in the effective action. Motivated by this possibility, we introduce a toy metric--affine gravity model that modifies only the geometric sector. The model realizes stable causality by dynamically generating a global time function via breaking of projective invariance. We further show that mimetic gravity is recovered as a special case, while a broader dark sector emerges naturally.

</details>

### [106] [Linear odd electrophoresis of a sphere in a charged chiral active fluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07510)
*Reinier van Buel,Bogdan Cichocki,Jeffrey C. Everts*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究首次提出了带电手性活性流体（charged chiral active fluid）概念，将电动力学与奇斯托克斯流（odd Stokes flow）耦合，推导了任意形状粒子在弱电场中的电泳迁移率（electrophoretic mobility）通用表达式，并获得了带电球体在低zeta电位下的精确解析解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解带电胶体粒子在具有奇粘度（odd viscosity）流体中的电泳现象，这是理解电荷稳定手性活性悬浮液（charge-stabilized chiral active suspensions）中输运现象的基础挑战。需要探索经典牛顿流体电泳结果在奇粘度存在下的推广情况。

Method: 采用奇流体的洛伦兹互易定理（Lorentz reciprocal theorem for odd fluids），推导了任意形状粒子在弱外电场中电泳迁移率的通用表达式。将此结果应用于低zeta电位的导电带电球体，获得了精确的封闭形式解析表达式。

Result: 研究发现电泳迁移率与中性球体的平动迁移率成正比，并由亨利函数（Henry function）调制，这与牛顿流体相似。然而，奇粘度导致电泳迁移率张量出现方向不对称性（directional asymmetries），即使在薄双电层（thin electric double layers）条件下也持续存在。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了带电手性活性流体的理论框架，揭示了奇粘度引入的电泳迁移率方向不对称性，这与各向同性牛顿流体中带电各向异性粒子的行为形成鲜明对比，后者在相同静电屏蔽条件下各向异性效应会消失。

Abstract: The electrophoresis of charged colloidal particles in fluids exhibiting odd viscosity represents a fundamental challenge in understanding transport phenomena within charge-stabilized chiral active suspensions. Here, we provide the first concept of a charged chiral active fluid, where electrokinetics is coupled to odd Stokes flow, to explore how classical results from electrophoresis in Newtonian fluids generalize in the presence of odd viscosity. In particular, we derive a general expression for the electrophoretic mobility for particles of any shape under weak external electric fields using the Lorentz reciprocal theorem for odd fluids. By applying this result to a conducting charged sphere at low zeta potentials, we obtain an exact, closed-form analytical expression for the electrophoretic mobility, valid for arbitrary values of the Debye screening length and the odd-viscosity coefficient. Similar to Newtonian fluids, we find that the electrophoretic mobility is proportional to the translational mobility of an uncharged sphere, modulated by the Henry function. However, unlike in Newtonian fluids, odd viscosity leads to directional asymmetries in the electrophoretic mobility tensor that persist even for thin electric double layers. This case contrasts significantly with a charged anisotropic particle suspended in an isotropic Newtonian fluid, where anisotropic effects would vanish under the same electrostatic-screening conditions.

</details>


### [107] [Statistical Physics of the Two-Dimensional Coulomb Liquid with Ionic Hard-Core Size](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07620)
*Sahin Buyukdagli*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文应用了一种自洽理论来研究具有有限离子尺寸的二维库仑液体，该理论将静电相互作用和硬核相互作用置于同等地位。通过与蒙特卡洛模拟结果比较，该理论在中度盐密度下能准确描述从弱到中等耦合强度的二维溶液热力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于发展一个能够同等处理静电相互作用和硬核相互作用的电解质理论，以更准确地描述二维库仑液体的性质。现有连续介质方法在描述带电硬盘的非均匀屏蔽效应方面存在局限。

Method: 采用自洽理论框架，将静电相互作用和硬核相互作用置于同等地位处理。通过计算离子对分布、结构因子和热力学函数，并与文献中的广泛蒙特卡洛模拟结果进行比较验证。

Result: 在中度盐密度下，该计算方法能够准确描述从弱到中等耦合强度的二维溶液热力学。相对于连续介质方法，本理论精度的提高主要源于其能够考虑带电硬盘离子氛围不可穿透性相关的静电相互作用非均匀屏蔽效应。

Conclusion: 在低盐密度下，自洽框架的有效域低估了离子簇形成的程度，低于二维带电硬盘发生导体-绝缘体转变的临界耦合域。这表明要通过本形式体系接近低温介电相，需要将基础自洽近似至少扩展到下一个累积阶。

Abstract: A self-consistent theory of bulk electrolytes incorporating electrostatic and hard-core interactions on an equal level is applied to the two-dimensional Coulomb liquid with finite ion size. The ionic pair distributions, the structure factors, and the thermodynamic functions of the formalism are compared with extensive Monte-Carlo simulation results from the literature. At moderate salt densities, our computational approach can accurately describe the thermodynamics of two-dimensional solutions from weak to intermediate coupling strengths. The improved accuracy of the present theory with respect to continuum approaches stems mainly from its ability to account for the non-uniform screening of electrostatic interactions associated with the impenetrability of the charged hard disks by their ionic atmosphere. At low salt densities, the validity domain of our self-consistent framework underestimating the extent of ionic cluster formation drops below the critical coupling domain where the conductor-insulator transition of two-dimensional charged hard disks occurs. This indicates that approaching the low-temperature dielectric phase via the present formalism will require the extension of the underlying self-consistent approximation at least up to the next cumulant order.

</details>


### [108] [Mode-coupling theory for aging in active glasses: relaxation dynamics and evolution towards steady state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07820)
*Soumitra Kolya,Nir S. Gov,Saroj Kumar Nandi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究建立了活性玻璃（active glasses）的通用模式耦合理论（MCT），以探究活性系统中老化（aging）动力学的调控机制。理论分析表明，活性参数（自推进力f₀和持续τₚ）通过改变MCT临界点λ_C来影响老化行为，其中弛豫时间t_r与等待时间t_w呈幂律关系t_r∼t_w^δ，且δ随f₀增大而减小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 老化（aging）是玻璃态动力学（glassy dynamics）的关键特征，指系统性质随等待时间t_w的演化。近期实验在具有内在活性（inherently active）的生物系统中也观测到老化现象，这些系统具有自推进力（self-propulsion force）f₀和持续时间（persistence time）τₚ。因此，探究活性系统中老化动力学的调控机制具有基础重要性。

Method: 研究构建了活性玻璃（active glasses）的通用模式耦合理论（mode-coupling theory, MCT）框架。该理论框架能够处理活性系统特有的动力学行为，并通过理论求解获得老化解（aging solutions）。

Result: 理论的老化解显示，两点关联函数（two-point correlation function）随等待时间t_w增长而衰减更慢，弛豫时间（relaxation time）t_r增加。活性对MCT临界点λ_C的修正对活性老化（active aging）有深远影响：淬火距离（quench distance）λ_C控制老化过程并决定指数δ，其中t_r∼t_w^δ。δ随f₀增大而减小，与现有模拟结果一致；但δ随τₚ的变化取决于活性的具体性质。

Conclusion: 该工作对活性玻璃（active glasses）具有基础理论意义，并为深入理解生物系统中的老化动力学（aging dynamics）开辟了道路。理论框架揭示了活性参数如何通过调控MCT临界点来影响老化标度行为。

Abstract: Aging refers to the evolution of system properties with waiting time $t_w$. It is a key feature of glassy dynamics. Recent experiments have demonstrated aging in biological systems that are inherently active with a magnitude of self-propulsion force $f_0$ and a persistence time $τ_p$. Thus, what governs the aging dynamics in these active systems has fundamental importance. We formulate a generic mode-coupling theory (MCT) of active glasses to address this question. The aging solutions of the theory show that the two-point correlation function decays more slowly with growing $t_w$, and the relaxation time $t_r$ increases. The activity-modification of the MCT critical point, $λ_\text{C}$, has profound significance for active aging: the quench distance from $λ_\text{C}$ governs aging and determines $δ$, where $t_r\sim t_w^δ$. $δ$ decreases with increasing $f_0$, in agreement with existing simulations. However, the variation with $τ_p$ depends on the nature of activity. Our work has fundamental theoretical implications for active glasses and paves the way for a deeper understanding of the aging dynamics in biological systems.

</details>


### [109] [Spatially Structured Cohesion from Extremal Alignment in Topological Active Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08134)
*Julian Giraldo-Barreto,Viktor Holubec*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于候选方向依赖的极值对齐规则（candidate-dependent extremal alignment），能够在没有显式吸引力的情况下实现自约束集体运动，克服了传统弛豫对齐（relaxational alignment）的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统弛豫对齐模型（relaxational alignment models）在无边界系统中与局部密度解耦，无法在没有额外吸引力的情况下维持自约束集体运动。本研究旨在探索如何通过改变对齐规则来克服这一限制。

Method: 引入候选方向依赖的极值对齐规则（candidate-dependent extremal alignment rules），其中相互作用邻域取决于候选方向。研究采用具有成对可加效用（pairwise additive utilities）的候选依赖规则，并比较了度量模型（metric models）和拓扑相互作用（topological interactions）的效果。

Result: 候选依赖规则使决策效用分解为平均相互作用分数与选定邻居数量的乘积，这种乘法结构将方向决策与局部密度耦合，从而在没有显式内聚力的情况下产生有效内聚偏置（cohesive bias）。拓扑相互作用能够调节度量模型中的全局连接倾向，在开放空间中稳定有限范围的自约束群体（self-confined flocks）。

Conclusion: 候选方向依赖的极值对齐是一种简单机制，能够在标准弛豫范式之外产生具有内聚性和空间结构的活性物质（active matter），其动力学展现出丰富的相图，包括极化群体、集群和持续旋转状态。

Abstract: Alignment interactions in active matter are typically modeled as relaxational dynamics toward local consensus. In unbounded systems, this makes alignment effectively decoupled from local density and therefore unable to sustain self-confined collective motion without additional attractive forces. Here we show that this limitation can be overcome by extremal alignment rules in which the interaction neighborhood depends on the candidate orientation. For a broad class of candidate- dependent rules with pairwise additive utilities, the decision utility factorizes into the product of an average interaction score and the number of selected neighbors. This multiplicative structure couples orientational decisions to local density and thereby generates an effective cohesive bias without explicit cohesive forces. In metric models, however, the same mechanism drives collapse toward globally connected, effectively mean-field states that suppress spatial structure. We show that topological interactions regularize this tendency, stabilizing self-confined flocks of finite extent in open space. The resulting dynamics exhibits a rich dynamical phase diagram as a function of noise intensity and turning rate, including polarized flocks, swarms, and persistent swirling states. Our results identify candidate-dependent extremal alignment as a simple mechanism for generating cohesive, spatially structured active matter beyond the standard relaxational paradigm.

</details>

Here, we highlight recent advances in the fabrication of anisotropic active particles and architectures enabled by the unprecedented design freedom of 3D microprinting. We discuss how additive manufacturing is expanding the accessible parameter space of active soft matter, allowing precise control over shape, location of active forces, and functionality at the microscale. These developments establish new model platforms for uncovering fundamental principles of active and soft matter, and simultaneously pave the way toward microrobotic systems with programmable dynamics and emergent functionalities.

### [111] [Exact Generalized Langevin Dynamics of Pair Coordinates in Elastic Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08320)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究解析推导了任意弹性网络中两个标记珠子相对坐标的精确hGLE。在小位移近似下，进一步推导了珠子间距离的hGLE，这是距离敏感单分子实验中的核心可观测量。

Result: 成功推导出记忆核和有效恢复力与网络矩阵的显式表达式，实现了高维网络动力学到对坐标的系统性约化。所得结果为建模蛋白质和其他软物质系统提供了广泛潜在应用。

Abstract: Generalized Langevin equations (GLEs) provide a powerful framework for describing slow dynamics in soft-matter systems, but deriving an exact homogeneous GLE (hGLE) for a reaction coordinate from an underlying many-body system remains generally difficult. Here, we analytically derive an exact hGLE for the relative coordinate of two tagged beads in arbitrary elastic networks. The memory kernel and effective restoring force are expressed explicitly in terms of the network matrices, thereby providing a systematic reduction of the high-dimensional network dynamics to a pair coordinate. Within the small-displacement approximation, we further derive a hGLE for the inter-bead distance, a central observable in distance-sensitive single-molecule experiments. These results therefore have broad potential applications in modeling proteins and other soft-matter systems.

### [112] [Axial forces in capillary liquid bridges of polymer solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08361)
*Sreeram Rajesh,Riley S. Tinianov,Jooyeon Park,Alban Sauret*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究测量了粘弹性聚合物溶液液桥在球形颗粒间受控分离时产生的轴向力，发现准静态速率下毛细力主导，而高速拉伸时粘性耗散和粘弹性丝形成增强峰值力并延迟断裂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业与环境中的许多粘合剂（binders）表现出粘弹性行为，而现有颗粒尺度研究大多假设牛顿流体。为建立预测模型，需要测量粘弹性液桥产生的颗粒尺度力。

Method: 测量粘弹性聚合物溶液在两个球形颗粒（beads）间受控单轴分离时产生的轴向力。通过改变聚合物浓度、分离速度和颗粒尺寸，追踪液桥变薄和断裂过程中的力变化。

Result: 准静态速率下轴向力仍由毛细力（capillarity）主导，不受聚合物流变学显著影响。增加拉伸速率通过粘性耗散（viscous dissipation）提高峰值力，并促进粘弹性丝（viscoelastic filament）形成从而延迟断裂。峰值轴向力通过毛细数（capillary number）和颗粒尺寸归一化后收敛，有效断裂距离通过韦森伯格数（Weissenberg number）归一化后收敛。

Conclusion: 研究结果为聚合物粘合剂提供了简单的一阶颗粒尺度力定律（first-order particle-scale force law），揭示了粘弹性液桥行为对分离速率的依赖性。

Abstract: Liquid bridges form between particles during wet mixing with binders or by condensation due to ambient humidity. The consequences of capillary bridges can be quite drastic, creating macroscopic cohesion, as seen in sandcastles and in the formation of particulate agglomerates. Bulk effects in cohesive particles arise from forces generated by capillary bridges, so particle-scale measurements are needed to develop predictive models. Most existing studies at the particle scale assume Newtonian liquids. Yet many binders in industry and in the environment can exhibit viscoelastic behavior. In this study, we measure the axial force generated by liquid bridges of viscoelastic polymer solutions between two spherical beads during controlled uniaxial separation. We vary the polymer concentration, separation velocity, and particle size, and track the force as the bridge thins and ruptures. At quasi-static rates, the axial force remains dominated by capillarity and is not significantly affected by polymer rheology. However, increasing the stretching rate increases the peak force through viscous dissipation and promotes the formation of a viscoelastic filament, thereby delaying rupture. The peak axial forces collapse when rescaled by a capillary number and particle size, while the effective rupture distance collapses with a Weissenberg number. These results provide a simple first-order particle-scale force law for polymeric binders.

</details>

### [113] [Johnson-Schwartzman Gap Labelling for Metric and Discrete Decorated Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08496)
*Ram Band,Gilad Sofer*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了度量图和离散装饰图上的薛定谔算子，通过证明Johnson-Schwartzman间隙标记定理，将间隙标记理论扩展到一维唯一遍历动力系统生成的图结构，并揭示了图几何驱动间隙闭合的新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在回答度量图和离散装饰图上薛定谔算子的谱间隙中哪些间隙标记（gap labels）可能出现，特别关注由一维唯一遍历动力系统生成的图结构，以扩展经典的Johnson-Schwartzman间隙标记理论。

Method: 采用谱分析方法研究度量图和离散装饰图上的薛定谔算子，证明Johnson-Schwartzman间隙标记定理在两种设置下的有效性。由于图中可能包含环（cycles），无法使用Sturm振荡理论，因此需要不同的谱方法。

Result: 成功将Johnson-Schwartzman间隙标记扩展到标准一维设置之外，分析了特定图族中积分态密度（integrated density of states, IDS）的不连续性，并证明并非每个可容许标记都对应开放的谱间隙。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了由图几何而非底层动力学驱动的间隙闭合机制，表明图结构中的环等几何特征对谱性质有重要影响，扩展了间隙标记理论的应用范围。

Abstract: We study Schrödinger operators on metric and discrete decorated graphs. The values taken by the integrated density of states (IDS) on spectral gaps are called gap labels. A natural question is which gap labels can occur. We answer this for graphs arising from uniquely ergodic one-dimensional dynamical systems by proving Johnson-Schwartzman gap-labelling theorems in both the metric and discrete settings.
  Our results extend Johnson-Schwartzman gap labelling beyond the standard one-dimensional setting. Unlike in one dimension, these graphs may contain cycles, which prevent the use of Sturm oscillation theory and require different spectral methods.
  We also analyze discontinuities of the IDS for certain graph families and show that not every admissible label corresponds to an open spectral gap. This reveals a mechanism of gap closing driven by graph geometry rather than by the underlying dynamics.

</details>

### [114] [Scalable continuous gravitational wave detection in PTA data with non-parametric red noise suppression and optimal pulsar selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07942)
*Yi-Qian Qian,Yan Wang,Soumya D. Mohanty,Siyuan Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种计算高效的频率论方法，用于在脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）数据中探测连续引力波（CGWs），解决了贝叶斯方法因参数数量随PTA规模增长而计算成本过高的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贝叶斯方法在探测连续引力波时面临计算成本过高的问题，其噪声和信号参数数量与脉冲星计时阵列规模成正比，限制了该方法在下一代射电天文设施预期的大型PTA（包含数百颗脉冲星）中的可扩展性。

Method: 该方法结合了自适应样条拟合算法（非参数化抑制红噪声，避免贝叶斯方法中复杂的噪声建模）和一种新颖的优化脉冲星子集选择方案，从而实现了计算效率的提升。

Result: 在基于NANOGrav 15年数据发布的模拟数据集上，该方法性能与贝叶斯分析相当：对于信噪比≈10的CGW信号，使用最优脉冲星选择时相对特征应变误差为1.0%，频率误差为0.072%，而标准贝叶斯分析分别为1.7%和0.16%。同时，该方法分析时间少于5小时，而贝叶斯方法需要1-2天。

Conclusion: 该方法通过多种数据实现和信号参数的严格研究，被确立为一种高效且可扩展的工具，适用于大规模脉冲星计时阵列的连续引力波搜索。

Abstract: Bayesian methods for the detection of continuous gravitational waves (CGWs) in Pulsar Timing Array (PTA) data incur substantial computational costs that grow rapidly due to the number of noise and signal parameters characterizing the fitted model being proportional to the size of the PTA. This computational burden limits the scalability of these methods for large-scale PTAs comprising hundreds of pulsars anticipated from next-generation radio astronomy facilities. In this work, we introduce a computationally efficient frequentist method designed to circumvent this challenge. This is achieved by combining an adaptive spline fitting algorithm that non-parametrically suppresses red noise, thereby eliminating the need for complex noise modeling inherent to Bayesian methods, with a novel scheme for optimizing the subsets of pulsars included in the search. We quantify the performance of our method on a simulated dataset based on the NANOGrav 15-year data release and find that it achieves a performance comparable to that of Bayesian analysis: for a CGW signal with a signal-to-noise ratio of $\approx 10$, our method yields a relative characteristic strain error of 1.0\% and a frequency error of 0.072\% from the injected values by using the optimal pulsar selections, while the same errors are 1.7\% and 0.16\%, respectively, for the standard Bayesian analysis. At the same time, our analysis completes in less than 5 hours, in contrast to the 1-2 days required by Bayesian methods. This allows us to perform a rigorous study of our method using multiple data realizations and signal parameters, establishing it as an efficient and scalable tool for CGW searches with large-scale PTAs.

</details>

Horiguchi,A. Minamino,Y. Sasaki,R. Shibayama,R. Shimamura*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该论文介绍了Super-Kamiokande（SK）中微子观测站对超新星实时监测系统"SNWATCH"的升级，包括新的HEALPix方向重建算法和最大似然拟合器的改进，使超新星警报生成时间缩短至约90秒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 邻近核心坍缩超新星（core-collapse supernova）的多信使天文学研究具有重要科学价值，特别是冲击波爆发（shock breakout）辐射的早期观测对理解超新星爆发机制和前身星性质至关重要。中微子观测站能够在冲击波爆发辐射到达前提供超新星早期警报。

Method: Super-Kamiokande（SK）通过添加钆（gadolinium）升级探测体积，并开发了两种方向重建方法：基于HEALPix的新算法"HP-Fitter"能在1秒内计算超新星方向；改进的最大似然方向拟合器"ML-Fitter"整合了钆中子俘获事件信息，并使用HP-Fitter提供初始拟合参数。

Result: HP-Fitter方向重建时间小于1秒，ML-Fitter具有更好的角分辨率但重建时间为O(秒)量级。结合爆发探测和事件重建时间的改进，SNWATCH系统现在能够在约90秒内生成包含指向信息的超新星警报。这些升级已在SK实施并集成到新的自动化系统中，用于提供GCN通知。

Conclusion: Super-Kamiokande的升级显著提高了超新星方向重建的速度和精度，使SNWATCH系统能够快速提供包含准确指向信息的超新星警报，为多信使天文学研究提供了重要技术支持。

Abstract: The next nearby core-collapse supernova (SN) promises to yield a treasure of scientific information through multi-messenger astronomy. Early observations of the shock breakout (SBO) emissions are especially critical to understand the SN explosive mechanism as well as the properties of the progenitor star. Neutrino observatories are able to provide an early alert of a SN before the arrival of the SBO radiation. Super-Kamiokande (SK) has the unique capability to independently reconstruct an accurate SN pointing direction as part of its real-time monitoring system, ``SNWATCH.'' Recent upgrades to SK by adding gadolinium (Gd) to the detection volume have been accompanied by efforts to improve the speed and accuracy of SN direction reconstruction. A new, novel HEALPix-based approach (``HP-Fitter'') can calculate the SN direction from the reconstructed burst event directions in less than one second. As well, the previous maximum-likelihood direction fitter (``ML-Fitter'') was upgraded by incorporating event information from Gd neutron-capture as well as using the HP-Fitter for the initial fit parameters and from code refactoring and optimization. The improved ML-Fitter has better angular resolution but direction reconstruction time is $\mathcal{O}$(sec). Together with improvements in burst detection and event reconstruction times, SNWATCH is now able to generate an SN alert with pointing information in about 90 seconds. These upgrades have been implemented at SK and integrated into a new automated system to provide GCN notices.

</details>


### [116] [GW190711_030756 and GW200114_020818: astrophysical interpretation of two asymmetric binary black hole mergers in the IAS catalog](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07388)
*Tousif Islam,Tejaswi Venumadhav,Digvijay Wadekar,Ajit Kumar Mehta,Javier Roulet,Jonathan Mushkin,Mark Ho-Yeuk Cheung,Barak Zackay,Matias Zaldarriaga*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究对IAS目录中两个重要的双黑洞并合候选体GW190711_030756和GW200114_020818进行了全面分析，揭示了它们的不对称质量比、高自旋特性以及在不同宿主环境中的残留黑洞保留概率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在深入分析IAS目录中两个具有重要天体物理意义的双黑洞并合候选体，其中GW190711_030756的天体物理起源概率为0.99，GW200114_020818为0.71，信噪比分别约为10.0和13.4。

Method: 采用数值相对论替代模型（numerical relativity surrogate models）来推断这两个候选体的源特性（source properties）和残留特性（remnant properties）。

Result: 发现两个候选体均为不对称质量双星，质量比分别为0.35^{+0.32}_{-0.15}和≤0.20。GW200114_020818的源帧总质量约为220M⊙，具有高自旋黑洞，主次黑洞的无量纲自旋幅值分别为0.96^{+0.03}_{-0.07}和0.84^{+0.13}_{-0.34}，与GW231123_135430相似。该候选体还具有置信的负有效旋进自旋χ_eff=-0.60^{+0.22}_{-0.13}和强自旋进动特性，有效进动参数χ_p=0.60^{+0.21}_{-0.19}。

Conclusion: GW200114_020818（与GW231123_135430一起）指向了一个新兴的大质量、快速自旋双黑洞并合群体。虽然GW231123_135430与球状星团中的并合一致，但在这种环境中产生类似GW200114_020818的系统即使在分层并合情景下也很困难。两个候选体在不同宿主环境中的残留黑洞保留概率存在显著差异。

Abstract: We provide a comprehensive analysis of GW190711_030756 and GW200114_020818, two of the most significant binary black hole merger candidates in the IAS catalog, with probabilities of astrophysical origin $p_{\rm astro}=0.99$ and $0.71$, respectively, and signal-to-noise ratios of approximately $10.0$ and $13.4$. We employ numerical relativity surrogate models to infer both the source properties and the remnant properties of these two candidates. We find that both GW190711_030756 and GW200114_020818 are asymmetric-mass binaries, with inferred mass ratios of $0.35^{+0.32}_{-0.15}$ and $\leq 0.20$. In addition, GW200114_020818 is inferred to have a source-frame total mass of approximately $220M_{\odot}$ and highly spinning black holes, with primary (secondary) dimensionless spin magnitudes of $0.96^{+0.03}_{-0.07}$ ($0.84^{+0.13}_{-0.34}$), closely resembling GW231123_135430. We further find that GW200114\_020818 has a confidently negative effective inspiral spin of $χ_{\rm eff}=-0.60^{+0.22}_{-0.13}$ and exhibits strong spin precession, characterized by an effective precession parameter of $χ_{\rm p}=0.60^{+0.21}_{-0.19}$. GW200114_020818 (when considered alongside GW231123_135430) points towards an emerging population of massive, rapidly spinning BBH mergers. While GW231123_135430 is consistent with mergers in globular clusters, producing systems like GW200114_020818 in such environments remains difficult even under hierarchical merger scenarios. The probability that the remnant black hole of GW190711_030756 (GW200114_020818) is retained in its host environment is $0.079$ ($0.0002$), $0.62$ ($0.965$), and $0.997$ ($1$) if the merger occurred in a globular cluster, a nuclear star cluster, or an elliptical galaxy, respectively.

</details>


### [117] [Accretion-powered flares from black hole-disk collisions in galactic nuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07443)
*Joaquin Pelle,Kyohei Kawaguchi,Masaru Shibata,Alan Tsz-Lok Lam*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个用于黑洞-吸积盘碰撞的相对论流体动力学模拟的辐射后处理框架，预测了不同参数下的光变曲线和光谱能量分布，发现辐射主要由次级黑洞上的超爱丁顿吸积流主导，而非未束缚抛射物的冷却。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞对星系核中吸积盘的撞击可以产生明亮的暂现源，但由于碰撞后流体的高度时变性和非均匀性，预测其可观测特征具有挑战性。需要建立框架来模拟这些过程的辐射特征。

Method: 提出了一个用于黑洞-吸积盘碰撞的相对论流体动力学模拟的辐射后处理框架。该框架采用物理驱动的激波加热处方、通过eikonal求解器计算光学深度，并考虑平流俘获和扩散的光子逃逸分数。

Result: 研究发现辐射主要由次级黑洞上长寿命、高度超爱丁顿（super-Eddington）的吸积流主导，而非未束缚抛射物的冷却。在探索的参数范围内，光度可达次级黑洞爱丁顿光度的数倍，且辐射通常以软X射线为主。较低速度的碰撞产生更亮的耀发，而盘面密度主要控制光谱演化。

Conclusion: 基于结果校准的耗散时间估计表明，中等质量次级黑洞的特征持续时间为数小时至数天，且耀发时间与QPE周期成正比。研究结果对类QPE暂现源和超大质量双黑洞候选体OJ 287具有重要启示。

Abstract: Black hole impacts on accretion disks in galactic nuclei can power luminous transients, but predicting their observable signatures is challenging because the post-collision flow is highly time-dependent and inhomogeneous. We present a radiative post-processing framework for relativistic hydrodynamics simulations of black hole-disk collisions. Using physically motivated prescriptions for shock heating, optical depth via an eikonal solver, and photon escape fractions that account for advection trapping and diffusion, we predict light curves and spectral energy distributions over a range of disk densities and collision velocities. Our results indicate that the emission is dominated by the long-lived, highly super-Eddington accretion flow onto the secondary black hole, rather than by cooling of the unbound ejecta. In the parameter range explored, the luminosity can reach several times the Eddington luminosity of the secondary, and the emission is generically dominated by soft X-rays. We find that lower velocity collisions produce brighter flares, while the disk surface density mainly controls spectral evolution: low-density disks typically produce keV-peaked flares with weak spectral evolution, whereas high-density disks show softer early emission and late-time hardening. A depletion-time estimate calibrated to our results suggests characteristic durations of hours to days for intermediate-mass secondaries, and yields $t_{\rm flare} \propto P_{\rm QPE}$. We discuss implications for QPE-like transients and for the SMBH-binary candidate OJ 287.

</details>


### [118] [The deci-Hz gravitational wave signal from the collapse of rotating very massive stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07878)
*Bailey Sykes,Jade Powell,Bernhard Müller,Alexander Heger*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究计算了在电子对不稳定性（pair-instability）质量上限的300太阳质量旋转恒星坍缩产生的引力波信号，发现其在0.1 Hz频段具有特征波形，可能适用于基于模板的探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索大质量旋转恒星在电子对不稳定性质量上限坍缩时产生的引力波信号特性，特别是其在0.1 Hz探测频段的可探测性。

Method: 通过计算300太阳质量旋转恒星的坍缩过程，分析其大规模不对称性发展对引力波信号的影响，重点关注0.1 Hz频段的信号特征。

Result: 坍缩过程中产生的大规模不对称性在0.1 Hz频段产生强引力波信号，具有特征波形；最先进的0.1 Hz探测器可在200 Mpc距离内探测此类信号，年探测率约为0.5次。

Conclusion: 电子对不稳定性质量上限的大质量旋转恒星坍缩产生的引力波信号具有可识别的特征波形，在0.1 Hz频段具有可探测性，为未来引力波天文学提供了新的探测目标。

Abstract: We calculate the gravitational wave signal from the collapse of a rotating 300 $M_\odot$ star at the upper end of the pair-instability regime. The large-scale asymmetries that develop during the collapse produce a strong signal in the deci-Hz range that has a characteristic shape which is likely amenable to a template-based search. The most ambitious designs for deci-Hz detectors could detect such signals out to distances of 200 Mpc, possibly at a rate of 0.5 per year.

</details>


### [119] [Stochastic problems in pulsar timing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08373)
*Reginald Christian Bernardo*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究利用扩散理论方法，推导了描述脉冲星计时噪声和引力波背景信号的朗之万随机微分方程的解析解，揭示了脉冲星计时信号动力学的物理本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 朗之万随机微分方程（Langevin stochastic differential equations）为脉冲星计时噪声和引力波背景信号提供了动力学描述，且在脉冲星计时阵列分析中具有线性计算复杂度优势。然而，需要解析解来深入理解这些信号的物理本质。

Method: 采用扩散理论（diffusion theory）的既定方法，推导了与红噪声和引力波背景信号相关的朗之万方程的解析解，包括均值、协方差和概率密度函数。研究分析了奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克过程、过阻尼谐振子模型以及中子星双组分模型。

Result: 研究发现，将脉冲星自旋频率建模为奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克过程（Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process）与平稳引力波背景信号在数学上不一致。而过阻尼谐振子（overdamped harmonic oscillator）随机过程则能同时支持平稳自旋频率和相位残差。对于中子星双组分模型，解析解揭示了残差模型中非平稳性的物理起源：系统阻尼本征模和扩散本征模的共存。

Conclusion: 该研究通过推导朗之万方程的解析解，为脉冲星计时信号的动力学提供了直接的物理洞察。这些解不仅揭示了现有模型的内在一致性，还阐明了中子星双组分模型中非平稳性的物理机制，对脉冲星计时阵列分析具有重要意义。

Abstract: Langevin stochastic differential equations provide a dynamical description of pulsar timing noise and gravitational wave background (GWB) signals. They are also central to state space algorithms that have gained traction in pulsar timing array analysis due to their linear computational scaling with the number of observations. In this work, we utilize established methods in diffusion theory to derive analytical solutions (means, covariances, and probability density functions) to Langevin equations relevant to red noise and the GWB signal in pulsars. The solutions give direct physical insight on the dynamics of pulsar timing signals. As a canonical example, we show that the pulsar spin frequency modeled as an Ornstein-Uhlenbeck process is mathematically inconsistent with a stationary GWB signal when the timing residual is the direct observable. The nonstationarity can be partially dealt with by marginalizing over long time deterministic trends in the data. Then, we show that a random process based on an overdamped harmonic oscillator supports both a stationary spin frequency and phase residuals, consistent with a stationary GWB signal. We also turn our attention to a phenomenological model of a neutron star -- a two-component model with spin wandering -- that has been motivated to explain observed timing noise in radio pulsars. We derive analytical expressions for the means, covariances, and cross-covariances of the crust and superfluid rotational states driven by white noise. The associated constant deterministic torques are linked to the quadratic spin-down of pulsars. The solutions reveal the physical origin of nonstationarity in the residual model: the coexistence of damped and diffusive eigenmodes of the system.

</details>


### [120] [Optical images of Kerr-Sen black hole illuminated by thick accretion disks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08439)
*Yu-Kang Wang,Chen-Yu Yang,Xiao-Xiong Zeng*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究了克尔-森（Kerr-Sen）黑洞在几何厚、光学薄的吸积盘照射下的阴影和偏振图像。通过对比两种吸积模型，分析了黑洞自旋、电荷和观测倾角对图像特征的影响，发现电荷增加会使光子环和中心暗区同时收缩，而参考系拖曳则导致亮度不对称性增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究克尔-森黑洞在两种不同几何厚度的吸积盘模型（RIAF和BAAF）照射下的观测特征。重点关注黑洞自旋参数a、电荷Q以及观测者倾角θ对阴影图像和偏振图像的影响，以理解这些物理参数如何通过引力透镜和参考系拖曳效应在观测图像中显现。

Method: 采用两类吸积模型：现象学的辐射无效吸积流（radiatively inefficient accretion flow, RIAF）模型和解析的弹道近似吸积流（ballistic approximation accretion flow, BAAF）模型。基于辐射转移理论，系统研究自旋参数a、黑洞电荷Q和观测倾角θ对阴影图像的影响。

Result: 两种模型均显示，随着电荷Q增加，光子环（photon rings）和中心暗区同时收缩。参考系拖曳（frame dragging）导致显著的亮度不对称性，且随着a和θ增大而更加明显。各向异性辐射（anisotropic radiation）使高阶图像在上下极区更亮。BAAF模型中，由于锥形近似使某些区域几何上更薄，高阶图像的空间范围比RIAF模型更窄，且直接图像与高阶图像的分离更明显。

Conclusion: 偏振图像中，偏振矢量方向的空间分布主要由引力透镜（gravitational lensing）和参考系拖曳决定，而光子环附近的强度和更高阶图像的尺度则显著受电荷Q影响。研究揭示了黑洞电荷、自旋和吸积盘几何结构对观测图像的复杂影响机制。

Abstract: This paper investigates the shadow and polarization images of a Kerr-Sen black hole illuminated by geometrically thick and optically thin accretion disks. We adopt two classes of accretion models, namely the phenomenological radiatively inefficient accretion flow (RIAF) model and the analytical ballistic approximation accretion flow (BAAF) model. Based on radiative transfer theory, we examine the effects of the spin parameter $a$, black hole charge $Q$, and observer inclination angle $θ$ on the shadow images. Both models show that, as the charge $Q$ increases, the photon rings and the central dark regions shrink simultaneously. Meanwhile, frame dragging gives rise to a pronounced brightness asymmetry, which becomes more significant with increasing $a$ and $θ$. The main difference between isotropic and anisotropic radiation is that, in the latter case, the higher order images are brighter in the upper and lower polar regions. For the BAAF model, because the conical approximation renders certain regions geometrically thinner, the spatial extent of the higher order images is narrower than that in the RIAF model, and the separation between the direct image and the higher order images is more distinct. In the polarization images, the spatial distribution of the polarization vector directions is mainly determined by gravitational lensing and frame dragging, whereas the intensity near the photon ring and the scale of the higher order images are significantly influenced by $Q$.

</details>

### [121] [Long-term stability study of single-mask triple GEM detector: impact of continuous irradiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07381)
*S. Mandal,S. Gope,S. Das,S. Biswas*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该研究通过使用$^{55}$Fe放射源与Argon/CO$_2$混合气体，在实验室环境中评估了气体电子倍增器（GEM）室原型的性能稳定性，重点关注探测器增益、效率和能量分辨率在长期连续辐射条件下的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在评估气体电子倍增器（Gas Electron Multiplier, GEM）探测器在长期运行中的性能稳定性，这对于微模式气体探测器（Micro Pattern Gaseous Detectors, MPGD）在大型实验装置中安装前的可靠性验证至关重要。

Method: 研究采用$^{55}$Fe放射源与Argon/CO$_2$混合气体，对GEM探测器原型进行约98天的连续不间断辐射测试。测量参数包括探测器增益、能量分辨率以及环境参数如温度、压力和相对湿度，同时监测强放射源下的计数率长期行为。

Result: 研究获得了GEM探测器在长期连续辐射条件下的性能数据，包括增益、能量分辨率随环境参数的变化规律，以及计数率的长期稳定性特征，为MPGD类探测器的实际应用提供了重要参考依据。

Conclusion: 该工作为微模式气体探测器（MPGD）特别是GEM探测器在大型实验装置中的部署提供了关键的长期稳定性评估，证明了其在连续辐射条件下的性能可靠性，对实际应用具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: A study has been carried out to evaluate the performance stability of Gas Electron Multiplier (GEM) chamber prototypes in the laboratory using $^{55}$Fe radiation source with Argon and CO$_2$ gas mixture. This research focuses on the characterisation of the GEM detector's gain, efficiency (count rate with radioactive source), and energy resolution under varying operational conditions. A patch on the detector has been subjected to continuous and absolutely uninterrupted radiation for about 98 days. The gain and energy resolution of the detector are measured along with the ambient parameters temperature (t), pressure (p) and relative humidity (RH). In addition to that, the long-term behaviour of the count rate with a strong radioactive source are also studied. This work is very relevant for Micro Pattern Gaseous Detectors (MPGD) such as GEM before installing on large experiment. ### [122] [Characterization of afterpulse in SiPMs with single-cell readout as a function of bias voltage and fluence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08308)
*P. Parygin,E. Garutti,E. Popova,J. Schwandt*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用具有单单元读出（single-cell readout）的专用结构，开发了三种独立分析方法：基于电荷积分的方法，以及两种使用多元线性回归（multiple linear regression）重建瞬态波形并精确定位脉冲位置的方法。这些方法通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）进行验证。

Result: 测量了三个SiPM样品：一个未辐照参考器件和两个分别暴露于2e12和1e13 cm^-2反应堆中子通量的辐照器件。在击穿电压以上3-5V的过电压范围内，余脉冲时间常数低于10纳秒，余脉冲概率低于6%。两个参数均未显示出对辐照通量的显著依赖性。

Abstract: We present a detailed investigation of the afterpulse effect in silicon photomultipliers (SiPMs), using a dedicated structure with single-cell readout. This enables direct measurement of intrinsic device properties and observation of individual pulses even after irradiation. Three independent analysis methods to quantify afterpulse induced events were developed and validated by Monte Carlo simulations. The first method is based on charge integration, while the other two methods use multiple linear regression to reconstruct transient waveforms and accurately identify individual pulse positions. These positions are then used either as direct event counts or to construct time interval distributions, enabling comprehensive characterization of the afterpulse probability and providing insights into the dynamics of trapping in silicon. Using this framework, we measured three SiPM samples: one fresh reference device and two irradiated devices exposed to reactor neutron fluences of 2e12 and 1e13 cm^-2. We report systematic measurements of the afterpulse probability and time constant as functions of bias voltage and irradiation fluence. For overvoltages in the range of 3 to 5 V above breakdown, the afterpulse time constant is found to be below 10 ns and the afterpulse probability below 6%. The quantum simulation of the dynamics of confining strings and glueballs, both essential aspects of quark confinement, in a controllable first-principles way is an important step towards this goal. Here, we realize a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ lattice gauge theory in $2+1$D with a tunable plaquette term on a \texttt{Quantinuum System Model H2} trapped-ion quantum computer. We implement a shallow depth-6 Trotter circuit on a $6 \times 5$ matter-site square lattice utilizing all $56$ available qubits to execute over $1000$ entangling gates. We prepare far-from-equilibrium initial string configurations that we quench across a range of parameters to observe rich dynamical phenomena, such as the formation of gauge-invariant closed-loop excitations reminiscent of glueballs in QCD and multi-order string breaking accompanied by spontaneous matter creation. We further demonstrate experimentally that the system displays genuine $2+1$D dynamics, as evidenced by string snapshots over time that cannot be trivially mapped to $1+1$D physics. Our results demonstrate digital quantum simulations of nonequilibrium dynamics in a higher-dimensional lattice gauge theory and provide an experimentally accessible setting for phenomena related to confinement physics.

### [125] [Time-dependent THz dielectric function of ZnTe under two-photon optical excitation at 800 nm wavelength](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08091)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用光学泵浦-太赫兹探测光谱技术（optical pump-THz probe spectroscopy），在不同泵浦通量和泵浦-探测延迟条件下，表征了ZnTe在800 nm激发下的太赫兹介电函数。实验数据通过Drude-Lorentz模型进行分析。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了ZnTe的太赫兹介电函数在800 nm亚带隙激发条件下会发生依赖于激发条件的瞬态演化，这一发现对于优化基于ZnTe的太赫兹产生和检测系统具有重要意义，因为介电函数的瞬态变化直接影响太赫兹产生和检测的效率与带宽。

Abstract: ZnTe is arguably the most widely used nonlinear crystal for the generation and detection of THz radiation, used in conjunction with sub-bandgap optical excitation by femtosecond lasers operating near 800 nm. The THz dielectric function of ZnTe is the key parameter defining the efficiency and bandwidth of THz generation and detection. Here, we demonstrate that the THz dielectric function of ZnTe undergoes substantial transient modification at 800 nm sub-bandgap excitation under conditions typical for THz generation. These modifications arise from significant free-carrier generation via two-photon absorption of the 800 nm pump, accompanied by the pump-driven activation of the THz-active phonon modes. Using optical pump-THz probe spectroscopy, we characterized the THz dielectric function of ZnTe under 800 nm excitation as a function of pump fluence and pump-probe delay. Analysis of the experimental data within the Drude-Lorentz model provided the generated free carrier density and momentum scattering time, and oscillator strength of the pump activated THz phonon modes, revealing their transient evolution in dependence on the excitation conditions.

In this work, we describe the hydroflux synthesis of K$_2$Co$_2$(TeO$_{3}$)$_{3}$ $\cdot$ 2.5 H$_2$O (KCoTOH), a novel zemannite-type antiferromagnet (AFM) possessing structural elements of both triangular dimer and honeycomb structural motifs. We resolve three unique oscillation frequencies from the zero-field $μ$SR spectra, additionally suggesting a remarkably low level of structural disorder in as-grown KCoTOH crystals. Whereas interactions between dimerized chains of Co$^{2+}$ cations are typically observed to be negligible or ferromagnetic in nature, the largely planar ordering motif observed in KCoTOH is instead stabilized by net antiferromagnetic interactions through bridging tellurite groups. This work highlights the potential of hydroflux synthesis methods in the stabilization of magnetic materials possessing novel and potentially more frustrated lattice geometries.

### [128] [Fortuitous Universality of Bose-Kondo Impurities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07554)
*Abhijat Sarma,Zheng Zhou,Ryan A. Lanzetta,Yin-Chen He*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究使用模糊球方法研究玻色-近藤杂质问题，发现不同自旋S的杂质会流向各自稳定的红外共形不动点，这一现象被称为"偶然普适性（fortuitous universality）"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究玻色-近藤（Bose-Kondo）杂质问题，即自旋S杂质与(2+1)维O(3) Wilson-Fisher共形场论（Heisenberg普适类）耦合的系统。探索不同自旋值下杂质的红外行为。

Method: 采用模糊球（fuzzy-sphere）方法，结合大规模精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）技术。研究自旋S=1/2, 1, 3/2的情况。

Result: 对于每个S值，杂质都流向一个独特的稳定相互作用共形缺陷（interacting conformal defect）。观察到整数间隔的缺陷谱，符合缺陷共形对称性，并计算了多个低能缺陷原初算符以及重整化群单调g-函数。

Conclusion: 尽管具有相同的对称性和反常，玻色-近藤杂质会流向不同的稳定红外共形不动点，这一现象被称为"偶然普适性"。预期该现象对所有S值都成立，包括S→∞极限，每个自旋S杂质都流向其自身的稳定红外共形不动点。

Abstract: We use the fuzzy-sphere approach to study the Bose-Kondo impurity problem, namely a spin-$S$ impurity coupled to the $(2+1)$-dimensional $O(3)$ Wilson-Fisher CFT (Heisenberg universality class). We demonstrate that for $S=1/2,1,3/2$ the impurity flows to a distinct stable interacting conformal defect for each $S$. Using large-scale exact diagonalization and density-matrix renormalization group methods, we observe integer-spaced defect spectrum consistent with defect conformal symmetry and compute several low-lying defect primary operators as well as the RG monotonic $g$-function. Our findings show that despite sharing the same symmetry and anomaly, Bose-Kondo impurities flow to distinct stable infrared conformal fixed points, which we refer to as \emph{fortuitous universality}. We expect this fortuitous universality to persist for all $S$, extending to $S\rightarrow\infty$, with each spin-$S$ impurity flowing to its own stable infrared conformal fixed point.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统范霍夫奇点分类仅关注能带梯度在所有方向都消失的临界点，这限制了对其在三维系统中丰富行为的理解。研究旨在建立更全面的分类体系，以涵盖梯度在部分方向消失而其他方向保持有限的非临界奇点。

Method: 研究基于能带梯度消失分量数量和Hessian矩阵本征值特征，建立了包含普通型（M-type）、高阶型（T₁、T₂、T₃）、非临界普通型（N₀、N₁、N₂）和非临界高阶型（S₁、S₂）的统一分类。通过在具有自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的烧绿石晶格（pyrochlore lattice）上构建s轨道紧束缚模型（s-orbital tight-binding model），并通过调控跃迁比（hopping ratio）来验证分类体系。

Result: 非临界范霍夫奇点表现出方向性淬灭（directional quenching）特征：梯度在二维子空间消失，而在正交方向保持有限，产生具有不同能量依赖性的有限态密度增强。所有奇点类别都可在不同高对称点通过控制跃迁比实现，验证了分类体系的完备性。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了方向临界性（directional criticality）和高阶平坦性（higher-order flatness）作为调控三维量子材料中态密度增强的设计原则，为理解和设计相关电子现象提供了新框架。

Abstract: Van Hove singularities (VHSs) play a pivotal role in driving correlated electronic phenomena. Traditional classifications focus only on critical points where the band gradient vanishes in all directions. Here we establish a unified classification of VHSs in three-dimensional systems, characterized by the number of vanishing gradient components and Hessian eigenvalues: ordinary ($M$-type), higher-order ($T_1$, $T_2$, $T_3$), noncritical ordinary ($N_0$, $N_1$, $N_2$), and noncritical higher-order ($S_1$, $S_2$) types. Noncritical VHSs exhibit directional quenching: the gradient vanishes in a two-dimensional subspace while remaining finite along the orthogonal direction, yielding finite density-of-states enhancements with distinct energy dependencies. Using an $s$-orbital tight-binding model on the pyrochlore lattice with spin-orbit coupling, we demonstrate that all singularity classes emerge at distinct high-symmetry points through controlled tuning of the hopping ratio. This work establishes directional criticality and higher-order flatness as design principles for tailoring density-of-states enhancements in three-dimensional quantum materials.

</details>


### [130] [Fluctuation Mechanism of Single-Ion Anisotropy of Topological Insulator MnBi$_2$Te$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07852)
*V. V. Val'kov,A. O. Zlotnikov,A. Gamov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了电子跳跃诱导的电荷涨落与自旋轨道耦合共同作用，能够解除MnBi₂Te₄中Mn离子轨道单重态⁶S的六重简并，产生单离子各向异性，为理解该拓扑绝缘体的磁性各向异性提供了新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释拓扑绝缘体MnBi₂Te₄中观察到的单离子各向异性来源。传统晶体场理论无法充分解释轨道单重态⁶S的简并解除，需要探索新的物理机制。

Method: 引入多重量子态表示法，用原子态费米子的产生算符描述多体波函数间的跃迁。采用二阶微扰理论的算符形式，推导Mn离子⁶S项自旋投影M态占据数n_M的表达式，并确定单离子各向异性常数。

Result: 计算表明涨落机制能够实现MnBi₂Te₄中观察到的易轴各向异性。通过调节模型参数获得的各向异性常数D₂范围包含实验所需的D₂ = -0.0095 meV值，该值能重现自旋翻转转变的临界磁场H_sf。

Conclusion: 提出的涨落机制具有广泛适用性，适用于描述弱晶体场中磁性离子基态为轨道单重态的化合物的各向异性，为理解这类材料的磁性行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: We demonstrate that charge fluctuations induced by electron hopping, combined with spin-orbit coupling, lift the sixfold degeneracy of the orbital singlet $^{6}S$ of Mn ions in the topological insulator MnBi$_2$Te$_4$, resulting in single-ion anisotropy. To solve the problem, a multiplet representation is introduced for the creation operators of atomic-state fermions in terms of the operators describing transitions between many-body wavefunctions. Using the operator form of perturbation theory up to the second order, we derive expressions for the populations $n_M$ of Mn ion states with spin projections $M$ of the $^{6}S$ term and determine the single ion anisotropy constants. The calculations reveal that the fluctuation mechanism ensures the possibility of implementing the easy-axis anisotropy observed in MnBi$_2$Te$_4$. Notably, the range of anisotropy constants $D_2$ obtained by varying the model parameters includes the value $D_2 = -0.0095$ meV, required to reproduce the critical field of the spin-flop transition $H_{\text{sf}}$, known from the experiment. The proposed mechanism has a wide range of applicability for describing the anisotropy in compounds where the ground state of a magnetic ion in a weak crystal field is described by an orbital singlet.

</details>


### [131] [Hubbard vs. Emery model: spectra, transport and relevance for cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08085)
*Jakša Vučičević,Rok Žitko*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究比较了铜基超导体中两种常用模型（单轨道Hubbard模型和三轨道Emery模型）的光谱与输运性质，发现两者物理图像相似但存在定量差异，并通过与实验对比验证了模型的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解铜基超导体的输运性质是强关联电子物理的核心挑战之一。主要不确定性在于模型轨道自由度的选择以及有效耦合的定义，需要确定能够捕捉所有相关机制并提供定量预测的最小模型。

Method: 研究比较了两种最常考虑的模型：单轨道Hubbard模型（single-orbital Hubbard model）和三轨道Emery模型（three-orbital Emery model）。通过分析它们的光谱和输运性质，并与基于La₂CuO₄的三种不同铜酸盐的7个不同实验结果进行比较。

Result: 两种模型呈现相似但不完全相同的物理图像，存在显著的定量差异可用于区分模型。与实验对比显示良好一致性，直流电阻率和有效质量结果表明有效Hubbard模型中的耦合常数比预期更大。发现多个性质对耦合常数精确值敏感，包括Lifshitz转变的临界掺杂和费米能级附近的局域谱权重。

Conclusion: 研究为区分两种模型提供了定量标准，并表明有效Hubbard模型的耦合常数需要重新评估。费米能级附近的局域谱权重可作为未来光电子能谱实验中估计有效耦合常数的有前景方法。

Abstract: Understanding the transport properties of cuprate superconductors is one of the central challenges in the physics of strongly correlated electrons. The most common approach is to define and solve a low-energy lattice model, but it is still unclear what the minimal model is to capture all relevant mechanisms and provide quantitative predictions. The main uncertainty concerns the choice of the orbital degrees of freedom to be included in the model, as well as the definition of the effective coupling. In this paper, we study the two most commonly considered models, namely the single-orbital Hubbard model and the three-orbital Emery model. We investigate and compare their spectral and transport properties, and find that the two models present a similar, but not the same, physical picture. We identify several strong quantitative differences which might allow one to discriminate between the two models by comparing theory with experiments. We compare our results for several physical quantities with 7 different experiments on 3 different La$_2$CuO$_4$-based cuprates, and in general find excellent agreement. The dc resistivity and the effective mass results suggest that the coupling constant in the effective Hubbard model is larger than expected. We find several more properties that are sensitive to the precise value of the coupling constant, including the critical doping for the Lifshitz transition, and the local spectral weight in the vicinity of the Fermi level; the latter provides a promising way to estimate the effective coupling constant in future photoemission experiments.

</details>


### [132] [Co-operating multiorbital and nonlocal correlations in bilayer nickelate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08221)
*Evgeny A. Stepanov,Steffen Bötzel,Ilya M. Eremin,Frank Lechermann*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过先进多体方法分析高压下La₃Ni₂O₇双层镍酸盐的三轨道模型，揭示了轨道间相互作用强度如何决定γ准粒子能带的位置，并发现自旋极化子形成导致费米能级下出现阴影能带。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇高压正常态中多轨道物理与非局域自能效应（nonlocal self-energy effects）的相互作用，以解释近期角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission experiments）实验结果的争议。

Method: 采用有效的三轨道模型（three-orbital model）描述体系，在超越动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）的先进多体框架内求解，捕捉k依赖的关联效应（k-dependent correlations）。

Result: 轨道间相互作用强度微妙地决定低能物理图像：或将著名的平坦γ准粒子能带（flat γ quasiparticle band）置于谱的占据部分，或使其穿越费米能级。后者情况下，电子与顺磁子激发（paramagnon excitations）散射导致自旋极化子形成（spin-polaron formation），产生表现为阴影能带（shadow band）的束缚态，并在费米能级下具有非相干低能谱权重。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了双层镍酸盐中存在的额外竞争态，这些态可能解释近期角分辨光电子能谱实验的争议，为理解该体系复杂的多轨道关联物理提供了新视角。

Abstract: The interplay of multiorbital physics and nonlocal self-energy effects is studied within an effective three-orbital model for the high-pressure normal state of superconducting bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$. The model is solved within an advanced many-body framework capturing $k$-dependent correlations beyond dynamical mean-field theory. Different low-energy scenarios subtly depend on the strength of the interorbital interaction, either placing the notorious flat $γ$ quasiparticle band in the occupied part of the spectrum, or letting it cross the Fermi level. In the latter case, intriguing spin-polaron formation due to the scattering of electrons with paramagnon excitations takes place. This leads to bound states appearing as a shadow band with incoherent low-energy spectral weight below the Fermi level. Our results uncover additional competing states that exist in bilayer nickelates and could explain the controversy of recent angle-resolved photoemission experiments.

</details>


### [133] [Orbital-Selective $d$-wave Superconductivity in the Two-Band $t$-$J$ Model: Possible Applications to La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08319)
*Zhan Wang,Kun Jiang,Fu-Chun Zhang,Hui-Ke Jin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过变分蒙特卡洛方法发现，在包含巡游轨道和准局域轨道的双带t-J模型中，d波超导态仅从巡游轨道中产生，而准局域轨道通过形成局域轨道间束缚态来竞争并抑制超导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究受到镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇中超导现象的启发，旨在探究超越单带t-J框架的多轨道物理在超导中的关键作用，特别是不同轨道类型对超导态的影响。

Method: 采用变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）方法研究双带t-J模型，该模型包含一个巡游轨道（orbital-0）和一个准局域轨道（orbital-1）。

Result: 研究发现轨道选择性d波超导态仅从巡游轨道中产生；准局域轨道通过形成局域轨道间束缚态与超导竞争，这些束缚态作为能量缺陷破坏相位相干性；超导序参数随轨道-1占据数的增加而单调抑制。

Conclusion: 研究强调了超越单带t-J框架的多轨道物理在超导中的关键作用，并指出提高临界温度Tc的具体途径：抑制局域化dz²衍生轨道的参与。

Abstract: We investigate superconductivity in a two-band $t$-$J$ model consisting of an itinerant orbital (orbital-0) and a quasi-localized orbital (orbital-1) using variational Monte Carlo. A robust orbital-selective $d$-wave superconducting state is found to emerge exclusively from the itinerant orbital. An analysis of the superexchange energy hierarchy shows that the quasi-localized orbital-1 competes with superconductivity by favoring local inter-orbital bound states, which act as energy defects and disrupt phase coherence. Consistently, the superconducting order parameter is monotonically suppressed as the occupancy of orbital-1 increases. Motivated by superconductivity in nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, these results highlight the essential role of multi-orbital physics beyond the single-band $t$-$J$ framework and point to a concrete route to enhance $T_c$: suppressing the involvement of localized $d_{z^2}$-derived orbitals.

</details>


### [134] [Revealing the nature of the charge density wave order of ErTe$_3$ via Raman scattering under anisotropic strain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08440)
*Theotime Freitas,Mattia Udina,Alexandr Alekhin,Niloufar Nilforoushan,Sarah Houver,Alain Sacuto,Benito A. Gonzalez,Ian R. Fisher,Indranil Paul,Yann Gallais*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过偏振分辨拉曼散射研究ErTe₃电荷密度波（CDW）序参量性质，发现单分量CDW序参量能解释观测到的镜面对称破缺，反驳了铁轴多分量序参量模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究三碲化铒（ErTe₃）中电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）序参量的本质特性，特别是针对近期提出的铁轴多分量序参量（ferro-axial multi-component order）模型进行验证。

Method: 采用偏振分辨拉曼散射（polarization-resolved Raman scattering）技术，在施加各向异性应变（anisotropic strain）条件下，利用CDW振幅模（amplitude mode）追踪与CDW序相关的镜面对称破缺（mirror-symmetry breakings）。

Result: 研究发现镜面对称破缺随应变和温度变化而相互关联，这与铁轴多分量序参量模型相矛盾。相反，具有偏离主晶轴（principle crystallographic axis）的序波矢（ordering wavevector）的单分量CDW序参量能够重现观测到的镜面对称破缺及其在对称分辨拉曼光谱中的表现。

Conclusion: ErTe₃中的CDW序参量本质为单分量，其序波矢偏离主晶轴方向，而非近期提出的铁轴多分量序参量模型，这为理解该材料的对称性破缺行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: The nature of charge density wave (CDW) order parameter of the tritelluride ErTe$_3$ is investigated by polarization-resolved Raman scattering under anisotropic strain. We show that the CDW amplitude mode can be used to track the mirror-symmetry breakings associated with the CDW order. The mirror-symmetry breakings are found to track each other as a function of strain and temperature arguing against the recently proposed ferro-axial multi-component order. Instead, we show that a single component CDW order parameter with an ordering wavevector tilted away from the principle crystallographic axis can reproduce the observed mirror symmetry breakings and their manifestation in the symmetry-resolved Raman spectra.

</details>

### [135] [Stability of Supported Pd-based Ethanol Oxidation Reaction Electrocatalysts in Alkaline Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07483)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用扫描流动池（scanning flow cell, SFC）耦合在线电感耦合等离子体质谱（online ICP-MS）在宽电位窗口评估溶解稳定性。使用旋转圆盘电极（rotating disk electrode, RDE）进行有无乙醇的加速应力测试，并通过非原位ICP-MS分析溶解产物。采用模拟燃料电池实际运行条件的电位分布。

Conclusion: PdSn/C和PdFe3O4/C电催化剂因其改善的活性和溶解稳定性而适用于碱性直接乙醇燃料电池（ADLFC）应用。催化剂设计时必须同时考虑添加剂对反应动力学的促进作用和其自身的溶解稳定性，以避免如Nb添加剂那样反而破坏整体催化剂稳定性的情况。

Abstract: This study evaluates the dissolution of the supported electrocatalysts Pd/C, PdSn/C, PdNb/C, and PdFe3O4/C during ethanol oxidation reaction for ADLFC applications. A scanning flow cell (SFC) coupled to an inductively coupled mass spectrometry (online ICP-MS) is used to assess the dissolution stability in a broad potential window. Accelerated stress tests with and without ethanol are developed using a rotating disk electrode (RDE) with dissolution products analysis by ex-situ ICP-MS. Potential profiles simulating those experienced by the catalyst during regular fuel cell operation were used. Sn and Fe catalysts demonstrate improved activity and stability compared with the material with Pd alone. For these reasons, PdSn/C and PdFe3O4/C are suitable for ADLFC applications. Severe Nb dissolution destabilizes Pd, increasing its leaching. This work demonstrates that while additional metals and oxides can improve the alcohol oxidation kinetics of Pd, these additives' dissolution stability must already be considered at the catalyst design stage.

*Pete E. Lauer,Kensuke Hayashi,Yuichiro Kunai,Ondřej Wojewoda,Jan Klíma,Ekaterina Pribytova,Michal Urbánek,Aubrey Penn,Takayuki Kikuchi,Renzhi Ma,Takayoshi Sasaki,Takaaki Taniguchi,Caroline A. Ross*

Abstract: Multifunctional materials can exhibit emergent behavior from the coupling of two or more different properties. For example, coupling between magnetic and ferroelectric order enables electrical control of the magnetic state, enabling for example magnetoelectric memory or logic devices that combine the nonvolatility of magnetic order with the energy efficiency of voltage control. Magnetic iron garnets have outstanding magnonic and magnetooptical properties making them valuable in a range of technologies, but they have not been successfully incorporated into thin film two-phase magnetoelectric nanocomposites. Taking advantage of heterogeneously patterned substrates, this work demonstrates the engineering of garnet-perovskite composites in which both phases are polymorphs with the same composition but dramatically different structures and properties. Applying an electric field to the perovskite phase modulates the magnon dispersion and magnetooptical response of the garnet, opening a path to voltage-controlled garnet devices.

### [137] [Impact of charge transition levels on grain boundary properties in acceptor doped oxide ceramics: A phase-field study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07545)
*Kai Wang,Sangjun Kang,Mahmoud Serour,Roger A. De Souza,Andreas Klein,Rotraut Merkle,Wolfgang Rheinheimer,Christian Kübel,Lijun Zhang,Karsten Albe,Bai-Xiang Xu*
