<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先进掺杂策略通过调控体缺陷化学和界面空间电荷层（space-charge-layer, SCL）行为来实现氧化物陶瓷功能化。电荷跃迁能级（charge transition levels, CTLs）在其中起核心作用，其对齐控制体缺陷化学，其在SCL内的弯曲诱导额外电荷态转变。因此，将CTLs纳入模型对于一致描述缺陷平衡和SCL形成至关重要。

Method: 本研究提出了一个与电荷跃迁能级（CTLs）显式耦合的缺陷化学一致相场模型（defect-chemistry-consistent phase-field model）。该模型包含多价氧空位、多价受主掺杂剂、电子和空穴，应用于Fe掺杂SrTiO3体系，涵盖广泛的氧分压和温度范围。

Result: 模拟捕获了静止晶界的对称SCL和迁移过程中的不对称SCL。在迁移过程中出现了慢速和快速两种不同的晶界类型，与实验观察一致。CTL调控的体缺陷化学与SCL内CTL诱导的电荷态转变共同决定了SCL特性。CTL介导的空穴传输显著快于受主掺杂剂扩散，调控溶质拖曳和晶界动力学。

Conclusion: 该模型预测晶界性质同时依赖于热历史和晶界类型，慢速和快速晶界表现出不同的行为。该框架将缺陷化学、费米能级、CTLs和晶界动力学联系起来，为设计具有定制性能的氧化物陶瓷提供了新见解。

Abstract: Advanced doping strategies enable oxide ceramic functionalities by tailoring bulk defect chemistry and space-charge-layer (SCL) behavior at interfaces. Charge transition levels (CTLs), defined as the Fermi level at which a defect changes its stable charge state, play a central role. Their alignment governs bulk defect chemistry, while their bending within SCLs induces additional charge-state transitions. Incorporating CTLs is therefore essential for a consistent description of defect equilibria and SCL formation. In this work, we propose a defect-chemistry-consistent phase-field model explicitly coupled with CTLs to investigate their role in SCL evolution. The model includes multivalent oxygen vacancies, multivalent acceptor dopants, electrons, and holes. It is applied to Fe-doped SrTiO3 over wide ranges of oxygen partial pressure and temperature, capturing both symmetric SCLs at stationary grain boundaries and asymmetric SCLs during migration. Two distinct grain boundary types, slow and fast boundaries, emerge during migration, consistent with experimental observations. Simulations reveal that CTL-governed bulk defect chemistry, together with CTL-induced charge-state transitions within SCLs, critically determine SCL characteristics. Moreover, CTL-mediated hole transport is significantly faster than acceptor dopant diffusion, modulating solute drag and grain boundary kinetics. Finally, the model predicts grain boundary properties dependent on both thermal history and boundary type, with slow and fast boundaries exhibiting distinct behaviors. This framework links defect chemistry, Fermi level, CTLs, and grain boundary kinetics, providing new insights for designing oxide ceramics with tailored properties.

</details>


### [138] [Optomagnetic non-thermal modification of the ferromagnetic resonance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07555)

Motivation: 研究旨在探究线性偏振光通过逆Cotton-Mouton效应（inverse Cotton-Mouton effect, ICME）对磁体中铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance, FMR）频率的光致偏移作用。这一研究动机源于理解光与磁系统相互作用的基本机制，以及探索利用光控制磁共振的可能性。

Method: 采用磁化动力学的拉格朗日（Lagrangian）描述方法，推导运动方程并获得面内（in-plane）和面外（out-of-plane）平衡构型下共振频率的解析表达式。通过理论分析与数值模拟相结合，并与铋取代钇铁石榴石（bismuth-substituted yttrium iron garnet）的实验数据进行对比验证。

Result: 理论表明铁磁共振频率依赖于光的偏振角和传播方向，逆Cotton-Mouton效应产生的频率偏移可主导热效应。解析结果与数值模拟及实验数据吻合良好，能够估算ICME的贡献量，证实了线性偏振光通过磁光效应控制铁磁共振的可行性。

Conclusion: 研究发现线性偏振光可通过逆Cotton-Mouton效应有效控制铁磁共振频率，该效应产生的频率偏移显著且可超越热效应。这一发现为利用磁光效应进行磁共振的光学调控提供了理论基础和实验验证。

Abstract: We investigate the photoinduced shift of the ferromagnetic resonance (FMR) frequency in magnets caused by the inverse Cotton-Mouton effect (ICME) under linearly polarized light. Using a Lagrangian description of magnetization dynamics, we derive the equations of motion, and obtain analytical expressions for the resonance frequency in both in-plane and out-of-plane equilibrium configurations. The theory shows that the FMR frequency depends on the polarization angle and propagation direction of light, with ICME producing a frequency shift that can dominate over thermal effects. The analytical results agree well with numerical simulations and with available experimental data for bismuth-substituted yttrium iron garnet, enabling estimation of the ICME contribution. These findings demonstrate that linearly polarized light can be used to control ferromagnetic resonance through magneto-optical effects.

### [139] [Strain continuously rotates the Néel vector in altermagnetic MnTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07653)
*Alex Liebman-Peláez,Jon Kruppe,Resham Babu Regmi,Nirmal J. Ghimire,Yue Sun,Igor I. Mazin,Hilary M. L. Noad,James Analytis,Veronika Sunko,Joseph Orenstein*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 应变作为交变磁体（altermagnets）的关键调控参数备受关注，但现有研究对如何通过应变和磁场组合实现单畴态的机制尚不明确。需要澄清应变对奈尔矢量取向的具体作用机制。

Method: 采用磁光测量技术对施加应变的MnTe单晶进行研究，分析应变对奈尔矢量取向的影响。同时考察自由支撑晶体中内建应变对奈尔矢量的钉扎效应。

Result: 应变主要作用是连续旋转奈尔矢量L，而非诱导单畴态。奈尔矢量取向决定了磁点群对称性（magnetic point group symmetry），因此这种连续旋转可有效调控对称性及相关物理性质。自由支撑晶体中的内建应变足以在毫米尺度上钉扎奈尔矢量形成连续织构。

Abstract: Altermagnetism has recently emerged as a distinct class of collinear antiferromagnets that break time-reversal symmetry, exhibiting a host of novel properties. Applied strain has attracted particular attention as a key tuning parameter for altermagnets. Although several experimental studies have demonstrated the preparation of single-domain states through a combination of applied strain and magnetic field, the route to such states remains unclear. Here, we use magneto-optical measurements on single crystals of MnTe under applied strain to show that, in contrast to previous reports, strain acts primarily to rotate the Néel vector L continuously. Since the orientation of L determines the magnetic point group symmetry, this continuous rotation effectively tunes the symmetry and its associated physical properties. Furthermore, we demonstrate that built-in strain in free-standing crystals is sufficient to pin L into continuous textures over millimeter length scales. Together, these results provide guidance for future device design and open the door to leveraging the Néel vector orientation as a tunable degree of freedom in spintronic applications.

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了iTMDs作为自旋电子学（spintronics）的多功能平台，并为加速设计对称性增强量子材料（symmetry-enforced quantum materials）提供了通用策略。

Abstract: The advancement of antiferromagnetic spintronics depends on quantum materials with target symmetry-dictated functionalities, however, their systematic discovery is hindered by the immense configurational complexity of the available material space. Based on fully intercalated transition metal dichalcogenides (iTMDs) and using only 200 relaxed partially intercalated structures for transfer learning, our model effectively explores more than 100,000 partially intercalated configurations and identifies 35 altermagnetic and 20 $Tτ$-antiferromagnetic ground-state candidates. ### [142] [Differentiable hybrid force fields support scalable autonomous electrolyte discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07979)
*Xintian Wang,Junmin Chen,Zhuoying Zhu,Peichen Zhong*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出可微分混合力场（differentiable hybrid FFs）作为解决电解质自主发现中速度、精度和可校准性三重困境的解决方案，通过融合物理函数形式与神经网络短程修正，实现高通量筛选和实验可校准的闭环发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电解质自主发现需要满足三重困境（trilemma）的计算引擎：高通量筛选的速度、定量性质预测的精度以及在线细化的可校准性。经典经验力场（empirical force fields）虽快但依赖误差抵消，而标准机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials）计算昂贵、缺乏严格长程物理且难以基于梯度校准。

Method: 提出可微分混合力场（differentiable hybrid FFs），融合物理驱动的函数形式与神经网络短程修正。基于能量分解分析（Energy Decomposition Analysis），如PhyNEO-Electrolyte和ByteFF-Pol等先进模型，通过可微分分子动力学（differentiable molecular dynamics）实现双校准范式：自下而上的从头算参数化与自上而下的宏观实验观测值微调相结合。

Result: 该架构实现零样本泛化（zero-shot generalization）到体相，在10,000原子系统中达到约数十纳秒/天的通量（最高约50纳秒/天，取决于模型复杂度）。物理骨架提供了良好条件的参数空间，支持基于梯度的校准，满足"化学机器人就绪"数字孪生（ChemRobot-ready digital twin）的要求。

Conclusion: 可微分混合力场通过整合物理基础模拟与实验可校准细化，解决了电解质自主发现的三重困境，实现了闭环自主电解质发现，为构建化学机器人就绪的数字孪生提供了可行架构。

Abstract: Autonomous electrolyte discovery demands a computational engine that satisfies a critical trilemma: it must be fast enough for high-throughput screening, accurate enough for quantitative property prediction, and calibratable enough for online refinement. Classical empirical force fields (FFs) are fast but rely heavily on error cancellation, while standard machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) are computationally expensive, lack rigorous long-range physics, and resist gradient-based calibration. In this Perspective, we highlight that differentiable hybrid FFs resolve this trilemma by fusing physically motivated functional forms with neural-network short-range corrections. Grounded in Energy Decomposition Analysis (EDA), state-of-the-art models such as PhyNEO-Electrolyte and ByteFF-Pol achieve zero-shot generalization to bulk phases, delivering throughputs on the order of tens of ns/day (up to $\sim$50 ns/day, depending on model complexity) for 10,000-atom systems. Crucially, their physical skeletons provide a well-conditioned parameter space for differentiable molecular dynamics (dMD). This enables a dual-calibration paradigm: bottom-up \textit{ab initio} parameterization combined with top-down fine-tuning from macroscopic experimental observables. We propose that this architecture meets the requirements of a ``ChemRobot-ready'' digital twin by integrating physics-grounded simulation with experimentally calibratable refinement, thereby enabling closed-loop autonomous electrolyte discovery.

The complex dielectric function is analyzed to explore their optical response, revealing strong absorption in the infrared and visible regions, indicating suitability for optoelectronic applications. Thermoelectric properties, including the Seebeck coefficient, electrical conductivity, and figure of merit (ZT), are evaluated over a temperature range of 30 to 800 K. The relatively small bandgaps contribute to enhanced thermoelectric performance, reflected in improved power factors. Furthermore, photocatalytic analysis indicates that Li2InBiX6 compounds are suitable candidates for water oxidation reactions within the pH range of 0 to 7. Overall, the combined thermoelectric and optical performance highlights these double perovskite halides as promising materials for future energy conversion applications.

### [144] [Emergence of Lissajous trajectories in skyrmion oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08073)
*Tamali Mukherjee,V Satya Narayana Murthy*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过施加交流电流脉冲驱动Co/Pt薄膜中的斯格明子（skyrmion），发现其在特定电流和频率范围内表现出受迫振荡器（forced oscillator）行为，并在x-y平面形成利萨如图形（Lissajous figures）。温度升高导致斯格明子偏离理想路径，产生变形图形。

Motivation: 理解电流驱动斯格明子的动力学特性对其实际应用至关重要。本研究旨在探究交流电流脉冲作用下斯格明子的运动行为，并分析温度对其运动轨迹的影响。

Method: 在Co/Pt薄膜的自由层施加两种交流电流脉冲：(a) x方向脉冲，(b) x和y方向脉冲。电流密度范围为1×10¹¹至1×10¹² A/m²，频率范围为5×10⁸至1×10¹⁰ Hz。通过比较T=0 K和T>0 K条件下的结果，分析温度效应。

Result: 斯格明子在特定参数范围内表现出受迫振荡器行为，跟随正弦电流脉冲运动。对于(A₁sinω₁t, A₂sin(ω₂t+φ), 0)形式的电流脉冲，斯格明子在x-y平面形成利萨如图形。温度升高导致斯格明子偏离T=0 K时的路径，产生变形的利萨如图形。

Conclusion: 斯格明子在交流电流驱动下表现出类似经典力学的振荡行为，但温度通过影响斯格明子霍尔角（θ_{SkH}）和随机热涨落（F^{Th}）导致运动轨迹偏离理想状态。这一发现对基于斯格明子的器件设计具有重要意义。

Abstract: Understanding the dynamics of current-driven skyrmion is essential for their practical applications. In this study, we apply an AC current pulse (a) in x-- direction, and (b) in both x-- and y-- directions through the free layer of a Co/Pt thin film and investigate the motion of the skyrmion. We show that the skyrmion follows the sinusoidal current pulse and behaves like a forced oscillator in the range of current amplitude 1 $\times$ 10$^{11}$ A/m$^2$ to 1 $\times$ 10$^{12}$ A/m$^2$ and frequency 5 $\times$ 10$^{8}$ Hz to 1 $\times$ 10$^{10}$ Hz. For current pulse of (A$_1$sin$ω_1$t, A$_2$sin($ω_2$t+$φ$), 0), the skyrmion forms Lissajous figures in the x-y plane, same as observed in classical mechanics. The results are compared at T = 0 K and T $>$ 0 K to analyze the effect of temperature. As the skyrmion Hall angle ($θ_{SkH}$) and stochastic thermal fluctuation ($\textbf{F}^{Th}$) are functions of temperature, the skyrmion starts deviating from its path at T = 0 K with increasing temperature and eventually generates somewhat deformed Lissajous figures from ideal.

However, the incorporation of Pd and Au into the Ag matrix did not significantly alter the reaction mechanism. During GOR, the in situ FTIR studies demonstrated that catalyst composition influences the oxidation pathways: Pd-rich surfaces favor oxalate formation, while a significant presence of Ag promotes deeper oxidation (up to carbonate), with the AgPdAu ternary catalyst exhibiting intermediate behavior. One key benefit is the lower susceptibility of Ag to irreversible adsorption of reaction byproducts, which enhances electrocatalyst durability. Thus, surface segregation of Ag at high potentials can modify the catalytic surface reactivity, affecting both stability and efficiency.

However, multiple gene combinations can yield equally accurate SISSO models, with individual genes contributing with different weights. Here, we establish a derivative-based sensitivity analysis that resolves the non-uniqueness of symbolic-regression descriptions, enhances interpretability, thereby enabling deeper physical insight. To assess this hypothesis, we perform molecular dynamics simulations of CO$_2$ hydrate nucleation. First, we place hydrate seeds at different positions relative to the interface and monitor their evolution, finding that seeds embedded in the bulk are more likely to grow than those located near or at the interface. Second, we analyse spontaneous nucleation simulations with and without an interface. Our previous work showed that nucleation rates are indistinguishable in both systems, strongly indicating that the interface does not play a role. Here, trajectory analysis reveals that hydrates nucleate in regions of locally high CO$_2$ concentration, which arise spontaneously in the bulk and are not associated with the interface. Our results indicate that hydrate nucleation does not preferentially occur at the interface, at least at the at deep supercooling conditions explored in this work. ### [151] [Odd-parity Magnetism from the Generalized Bloch Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08233)
*Mikkel Christian Larsen,Thomas Olsen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文提出使用广义布洛赫定理（Generalized Bloch theorem）解决螺旋磁体（helimagnets）理论描述中的困难，通过原胞（primitive unit cell）描述系统，并在倒易空间（reciprocal space）中通过降维（downfolding）获取所有相关性质。以MnI₂、NiI₂和MnTe₂为例，分析了自旋劈裂（spin splitting）与能带轨道成分的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 螺旋磁体（helimagnets）的理论描述面临挑战，因为螺旋螺距（spiral pitch）可能需要大超胞（super cells）或甚至与晶格不相称（incommensurate）。在非相对论极限下，螺旋磁序总是与奇宇称磁性（odd-parity magnetism）相关，这意味着可以通过电场直接控制自旋。

Method: 采用广义布洛赫定理（Generalized Bloch theorem），允许通过原胞（primitive unit cell）描述系统，并通过在倒易空间（reciprocal space）中的降维（downfolding）过程获取所有相关性质。以MnI₂、NiI₂（已知的II型多铁性材料）和螺旋磁性金属MnTe₂为例进行演示。

Result: 分析了自旋劈裂（spin splitting）的大小如何依赖于能带的轨道成分，发现自旋劈裂在具有大奇轨道（odd-orbital，p型）特征的态中最大化。该方法可以推广到处理螺旋磁体的响应函数（response functions）。

Conclusion: 广义布洛赫定理和降维程序可以解决螺旋磁体理论描述中的困难，仅使用原胞就能描述系统，从而极大地促进了该领域的理论进展。该方法为螺旋磁体的理论研究提供了有效的计算框架。

Abstract: In the non-relativistic limit, helimagnetic order is always associated with odd-parity magnetism. That is, for single-particle states the expectation value of the electronic spin is odd in crystal momentum, which implies direct control of the spin by means of electric fields. However, the theoretical description of helimagnets is hindered by the fact that the spiral pitch may require large super cells or even be incommensurate with the lattice. In the this letter we show that such issues may be remedied by use of the Generalized Bloch theorem. It allows one to describe (by models or first principles) the system in terms of the primitive unit cell, from which all relevant properties can be obtained by downfolding in reciprocal space. We exemplify the procedure using MnI$_2$ and NiI$_2$, which are known type II multiferroics having spiral order and the helimagnetic metal MnTe$_2$. We analyze how the magnitude of spin splitting depends on orbital composition of bands, and we show that spin splitting is maximized for states having large odd-orbital ($p$-type) character. It is straightforward to generalize the framework to handle response functions for helimagnets using only the primitive unit cell and the present downfolding procedure thus strongly facilitate theoretical progress in the field.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声催化（sonocatalysis）与光催化（photocatalysis）的结合为克服传统光催化系统中电荷载流子快速复合问题提供了有效策略。尽管两种过程机制不同常被分开处理，但它们的组合能创建高效协同系统，用于高级废水处理。

Method: 研究采用铜掺杂的LaFeO3钙钛矿（perovskite）纳米颗粒作为催化剂，在超声和光照射协同条件下进行甲基橙（MO）的声光催化（sonophotocatalytic）降解实验。通过清除剂实验（scavenger experiments）进行机理研究。

Result: 铜掺杂催化剂表现出优异性能，在协同超声和光照射下，降解速率达0.0455 min⁻¹，120分钟内完全去除甲基橙。观察到强协同效应，协同指数约为10。催化剂在连续四个循环中保持高效率和良好稳定性。

Conclusion: 铜掺杂LaFeO3相比未掺杂材料具有更优的声光催化活性，证明了协同声光催化过程在高效污染物去除方面的潜力。机理研究表明羟基自由基和光生空穴是主要的降解活性物种，并基于此提出了合理的反应路径。

Abstract: The integration of sonocatalysis with photocatalysis offers a powerful strategy for advanced wastewater treatment by overcoming rapid charge carrier recombination in conventional photocatalytic systems. Although these processes are often treated separately due to their distinct mechanisms, their combination creates a highly efficient synergistic system. In this study, we investigate the sonophotocatalytic degradation of methyl orange (MO) using Cu-doped LaFeO3 perovskite nanoparticles. The Cu doped catalyst demonstrated excellent performance, achieving a degradation rate of 0.0455 min-1 and complete removal of MO within 120 minutes under combined ultrasonic and light irradiation. A strong synergistic effect was observed, with a synergy index of approximately 10, highlighting the enhanced interaction between sonocatalysis and photocatalysis. The catalyst also exhibited good stability and reusability, maintaining high efficiency over four consecutive cycles. Mechanistic studies using scavenger experiments revealed that hydroxyl radicals and photogenerated holes are the main reactive species responsible for degradation. A plausible reaction pathway is proposed based on these findings. Overall, Cu doped LaFeO3 shows superior sonophotocatalytic activity compared to the undoped material, demonstrating the potential of synergistic sonophotocatalytic processes for efficient pollutant removal.

### [153] [2D Ferroelectric Ruddlesden-Popper Perovskites: an Emerging Fully Electronically Controllable Shift Current and Persistent Spin Helix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08360)
*Yue Zhao,Fu Li,Vikrant Chaudhary,Hongbin Zhang,Gaoyang Gou,Niuzhuang Yang,Yue Hao,Wenyi Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理计算系统分析了三种C2v对称性Ruddlesden-Popper铁电钙钛矿的结构畸变与功能响应关系，发现其位移电流强度可与传统铁电氧化物媲美甚至更高，并识别出C2v对称性保护的自旋纹理，为高性能自旋电子-光伏集成器件设计提供指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维杂化有机-无机钙钛矿（2D HOIPs）是下一代光电子和自旋电子应用的有前景候选材料。本研究旨在系统探究C2v对称性Ruddlesden-Popper铁电钙钛矿中结构畸变与功能响应之间的关系。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合不可约表示分解（irreducible representation decomposition）和波矢点群对称性（wave-vector point-group symmetry, WPGS）分析，系统研究了三种C2v对称性Ruddlesden-Popper铁电钙钛矿：(4,4-DFPD)₂PbI₄、(DFCHA)₂PbI₄和PEPI。

Result: 铅-碘框架产生的位移电流（shift-current, SC）强度可与传统铁电氧化物媲美，PEPI最高达69.16 μA/V²。SC强度与八面体畸变指数（Di）正相关，同时发现共价键强度与结构不对称性之间的竞争机制。在自旋电子学方面，识别出C2v对称性保护的持久自旋纹理（persistent spin textures, PST），单斜晶系(4,4-DFHHA)₂PbI₄中观察到向C2保护准PST的转变，形成具有长距离自旋输运的持久自旋螺旋（persistent spin helix, PSH）。

Conclusion: 铁电性、位移电流和持久自旋纹理之间的协同作用实现了对光电流方向和自旋构型的非易失性电控制。该工作为设计高性能集成自旋电子-光伏器件提供了评估标准和实践指导。

Abstract: Two-dimensional (2D) hybrid organic--inorganic perovskites (HOIPs) are promising candidates for next-generation optoelectronic and spintronic applications. This work systematically investigates the relationship between structural distortions and functional responses in three $C_{2v}$-symmetric Ruddlesden--Popper (RP) ferroelectric perovskites, $(4,4\text{-DFPD})_{2}\mathrm{PbI}_{4}$, $(\mathrm{DFCHA})_{2}\mathrm{PbI}_{4}$, and PEPI, using first-principles calculations combined with irreducible representation decomposition and wave-vector point-group symmetry (WPGS) analysis. The results reveal that the lead--iodide framework yields shift-current (SC) magnitudes comparable to, and in specific cases even an order of magnitude larger than, those of traditional ferroelectric oxides, with PEPI reaching a maximum of $69.16\ μ\mathrm{A}/\mathrm{V}^{2}$. The SC magnitude correlates positively with the octahedral distortion index ($D_i$), while a competition mechanism is identified between covalent bond strength and structural asymmetry, where increased average bond lengths can offset the enhancement induced by $D_i$. Regarding spintronics, $C_{2v}$ symmetry-protected persistent spin textures (PST) are identified. A transition to $C_2$-protected quasi-PST occurs in monoclinic $(4,4\text{-DFHHA})_{2}\mathrm{PbI}_{4}$, leading to a persistent spin helix (PSH) with long-distance spin transport. The synergy among ferroelectricity, SC, and PST enables nonvolatile electrical control of both photocurrent direction and spin configurations. This work provides evaluation criteria and practical guidance for designing high-performance integrated spintronic--photovoltaic devices.

### [154] [Comparative high-pressure study on rare-earth entropy fluorite-type oxides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08371)
*Pablo Botellaa,David Vie,Leda Kolarek,Neha Bura,Peijie Zhang,Anna Herlihy,Dominik Daisenberger,Catalin Popescu,Daniel Errandonea*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文比较了两种萤石型稀土氧化物的高压行为：(CePr)O₂-δ和(CePrLa)O₂-δ。研究发现两者在高压下保持立方萤石结构，但在9-16 GPa出现异常行为，表现为压缩平台和振动模式变化。高熵体系(CePrLa)O₂-δ在22 GPa以上出现非晶化，表明其结构稳定性降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究构型熵（configurational entropy）增加对萤石型稀土氧化物高压结构稳定性的影响。通过比较两种不同熵值的体系，揭示构型熵、阳离子尺寸和压力之间的复杂相互作用如何决定稀土高熵氧化物的结构稳定性。

Method: 采用同步辐射粉末X射线衍射（synchrotron-based powder X-ray diffraction）和拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）技术，分别对(CePr)O₂-δ和(CePrLa)O₂-δ进行高压研究。X射线衍射实验压力达到30 GPa，拉曼光谱实验压力达到20 GPa。

Result: 两种化合物在整个压力范围内保持立方萤石结构，但在9-16 GPa区间观察到异常行为，表现为压缩平台和振动模式变化。高熵体系(CePrLa)O₂-δ在22 GPa以上出现非晶化，表明其结构稳定性降低。体模量（bulk modulus）在异常行为开始后轻微下降，暗示晶格软化。拉曼光谱显示F₂g模式强度随阳离子无序度增加而抑制，压缩下RE-O模式强度增加表明部分重排。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了构型熵、阳离子尺寸和压力在决定稀土高熵氧化物结构稳定性和振动特性中的复杂相互作用。异常行为归因于局部晶格畸变和渐进键角弯曲，而非急剧相变。结果为理解极端条件下高熵氧化物的韧性机制和局部无序提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We report a comparative high-pressure study of two fluorite-type rare-earth oxides with increasing configurational entropy, (CePr)O$_{2-δ}$ and (CePrLa)O$_{2-δ}$. Synchrotron-based powder X-ray diffraction and Raman spectroscopy were carried out up to 30 GPa and 20 GPa, respectively. Both compounds retain the cubic fluorite structure throughout the pressure range explored, although an anomaly is observed between 9-16 GPa, characterized by a compressibility plateau and changes in vibrational modes. This behavior is attributed to local lattice distortions and a progressive bond angle bending rather than abrupt phase transitions. In (CePrLa)O$_{2-δ}$, the onset of amorphization is observed above 22 GPa, highlighting its reduced structural stability. The bulk modulus of both systems shows a slight decrease after the onset of the anomaly, suggesting subtle lattice softening. Raman spectroscopy reveals suppression of the F$_{2g}$ mode intensity with increasing cationic disorder, and under compression, partial reordering is evidenced by an increase in the RE-O mode intensity. Our results highlight the complex interplay between configurational entropy, cation size, and pressure in determining the structural stability and vibrational properties of rare-earth high-entropy oxides and provide insight into the mechanisms governing their resilience and local disorder under extreme conditions.

### [155] [Theory-Guided Discovery of Pressure-Induced Transitions in Fast-Ion Conductor BaSnF4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08376)
*Robin Turnbull,Zhang YingLong,Claudio Cazorla,Akun Liang,Rahman Saqib,Miriam Pena-Alvarez,Catalin Popescu,Laura Pampillo,Daniel Errandonea*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BaSnF4等快离子导体因其高离子电导率和化学稳定性对下一代固态电池技术具有重要意义，但其在极端条件下的行为仍不清楚。压力诱导改性对于调控功能性质具有相关性，需要深入研究。

Method: 研究结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算与高压实验，包括角度色散X射线衍射（angle-dispersive X-ray diffraction）、拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）和电阻率测量，均在室温下进行。

Result: DFT预测BaSnF4在10 GPa发生从四方相P4/nmm到单斜相P21/m-I的相变，在32 GPa进一步转变为更致密的单斜相P21/m-II。首次相变被实验证实，第二次相变由高压拉曼模式和电阻率行为的明显变化支持。

Conclusion: 这些发现不仅阐明了BaSnF4的高压相图，还揭示了氟锡酸盐基固态电解质中压力调控离子传输的潜力，为理解极端条件下快离子导体的行为提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Fast-ion conductors such as BaSnF4 are of significant interest for next-generation solid-state battery technologies due to their high ionic conductivity and chemical stability. However, the behaviour of these materials under extreme conditions remains poorly understood, despite the relevance of pressure-induced modifications for tuning functional properties. In this study, we combine density functional theory (DFT) calculations with high-pressure experiments to investigate the structural evolution of BaSnF4 up to 40 GPa. DFT predicts two pressure-induced phase transitions: from the ambient-pressure tetragonal P4/nmm phase to a monoclinic P21/m-I structure at 10 GPa, and subsequently to a denser monoclinic P21/m-II phase at 32 GPa. The first transition is experimentally confirmed via angle-dispersive X-ray diffraction, Raman spectroscopy, and electrical resistivity measurements, all performed at ambient temperature. The second transition is supported by distinct changes in high-pressure Raman modes and resistivity behaviour, consistent with a further structural reorganization. These findings not only clarify the high-pressure phase diagram of BaSnF4, but also shed light on the potential for pressure-tuned ionic transport in fluorostannate-based solid electrolytes.

Result: 证明了此类结合半密度的存在性和分类，并将该理论应用于理解Kontsevich量子化公式中的半经典因子。在线性泊松结构（linear Poisson structure）的特殊情况下，恢复了Duflo同构（Duflo isomorphism）及其Kashiwara-Vergne扩展中出现的因子作为规范结合增强。

Conclusion: 结论表明，通过研究辛群胚上的结合半密度，可以系统地理解量子化中的半经典因子，特别是在线性泊松结构情况下，能够恢复Duflo同构及其扩展中的规范因子。

Abstract: In this paper, we study half-densities enhancing the multiplication map on a symplectic groupoid and which satisfy a suitable associativity condition. We show the existence and classification of such associative half-densities, and further apply this theory to the understanding of semiclassical factors in Kontsevich's quantization formula. In the particular case of a linear Poisson structure, we recover the factors appearing in the Duflo isomorphism and its Kashiwara-Vergne extensions as a canonical associative enhancement.

### [158] [Kohn--Nirenberg quantization of the affine group and related examples](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08274)
*Pierre Bieliavsky,Victor Gayral,Sergey Neshveyev,Lars Tuset*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 该论文展示了如何为一类与仿射群相似的半直积构造酉对偶2-上循环，主要应用于李代数为Frobenius海藻结构的李群，基于Kohn-Nirenberg型量化过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于为一类与仿射群${\rm Aff}(V)=\GL(V)\ltimes V$具有相似性的半直积构造酉对偶2-上循环（unitary dual 2-cocycles）。这类结构的主要实例来源于李代数为Frobenius海藻（Frobenius seaweeds）的李群。

Method: 方法基于作者先前的研究成果，主要依赖表示理论（representation theory）和相关的Kohn-Nirenberg型量化过程。技术关键在于将半直积$G=H\ltimes V$表示为双交叉积$G=P\bowtie N$，使得$G$的唯一平方可积不可约表示具有特别简洁的形式。

Result: 成功构造了与标量傅里叶变换$\CF\colon L^2(N)\to L^2(P)$密切相关的Kohn-Nirenberg量化，该变换交织了$P$和$N$的左正则表示与由着装变换（dressing transformations）定义的表示。

Conclusion: 该研究为具有Frobenius海藻李代数的李群等一类半直积结构提供了酉对偶2-上循环的构造方法，通过双交叉积表示和Kohn-Nirenberg量化建立了表示理论框架。

Abstract: We show how to construct unitary dual $2$-cocycles for a class of semidirect products that exhibit many similarities with the affine group ${\rm Aff}(V)=\GL(V)\ltimes V$ of a finite dimensional vector space over a local skew field. The primary source of examples comes from Lie groups whose Lie algebras are Frobenius seaweeds. The construction builds on our earlier results and relies heavily on representation theory and an associated quantization procedure of Kohn--Nirenberg type.
  On the technical side, the key point is the observation that any semidirect product $G=H\ltimes V$ in our class can be presented as a double crossed product $G=P\bowtie N$ with respect to which the unique square-integrable irreducible representation of $G$ takes a particularly nice form. The Kohn--Nirenberg quantization that we construct is intimately related to a scalar Fourier transform $\CF\colon L^2(N)\to L^2(P)$ intertwining the left regular representations of $P$ and $N$ with representations defined by the dressing transformations.

### [159] [The Schwarz function and the shrinking of the Szegő curve: electrostatic, hydrodynamic, and random matrix models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07832)
*Gabriel Álvarez,Luis Martínez Alonso,Elena Medina*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究从三个不同视角（静电平衡问题、对偶流体动力学模型、随机矩阵模型）分析了经典Szegő曲线γ₀的变形γₜ，揭示了这些模型在Laguerre多项式零点渐近分布中的统一框架，并建立了与Lambert W函数和Schwarz反射对称性的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于从多个数学物理视角（静电平衡、流体动力学、随机矩阵）统一理解经典Szegő曲线的变形γₜ，这些变形出现在缩放变化Laguerre多项式L_n^{(α_n)}(nz)在临界区域α_n/n→-1时的零点渐近分布中。

Method: 研究方法采用三重视角分析：1) 静电平衡问题；2) 对偶流体动力学模型；3) 随机矩阵模型。通过分析缩放变化Laguerre多项式在临界区域的零点分布，建立变形参数t与序列α_n逼近负整数指数速率的关系，并利用Lambert W函数表达曲线的Schwarz函数。

Result: 研究结果表明：1) 变形曲线γₜ的Schwarz函数可用Lambert W函数显式表达；2) Stahl、Gonchar和Rachmanov的S-性质可明确表述为Schwarz反射对称性；3) 建立了曲线γₜ内部到圆盘D(0,e^{-t})的共形映射，并讨论了曲线的调和矩。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了经典Szegő曲线变形在多个数学物理模型中的统一框架，揭示了Lambert W函数在描述曲线Schwarz函数中的核心作用，并将S-性质重新解释为Schwarz反射对称性，为相关渐近分析提供了新的几何视角。

Abstract: We study the deformation of the classical Szegő curve $γ_0$ given by $γ_t = \{ z\in\mathbb{C}: |z\, e^{1-z}| = e^{-t}, |z|\leq 1\}$, $t\geq 0$ from three different viewpoints: an electrostatic equilibrium problem, the dual hydrodynamic model, and a random matrix model. The common framework underlying these models is the asymptotic distribution of zeros of the scaled varying Laguerre polynomials $L^{(α_n)}_n(n z)$ in the critical regime where $\lim_{n\to\infty}α_n/n=-1$, for which the limiting zero distribution is supported on $γ_t$, where the deformation parameter $t$ encodes the exponential rate at which the sequence $α_n$ approximates the set of negative integers. We show that the Schwarz functions of these curves can be written in terms of the Lambert $W$ function, and that in this formulation the $S$-property of Stahl and Gonchar and Rachmanov can be explictly written as the Schwarz reflection symmetry. We also discuss a conformal map of the interior of the curves $γ_t$ onto the disks $D(0,e^{-t})$ and the harmonic moments of the curves.

### [162] [Collective Dynamics of Vortex Clusters on a Flat Torus: From Pair Interactions to a Quadrupole Description](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07373)
*Aswathy KR,Rickmoy Samanta*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究了双周期无粘性流体域上涡旋相互作用的哈密顿表述，基于Schottky-Klein素函数及其q表示的精确相互作用。通过将两涡旋问题简化为单一复自由度，获得了轨道旋转频率和偶极子平移速度的显式表达式，并通过模拟验证。进一步推导了小团簇展开，揭示了动力学分解为平面相互作用、各向同性环面修正和几何诱导各向异性模式的普遍结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究双周期无粘性流体域上涡旋相互作用的哈密顿表述，旨在建立平环面（flat torus）和紧致流体域上涡旋团簇的简化描述。通过精确的相互作用表达，理解涡旋动力学在周期性几何中的基本特性。

Method: 基于Schottky-Klein素函数（Schottky-Klein prime function）及其q表示的精确相互作用，将两涡旋问题简化为单一复自由度。推导小团簇展开（small-cluster expansion），将动力学分解为平面相互作用、各向同性环面修正和几何诱导各向异性模式。通过直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulations）验证理论预测。

Result: 获得了轨道旋转频率（orbital rotation frequency）和偶极子平移速度（dipole translation velocity）的显式表达式，并通过模拟验证。揭示了集体动力学（collective dynamics）可通过单一复四极矩（complex quadrupole moment）进行封闭描述：其实部控制旋转速率的修正，虚部控制团簇的缓慢呼吸（slow breathing）。理论预测得到数值模拟的定量证实。

Conclusion: 建立了平环面和紧致流体域上涡旋团簇的简化描述框架。小团簇展开揭示了动力学分解的普遍结构，为理解周期性几何中涡旋相互作用提供了理论基础。数值验证确认了理论预测的准确性。

Abstract: We investigate a Hamiltonian formulation of vortex interactions on a doubly periodic inviscid fluid domain, based on an exact interaction expressed in terms of the Schottky-Klein prime function and its q-representation. The two-vortex problem is reduced to a single complex degree of freedom, from which explicit expressions for the orbital rotation frequency and dipole translation velocity are obtained and verified against simulations. Building on this framework, we derive a small-cluster expansion that reveals a universal decomposition of the dynamics into planar interactions, isotropic torus corrections, and geometry-induced anisotropic modes. At leading order, the collective dynamics admits a closed description in terms of a single complex quadrupole moment: its real part governs the corrections to the rotation rate, while its imaginary part controls the slow breathing of the cluster. These predictions are quantitatively confirmed by direct numerical simulations, establishing a reduced description of vortex clusters on the flat torus and compact fluid domains.

### [163] [Efficient fluid extraction through hydraulic fracture in capillary fiber bundle model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07485)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用一维毛细管纤维束模型（one-dimensional capillary fiber bundle model）进行模拟，通过降低每个毛细管的阈值来模拟压裂导致的孔隙空间增加。结合数值模拟与特定极限下的解析方法分析流变学特性。

Result: 研究发现流速随压力梯度增加而显著提高，总水力功率随压力梯度及压裂幅度（fracking amplitude）增加而增加。确定了存在最优压力梯度使压裂效果最大化，并建立了通过局部流动剖面最大波动与Darcy流起始的相关性，以及通过Shannon熵相对变化识别最优压力的方法。

Abstract: We have simulated a one dimensional capillary fiber bundle model with fracking events while acted between a pressure gradient across the system. The hydraulic fractures are incorporated through a decreasing nature of capillary thresholds for each tube that replicates an increment in pore spaces due to fracking. An increment in flow rate is evident through the evolved rheology we observe in our study. Analytical approaches for certain limits are adopted to understand the rheology which matches well with the numerical results. The overall hydraulic power increases with pressure gradient as well as with the percentage decrease in capillary threshold due to a single event, defines as the fracking amplitude. This combined with the early onset of linear Darcy flow increases the quality of the fluid extraction. We successfully point towards an optimum pressure gradient at which the fracking events are most effective - maximum change in fluid extracting with a maximum rate. We observed that it is possible to extract the information regarding the change from non-linear to Darcy flow due to fracking as well as the optimum pressure for fluid extraction through local flow profile, something which in much superior from the point of view of computational cost. The former is done by correlating the maximum fluctuation in local flow profile to the onset of Darcy flow. The later is done through the relative change in Shannon entropy with respect to the fracking amplitude that points towards the pressure associated with the maximum fluid extraction criterion.

Here we derive a continuum description for the coupled evolution of flow and porosity by coarse-graining pore-scale dynamics and validating the resulting model with pore-scale simulations. Abstract: We study Hamiltonian field theories on the multisymplectic bundle of a principal G-bundle with Hamiltonian densities invariant under a subgroup $H\subset G$. Using the covariant bracket formulation, we reduce the polysymplectic space and derive the corresponding reduced observables, brackets, and equations of motion, yielding a Lie--Poisson reduction by a subgroup for field theories. We also address the reconstruction problem, characterizing reconstruction in terms of the flatness of an associated connection. Several examples, including the heavy top, molecular strands with broken symmetry, and affine principal bundles, illustrate the general framework.

Method: 采用弱近接触结构$(f,ξ,η)$，其中$g(X,fY)=F(X,Y)$，并在自然条件下（在近接触情形下平凡）显式构造了$G=g+F$的爱因斯坦联络。进一步讨论了特殊爱因斯坦联络，并通过近厄米特流形与实线的加权乘积给出具体示例。

A.Einstein considered a linear connection $\nabla$ with torsion $T$ such that $(\nabla_X\,G)(Y,Z)=G(T(Y,X),Z)$. In this paper, we explicitly present the Einstein connection of $G=g+F$ using a weak almost contact structure $(f,ξ,η)$ with $g(X,fY)=F(X,Y)$ with a natural condition (trivial in the almost contact case). ### [167] [Score Shocks: The Burgers Equation Structure of Diffusion Generative Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07404)
*Krisanu Sarkar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过Burgers型演化定律分析扩散生成模型的得分场（score field），揭示了在方差爆炸（VE）扩散中得分场遵循粘性Burgers方程，为物种形成转变（speciation transitions）提供了PDE视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在从偏微分方程（PDE）角度理解扩散生成模型中的得分场演化，特别是物种形成转变现象。通过建立得分场与Burgers方程的联系，为分析模式间界面（inter-mode interfaces）的锐化过程提供理论框架。

Method: 采用Burgers型演化定律分析方差爆炸（VE）扩散的得分场，证明其在一维遵循粘性Burgers方程，在高维遵循无旋矢量Burgers系统。通过噪声密度的二元分解，将得分分离为平滑背景和由分量对数比决定的tanh界面项。

Result: 在对称二元高斯混合中，所得准则恢复了通过得分中点导数检测到的临界扩散时间，并与Biroli等人的谱准则一致。减去背景漂移后，模式间层呈现局部Burgers tanh剖面，在对称高斯情况下具有全局宽度σ_τ^2/a。研究还量化了得分误差在该层的指数放大。

Conclusion: 研究为扩散生成模型中的物种形成转变提供了系统的PDE理论框架，建立了得分场演化与Burgers方程的深刻联系。通过变量变换将方差保持（VP）SDE简化为VE情况，得到了闭式VP物种形成时间，并在高斯混合和四次双势阱模型上进行了数值验证。

Abstract: We analyze the score field of a diffusion generative model through a Burgers-type evolution law. For VE diffusion, the heat-evolved data density implies that the score obeys viscous Burgers in one dimension and the corresponding irrotational vector Burgers system in $\R^d$, giving a PDE view of \emph{speciation transitions} as the sharpening of inter-mode interfaces. For any binary decomposition of the noised density into two positive heat solutions, the score separates into a smooth background and a universal $\tanh$ interfacial term determined by the component log-ratio; near a regular binary mode boundary this yields a normal criterion for speciation. In symmetric binary Gaussian mixtures, the criterion recovers the critical diffusion time detected by the midpoint derivative of the score and agrees with the spectral criterion of Biroli, Bonnaire, de~Bortoli, and Mézard (2024). After subtracting the background drift, the inter-mode layer has a local Burgers $\tanh$ profile, which becomes global in the symmetric Gaussian case with width $σ_τ^2/a$. We also quantify exponential amplification of score errors across this layer, show that Burgers dynamics preserves irrotationality, and use a change of variables to reduce the VP-SDE to the VE case, yielding a closed-form VP speciation time. Gaussian-mixture formulas are verified to machine precision, and the local theorem is checked numerically on a quartic double-well.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We develop a model of musical rhythm and meter based on optimizing the trade-off between human psychological preferences for perceiving repeated patterns in time with a desire for variety and complexity. By mapping these competing preferences onto analogous quantities in statistical physics, we define an effective free energy which is minimized in the grand canonical ensemble. Using a mean field approximation, we observe phase transitions in the model from disordered events in time to orderings that closely reproduce those seen in music. We then compare the range of rhythmic characteristics predicted by the model to a dataset drawn from compositions by Johann Sebastian Bach, finding generally good quantitative agreement. The results provide a new lens through which to study musical rhythm, and a method for generatively producing rhythms.

*Haiqian Yang,Vishaal Krishnan,Sumit Sinha,L. Mahadevan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于时间反转对偶性的框架，用于计算从无序参考态到结构化目标系综的最小功随机过程，无需目标系综的轨迹知识，仅需样本即可。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 控制多体随机系统从无序参考态到结构化目标系综的演化是非平衡统计力学和随机控制中的自然问题。系统自然弛豫是从结构化目标向无序参考态发展，需要找到逆转这一弛豫的最小功随机过程。

Method: 通过建立时间反转对偶性：控制困难反向动力学的值函数满足等效的前向时间HJB方程，其解可直接从易模拟的前向弛豫轨迹中读取。利用Cole-Hopf变换及其相关的Feynman-Kac表示，前向势计算为路径空间自由能对这些前向轨迹的平均。

Result: 该框架提供了基于路径空间自由能、风险敏感控制和空间成本几何的随机输运物理解释。数值示例展示了学习到的值函数和诱导的受控扩散，说明空间成本场如何类似非均匀介质中的费马原理塑造输运几何。

Conclusion: 研究结果建立了随机最优控制、薛定谔桥理论和非平衡统计力学之间的统一联系，提供了一种仅需目标样本即可计算最优过程的方法，无需反向模拟或超出样本的目标知识。

Abstract: Controlling the evolution of a many-body stochastic system from a disordered reference state to a structured target ensemble, characterized empirically through samples, arises naturally in non-equilibrium statistical mechanics and stochastic control. The natural relaxation of such a system - driven by diffusion - runs from the structured target toward the disordered reference. The natural question is then: what is the minimum-work stochastic process that reverses this relaxation, given a pathwise cost functional combining spatial penalties and control effort? Computing this optimal process requires knowledge of trajectories that already sample the target ensemble - precisely the object one is trying to construct. We resolve this by establishing a time-reversal duality: the value function governing the hard backward dynamics satisfies an equivalent forward-in-time HJB equation, whose solution can be read off directly from the tractable forward relaxation trajectories. Via the Cole-Hopf transformation and its associated Feynman-Kac representation, this forward potential is computed as a path-space free energy averaged over these forward trajectories - the same relaxation paths that are easy to simulate - without any backward simulation or knowledge of the target beyond samples. The resulting framework provides a physically interpretable description of stochastic transport in terms of path-space free energy, risk-sensitive control, and spatial cost geometry. We illustrate the theory with numerical examples that visualize the learned value function and the induced controlled diffusions, demonstrating how spatial cost fields shape transport geometry analogously to Fermat's Principle in inhomogeneous media. Our results establish a unifying connection between stochastic optimal control, Schrödinger bridge theory, and non-equilibrium statistical mechanics.

</details>


### [170] [Harmonic morphisms and dynamical invariants in network renormalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08386)
*Francesco Maria Guadagnuolo,Marco Nurisso,Federica Galluzzi,Antoine Allard,Giovanni Petri*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究证明了离散调和态射（discrete harmonic morphisms）是网络粗粒化过程中保持随机游走动力学的必要条件，提出了调和度（harmonic degree）作为量化评估指标，并在实际网络中发现拉普拉斯重整化（Laplacian renormalization）能在特定尺度下自发产生精确的调和态射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂网络的重整化（renormalization）需要建立原则性标准来评估粗粒化过程是否保持动力学内容。当前缺乏系统方法来量化网络多尺度描述中随机游走（random walks）结构的保留程度。

Method: 证明了离散调和态射（discrete harmonic morphisms）——保持调和函数的满射——是精细网络上随机游走精确投影到粗粒化网络的最小条件。通过调和度（harmonic degree）这一诊断指标量化任意网络粗粒化近似调和态射的程度，并将该框架应用于几何、拉普拉斯和基于图神经网络（GNN-based）的重整化方法。

Result: 每种重整化方法产生独特的动力学指纹（dynamical fingerprint），编码其底层物理假设。最显著的是，拉普拉斯重整化（Laplacian renormalization）在多个网络中自发产生精确的调和态射，在特定尺度下实现首次退出随机游走（first-exit random-walk）转移结构的精确保留，这一性质是熵敏感性（entropic susceptibility）无法检测的。

Conclusion: 该研究为不规则网络拓扑结构识别了扩散保持共形映射（diffusion-preserving conformal maps）的离散类比，并为设计和评估多尺度网络描述提供了定量工具。调和度指标能够有效评估不同重整化方法在保持随机游走动力学方面的性能。

Abstract: Renormalization of complex networks requires principled criteria for assessing whether a coarse-graining preserves dynamical content. We prove that discrete harmonic morphisms -- surjective maps preserving harmonic functions -- provide the minimal condition under which random walks on a fine-grained network project exactly onto random walks on its coarse-grained image, through an appropriate random time change. We formalize this via the harmonic degree, a diagnostic quantifying how closely any network coarse-graining approximates a harmonic morphism. Applying this framework to geometric, Laplacian, and GNN-based renormalization across real-world networks, we find that each method produces a distinct dynamical fingerprint encoding its underlying physical assumptions. Most strikingly, Laplacian renormalization spontaneously yields exact harmonic morphisms in several networks, achieving exact preservation of first-exit random-walk transition structure at specific scales, a property that entropic susceptibility fails to detect. Our results identify a discrete analog of diffusion-preserving conformal maps for irregular network topologies and provide quantitative tools for designing and evaluating multi-scale network descriptions.

</details>


### [171] [Stochastic Thermodynamics for Autoregressive Generative Models: A Non-Markovian Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07867)
*Takahiro Sagawa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究建立了一个基于随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）的通用理论框架，用于分析自回归生成模型（autoregressive generative models）这类高度非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）过程，并引入了可高效估计的熵产生（entropy production）概念，为量化大语言模型（LLM）等现代生成模型的不可逆性提供了起点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归生成模型（包括Transformer、循环神经网络、卡尔曼滤波器等）通过基于过去确定性摘要采样每个输出来生成序列，产生真正非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）的观测过程。目前缺乏一个通用理论框架来分析这类高度非马尔可夫过程的不可逆性。

Method: 研究基于随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）为自回归生成模型类架构开发了一个通用理论框架，引入了熵产生（entropy production）概念，该量可以从采样轨迹中高效估计而无需指数级采样成本。作为概念验证，在预训练的Transformer模型GPT-2上评估了token级和句子级熵产生，并在线性高斯（linear Gaussian）案例中进行了演示。

Result: 熵产生可以精确分解为基于回顾性推断（retrospective inference）的非负每步贡献，每个贡献项进一步分解为信息论上有意义的项：压缩损失（compression loss）和模型失配（model mismatch）。在线性高斯情况下，模型简化为卡尔曼创新表示（Kalman innovation representation），熵产生具有解析表达式。

Conclusion: 该研究在随机热力学与现代生成模型之间建立了桥梁，为量化大语言模型等广泛高度非马尔可夫过程的不可逆性提供了起点。框架能够高效估计熵产生而无需指数采样成本，即使对于非马尔可夫观测动力学也是如此。

Abstract: Autoregressive generative models -- including Transformers, recurrent neural networks, classical Kalman filters, state space models, and Mamba -- all generate sequences by sampling each output from a deterministic summary of the past, producing genuinely non-Markovian observed processes. We develop a general theoretical framework based on stochastic thermodynamics for this class of architectures and introduce the entropy production, which can be efficiently estimated from sampled trajectories without exponential sampling cost despite the non-Markovian nature of the observed dynamics. As a proof-of-concept experiment for a large language model (LLM), we evaluate the token-level and sentence-level entropy production for a pre-trained Transformer-based model, GPT-2. We also demonstrate the framework in the linear Gaussian case, where the model reduces to the Kalman innovation representation and the entropy production admits an analytical expression. We further show that the entropy production decomposes exactly into non-negative per-step contributions in terms of retrospective inference, and each of those terms further splits into information-theoretically meaningful terms: a compression loss and a model mismatch. Our results establish a bridge between stochastic thermodynamics and modern generative models, and provide a starting point for quantifying irreversibility in a broad class of highly non-Markovian processes such as LLMs.

</details>


### [172] [Machine Learning the order-disorder Jahn-Teller transition in LaMnO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08058)
*Lorenzo Celiberti,Alexander Ehrentraut,Luca Leoni,Cesare Franchini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究使用基于机器学习力场的分子动力学模拟，揭示了LaMnO₃在约750K的Jahn-Teller结构相变机制，发现该相变由MnO₆八面体的Q₂ Jahn-Teller畸变有序化驱动，具有有序-无序（order-disorder）特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示LaMnO₃在T_JT ≈ 750 K的Jahn-Teller结构相变的微观机制，特别是区分有序-无序（order-disorder）与位移型（displacive）相变机制。

Method: 采用基于第一性原理（ab initio）数据训练的机器学习力场进行分子动力学模拟，并通过位点-位点关联函数（site-site correlation function）分析畸变，结合速度自相关函数（velocity autocorrelation function）分析振动性质。

Result: 研究发现相变由MnO₆八面体的Q₂ Jahn-Teller畸变有序化驱动，该畸变作为序参数（order parameter），证实了相变的有序-无序本质；在T_JT以上仍存在动态局域畸变，结果成功再现了结构和声子性质的实验温度依赖性，并揭示了有限温度下的非谐效应（anharmonic effects）。

Conclusion: 机器学习分子动力学与速度自相关函数分析的结合为揭示关联材料（correlated materials）结构相变的微观机制提供了稳健框架，能够清晰区分有序-无序相变与位移型（displacive）等替代机制。

Abstract: We investigate the Jahn-Teller structural phase transition in LaMnO$_3$ at $T_{JT} \simeq 750$ K using molecular dynamics simulations based on machine-learning force fields trained on ab initio data. Analysis of the site-site correlation function of the distortions reveals that the transition is driven by the ordering of the $Q_2$ Jahn-Teller distortion of the MnO$_6$ octahedra, which acts as the order parameter and establishes the order-disorder nature of the transition. Dynamical local distortions are found to persist above $T_{JT}$. Our results reproduce the experimental temperature dependence of both structural and phonon properties and highlight the presence of anharmonic effects at finite temperature. More broadly, the combined use of machine-learning molecular dynamics and velocity autocorrelation function analysis provides a robust framework for uncovering the microscopic mechanisms of structural phase transitions in correlated materials. In particular, this approach enables a clear distinction between order-disorder transitions and alternative mechanisms, such as displacive behavior, through the temperature evolution of vibrational properties.

</details>


### [173] [Controlling the rain fall statistics using Mean-Reverting Jump Diffusion model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08338)
*Joya GhoshDastider,D. Pal,Pankaj Kumar Mishra*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种随机均值回归跳跃扩散模型（stochastic mean-reverting jump-diffusion model），用于模拟降雨时间序列，并利用印度东北地区的长期半小时降雨数据进行验证。该模型能够捕捉降雨的间歇性和极端事件动态，重现超扩散行为（superdiffusive behavior）以及观测到的概率分布和多分形特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 降雨时间序列的模拟需要准确捕捉其复杂的统计特性，包括间歇性、极端事件动态以及多尺度特征。现有模型往往难以同时重现这些观测到的统计特征，特别是超扩散行为和多分形特性，因此需要开发更全面的建模框架。

Method: 采用随机均值回归跳跃扩散模型（stochastic mean-reverting jump-diffusion model）来模拟降雨时间序列。通过系统变化关键参数，研究模型行为的转变，并使用谱分析（spectral analysis）和小波分析（wavelet analysis）验证模拟序列与真实数据的匹配程度。

Result: 模型成功捕捉了降雨的间歇性和极端事件动态，重现了指数约为1.8的超扩散行为（superdiffusive behavior），并再现了观测到的概率分布和多分形特征（multifractal features）。通过参数调整，实现了对数正态分布（Log-Normal）和伽马分布（Gamma）之间的转变，并展示了如何控制极端事件的发生和干旱期持续时间。

Conclusion: 该随机建模框架为生成现实的合成降雨序列提供了稳健工具，同时作为理解控制降雨统计特性的底层随机过程影响的有效方法。模拟序列通过谱和小波分析进一步证实了其能够重现真实降雨数据中观察到的主要时间尺度。

Abstract: We present a stochastic mean-reverting jump-diffusion model to simulate rainfall time series and validate it using long-term half-hourly rain fall data from the North-East region of India. The model captures the intermittent and extreme-event dynamics of rainfall, reproducing superdiffusive behavior with an exponent $\sim 1.8$, along with the observed probability distributions and multifractal features. By systematically varying key parameters, we demonstrate a transition between Log-Normal and Gamma distributions, and show how the occurrence of extreme events and dry-patch durations can be controlled. Spectral and wavelet analyses further confirm that the simulated series reproduces the dominant temporal scales observed in real rainfall data. Our proposed framework provides a robust tool for generating realistic synthetic rainfall series and serves as an effective approach for understanding the influence of underlying stochastic processes that governs the rainfall statistics.

</details>

### [174] [The BOS-TMC Dataset: DFT Properties of 159k Experimentally Characterized Transition Metal Complexes Spanning Multiple Charge and Spin States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07623)
*Aaron G. Garrison,Jacob W. Toney,Tatiana Nikolaeva,Roland G. St. Michel,Christopher J. Stein,Heather J. Kulik*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了波士顿开壳层过渡金属配合物（BOS-TMC）数据集，包含从剑桥结构数据库（CSD）中提取的15.9万个实验表征的单核过渡金属配合物（TMCs）的密度泛函理论（DFT）性质，涵盖多种自旋态和形式电荷，总计34.38万个TMC/自旋组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有过渡金属数据集在电荷和自旋构型方面存在局限性，需要更全面、多样化的数据集来支持机器学习模型开发、DFT基准测试和探索性研究。BOS-TMC旨在提供更大规模、更多样化的过渡金属配合物性质数据。

Method: 通过迭代程序从剑桥结构数据库（CSD）中提取15.9万个实验表征的单核过渡金属配合物，并保持实验重原子坐标在优化过程中。使用PBE0/def2-TZVP方法计算单点能，并引入金属自旋依赖的原子化能计算方案。对于代表性子集（超过1万个配合物），评估了12种交换相关（xc）泛函对计算性质的影响。

Result: 生成了包含34.38万个TMC/自旋组合的数据集，报告了超过290万个TMC相关性质，包括电子能量、HOMO、LUMO、HOMO-LUMO间隙、原子部分电荷、偶极矩、原子化能和自旋分裂能。与先前数据集相比，BOS-TMC在电荷和自旋构型方面更加多样。

Conclusion: BOS-TMC数据集为机器学习模型开发、DFT基准测试和探索性研究提供了高保真度基础，其规模和多样性超越了现有过渡金属数据集，能够更好地支持相关领域的研究工作。

Abstract: We present the Boston Open-Shell Transition Metal Complex (BOS-TMC) dataset, a set of density functional theory (DFT) properties for 159k experimentally characterized mononuclear transition metal complexes (TMCs) in multiple spin states with a range of formal charges derived from the Cambridge Structural Database (CSD). To curate this set, we carried out an iterative procedure to confidently assign overall TMC charge. From this information, we then obtained properties in up to three spin states, i.e., low-, intermediate-, and high-spin for 3d metals and low- and intermediate-spin for 4d and 5d metals, depending on compatibility with the metal electron configuration, for a total of 343.8k TMC/spin combinations. At odds with prior sets, we preserved experimental heavy-atom coordinates in these structures during optimization. We report all properties using PBE0/def2-TZVP single-point energies on these structures. We introduce a scheme for computing metal-spin-dependent atomization energies, which we report for each TMC. Alongside electronic energies, we report up to seven additional properties including: HOMO, LUMO, HOMO-LUMO gap, atomic partial charges, dipole moments, atomization energies, and spin-splitting energies for a total of over 2.9M TMC-associated properties. For a representative subset of over 10k complexes chosen based on size, we evaluate the sensitivity of computed properties to exchange-correlation (xc) functional choice from a set of twelve xcs spanning rungs of "Jacob's ladder", highlighting hotspots of TMC space that have the greatest uncertainty. In comparison to prior transition-metal datasets, BOS-TMC is both larger and more diverse in terms of charge and spin configurations and, as a result, more diverse in its range of properties. This dataset is expected to provide a high-fidelity foundation for machine-learning model development, DFT benchmarking, and exploration.

</details>


### [175] [From Full Dynamic to Pure Static: A Family of $GW$-Based Approximations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08350)
*Pierre-François Loos,Johannes Tölle*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个从GW近似出发的一体格林函数方法体系，通过逐步减少自能（self-energy）的动力学内容，在完全动力学Dyson公式与纯静态有效单粒子哈密顿量之间建立了一系列近似方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于系统性地探讨动力学效应和粒子-空穴耦合（particle-hole coupling）在电离势描述中的作用，并开发能够简化计算复杂度的可靠方法。

Method: 方法基于GW近似，通过逐步减少自能的动力学内容构建了一个层次化的方法体系。采用降维策略（downfolding strategies）将空穴和粒子分支选择性解耦到简化的一粒子空间，并在分子电离能上进行基准测试。

Result: 结果表明，一致推导的部分静态方案能够产生可靠准粒子能量（quasiparticle energies），同时显著简化本征值问题。新引入的静态厄米自能（static Hermitian self-energy）作为该体系的静态极限，其结果与qsGW方法非常接近。

Conclusion: 该框架为研究动力学效应提供了受控途径，并提供了实现部分自洽性的替代静态路径。部分静态方案在保持精度的同时降低了计算复杂度，具有实用价值。

Abstract: We introduce a systematic hierarchy of one-body Green's function methods derived from the $GW$ approximation, constructed by progressively reducing the dynamical content of the self-energy. Starting from the fully dynamical Dyson formulation, we generate a family of approximations that interpolates between the standard $GW$ approximation to purely static effective single-particle Hamiltonians. This framework enables a controlled investigation of the role of dynamical effects and particle-hole coupling in the description of ionization potentials. Within this unified formalism, the hole and particle branches can be selectively decoupled through downfolding strategies into reduced one-particle spaces. By benchmarking the different members of this hierarchy on molecular ionization energies, we assess their accuracy, numerical robustness, and algorithmic complexity. We demonstrate that consistently derived partially static schemes can yield reliable quasiparticle energies while significantly simplifying the underlying eigenvalue problem. We further introduce a novel static Hermitian self-energy obtained as the static limit of this hierarchy. Despite its conceptually distinct origin, it produces results remarkably close to those of qs$GW$, thereby providing an alternative static route toward partial self-consistency.

</details>
